
-----title
宁波 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9d962ecb2fa84e23b9ecf1d2f3a25430_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9d962ecb2fa84e23b9ecf1d2f3a25430");'><span id='9d962ecb2fa84e23b9ecf1d2f3a25430_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1143')">1132-1143年</a>，1-12岁</div><div id='9d962ecb2fa84e23b9ecf1d2f3a25430' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　出生于明州鄞县桃源乡之方广院。以祖母命，为伯父张邵嗣子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居鄞县。生母孙氏或卒于是年，同年其父再娶李氏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　居鄞县。妹法善生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1136')">1135-1136年</a>　居鄞县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　居鄞县。从弟孝伯生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年2月</a>　居鄞县。以伯父张邵使金未归，有诏赐钱三百缗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年4月</a>　居鄞县。其父张祁被引对转官，主官告院，未久失官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　居鄞县。读胡铨上书，慕其高名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1142')">1139-1142年</a>　居鄞县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年6月</a>　居鄞县。其伯父张邵南归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年8月</a>　居鄞县。其伯父张邵入见高宗，除秘阁修撰，主管佑神观，改台州崇道观，回鄞县居住。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
芜湖
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='faf556e1a03549a4b959365fc165dba9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("faf556e1a03549a4b959365fc165dba9");'><span id='faf556e1a03549a4b959365fc165dba9_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1146')">1145-1146年</a>　居芜湖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　居芜湖。与李氏同居，生长子同之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　居芜湖。应乡试中举。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_111539'>远连天，茫茫都是，败芦枯蓼汀洲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111539'>认炊烟，几家蜗舍，映夕照，一簇渔舟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_545917'>传闻菰蒲中，相杀血新喋。<div id='poem_sentence_11_545917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_545917'>本是耕田农，饥寒实驱胁。<div id='poem_sentence_12_545917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_545917'>须公语县吏，早与支米帖。<div id='poem_sentence_13_545917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_545917'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_545917_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_545912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545912?labeling=true' target='_blank'>麒麟砚滴分韵得文字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545912")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545912_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545912'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545912'>素王西狩麟，笔削昌斯文。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545912'>茂陵一角兽，妙语闻终军。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545912'>壮哉笔砚间，英姿欲拿云。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545912'>名参龟龙瑞，威扫狐兔群。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545912'>岂独濡毫端，政尔清妖氛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545912'>会当献君王，玉殿春夜分。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545912'>输写胸中奇，恩波被无垠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545913'>忠义乃天赋，勋名要时早。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545913'>龙卧南阳客，鹰扬渭滨老。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545913'>当其尚栖迟，众或轻潦倒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545913'>风云会相遇，氛祲当独扫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='authorDate'>（1162年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545914_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545914'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545914'>吴甲组练明，吴钩莹青萍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545914'>战士三百万，猛将森列星。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545914'>挥戈却白日，饮渴枯沧溟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545914'>如何天骄子，敢来干大刑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545914'>呜呼三十年，中原饱膻腥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545914'>陛下极涵容，宗祊甚威灵。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545914'>犬羊尔何知，枭獍<span class='inlineComment2'>（原误作镜）</span>心未宁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545914'>囊血规射天，苍蝇混惊霆。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545914'>佛狸定送死，榆关不须扃。<div id='poem_sentence_10_545914'>便当收咸阳，政尔空朔庭。<div id='poem_sentence_10_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_545914'>明堂朝玉帛，剑佩鸣东丁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_545914'>八章车攻诗，十丈燕然铭。<div id='poem_sentence_12_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_545914'>我学益荒落，尚可写<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一本作纪）</span>汗青。<div id='poem_sentence_13_545914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　居芜湖。为芜湖吴波亭书额。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年1月10日</a>　居芜湖。凭吊芜湖玩鞭亭，有词纪之。作品：满江红（千古凄凉）<div id='poem_111667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_111667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111667'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111667'>千古凄凉，兴亡事、但悲陈迹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111667'>凝望眼、吴波不动，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_111667", 111667, onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_111667", 111667, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>云旆</span>连江赤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111667'>笑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_111667", 111667, "Clauses/6/Comments/1")'>老奸</span>、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_111667", 111667, "Clauses/6/Comments/2")'>遗臭</span>到如今，留空壁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111667_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_111667'>通轺传，销锋镝。<div id='poem_sentence_5_111667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_111667'>仰太平天子，坐收长策。<div id='poem_sentence_6_111667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_111667'>蹙踏扬州开帝里，渡江天马龙为匹。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　在芜湖。复集英殿修撰，除知静江府，领广南西路经略安抚使。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f78f21ccfe274999b06381d186122bab_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f78f21ccfe274999b06381d186122bab");'><span id='f78f21ccfe274999b06381d186122bab_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>，34岁</div><div id='f78f21ccfe274999b06381d186122bab' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年4月</a>　在芜湖。四月中旬，应太平州王秬（叔坚）之请，作《太平州学记》<div id='poem_1272032' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272032' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272032?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太平州学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272032")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272032_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272032'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272032'>学，古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272032_comment'></div>庙于学以祀孔子，后世之制也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272032_comment'></div>阁于学以藏天子之书，古今之通义，臣子之恭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272032_comment'></div>当涂于江、淮为名郡，有学也，无诵说之所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272032_comment'></div>有庙也，无荐享之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272032_comment'></div>有天子之书，坎而置之屋壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272032_comment'></div>甲申秋，直秘阁王侯秬来领太守事，于是方有水灾，尽坏堤防，民不粒食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272032_comment'></div>及冬，则有边事，当涂兵之冲，上下震摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272032_comment'></div>侯下车，救灾之政，备敌之略，皆有次叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272032_comment'></div>饥者饱，坏者筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272032_comment'></div>赤白囊昼夜至，侯一以静填之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272032_comment'></div>明年春，和议成，改元乾道，将释奠于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272032_comment'></div>侯语教授沈瀛曰：「学如是！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272032_comment'></div>今吾州内外之事略定，孰先于此者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272032_comment'></div>命其掾蒋晖、吕滨中撤而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272032_comment'></div>先是，郡将欲楼居，材既具，侯命取以为阁，辟其门而重之，凡学之所宜有，无一不备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272032_comment'></div>客有过而叹曰：「贤之不可已也如是夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272032_comment'></div>今之当涂，昔之当涂也，来为守者，孰不知学之宜葺，而独忘之者，岂真忘之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272032_comment'></div>力不赡耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272032_comment'></div>始王侯之来，民尝以水为忧，已又以兵为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272032_comment'></div>王侯易民之忧，纳之安乐之地，以其馀力大新兹学，役不及民，颐指而办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272032_comment'></div>贤之不可已也如是夫」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272032_comment'></div>客于是又有叹也：「尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武之天下，传之至今，天地之位，日月之明，江河之流，万世无敝者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272032_comment'></div>时治时乱，时强时弱，岂有他哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272032_comment'></div>人而已耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272032_comment'></div>财用之不给，甲兵之不强，人才之不多，宁真不可为耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272032_comment'></div>《诗》曰：『无竞维人』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272032_comment'></div>谓予不信，请视新学」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272032_comment'></div>夏四月既望，历阳张某记。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1272032'></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1272032_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9ab08af77e5a49c0bd58575f7dcf6f29_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9ab08af77e5a49c0bd58575f7dcf6f29");'><span id='9ab08af77e5a49c0bd58575f7dcf6f29_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>，35岁</div><div id='9ab08af77e5a49c0bd58575f7dcf6f29' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年9月</a>　九月中下旬至芜湖。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='84a31faa56c8466fa7627e8bbeeb9749_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("84a31faa56c8466fa7627e8bbeeb9749");'><span id='84a31faa56c8466fa7627e8bbeeb9749_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>，36岁</div><div id='84a31faa56c8466fa7627e8bbeeb9749' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在芜湖。除秘阁修撰，改知潭州，权荆湖南路提点刑狱公事。作品：辞免知潭州奏状。潭州谢复对表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（关于活动内容，宛敏灏《张孝祥年谱》（《词学》第二、三辑）将张孝祥起知潭州、权荆湖南路提点刑狱公事系于本年五月。）</span><div id='poem_1271840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免知潭州奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271840")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271840'>臣疏远微贱，遭遇陛下，叨荷眷隆，屡垂奖使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271840_comment'></div>昨者广西，罪戾盈积，劾章既上，谓当投窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271840_comment'></div>圣慈宽宥，止从罢免，至于贴职，复与全存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271840_comment'></div>天地父母，恩德莫喻，虽极糜捐，报称何有！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271840_comment'></div>自反私室，阖门讼愆，屏息避影，早夜怵惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271840_comment'></div>敢图简记，又俾藩郡，视旧所领，是为邻壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271840_comment'></div>委寄之重，与昔不殊，闻命之始，恐惧感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271840_comment'></div>臣实何人，叠此忝冒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271840_comment'></div>已别具奏，乞赐恩免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271840_comment'></div>蝼蚁之躯，有不尽者，辄具劄子，昧死上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271840_comment'></div>伏念臣父母年七十，气血素弱，近复多病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271840_comment'></div>顷赴广西，不曾迎侍，道里悠远，日以忧戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271840_comment'></div>臣弟年幼，侍旁无人，自臣来归，方获宁养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271840_comment'></div>今兹新任，复隔重湖，重白之亲，又难远涉，进退皇惑，莫知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271840_comment'></div>仰惟陛下推广孝道，本于人情，匹夫之微，皆得自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271840_comment'></div>臣之迫切，义当控告，抵冒大谴，矢心以辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271840_comment'></div>伏望陛下至仁哀矜，俯徇愚恳，于江、淮间易一小郡，父获就养，不违定省，臣得竭力以趋职事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271840_comment'></div>祈天请命，语无伦次，瞻望阙庭，伏增震作。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1271840_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1271808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>潭州谢复次对表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271808")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271808'>赐以赞书，还之次对，敢云旧服，是谓新恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271808_comment'></div>伏念臣智昧一官，仕尝三已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271808_comment'></div>江湖远引，自怜蹇剥之多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271808_comment'></div>雨露均沾，独倚乾坤之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271808_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下缉熙圣绪，骏发英猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271808_comment'></div>专予夺之柄，以驭群工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271808_comment'></div>明功过之使，以兴庶事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271808_comment'></div>乃如孤迹，亦预庆条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271808_comment'></div>臣敢不祗佩隆私，益追往咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271808_comment'></div>傥有及民之效，则为报上之忠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1271808_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0dc9508e53bc40b08049e36538632ce3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0dc9508e53bc40b08049e36538632ce3");'><span id='0dc9508e53bc40b08049e36538632ce3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>，36岁</div><div id='0dc9508e53bc40b08049e36538632ce3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　初夏归芜湖，有词。作品：醉蓬莱（问人间荣事）<div id='poem_111702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_111702'>海内高名，似今谁比。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111702'>脱屣归来，眇浮云富贵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111702'>致远钩深，乐天知命，且从容阅世。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111702'>火候周天，金文满义，从来活计。<div id='poem_sentence_4_111702_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_111702'>有酒一尊，有棋一局，少日亲朋，旧家邻里。<div id='poem_sentence_7_111702'>解愠薰风，做凉梅雨，又一般天气。<div id='poem_sentence_7_111702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_111702'>曲几蒲团，纶巾羽扇，年年如是。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_111702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年6月</a>　六月，以当暑送虞允文于芜湖舟中，中暑卒。<br /></div>

id='poem_1271809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271809?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代方务德庐州到任谢表</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271809'>外阃分忧，肆攽明命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271809_comment'></div>内朝赐对，载迩清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271809_comment'></div>已见荒郡创残之馀，具言圣主哀矜之意<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271809_comment'></div>伏念臣娄膺剧寄，蔑著微劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271809_comment'></div>谓孤踪宜在于弃捐，而庙论猥烦于推择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271809_comment'></div>属有负薪之疾，既辞挽粟之行，逮兹边琐之多虞，复俾帅藩而申命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271809_comment'></div>驰驱引道，偻佝拜恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271809_comment'></div>细札十行，亟承于汉诏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271809_comment'></div>土阶三尺，密奉于尧言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271809_comment'></div>轸民之穷，则使捐关市之征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271809_comment'></div>悯臣之病，则戒求药物之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271809_comment'></div>掩骼下度僧之牒，振饥分贡牧之金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271809_comment'></div>独揆谫能，曷胜隆委？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271809_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下至仁恻隐，盛德涵容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271809_comment'></div>革辂徂征，已克清于大憝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271809_comment'></div>玉关罢警，将永洽于泰和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271809_comment'></div>慨斯锋镝之淫夷，惧以茧丝而割刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271809_comment'></div>故铨冗吏，使布宽条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271809_comment'></div>臣敢不祗若神谟，恪恭贱职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271809_comment'></div>老于州县，敢图横草之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271809_comment'></div>固我封陲，庶弭搔爪之怨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1271809_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年2月</a>　在建康。除知抚州（实际到抚州的时间，在三月以后）<br /></div><div class='label1' id='78864bf21d0745809f20793ba35cf3a6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("78864bf21d0745809f20793ba35cf3a6");'><span id='78864bf21d0745809f20793ba35cf3a6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>，33岁</div><div id='78864bf21d0745809f20793ba35cf3a6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年3月</a>　以都督府参赞军事兼知建康，领行宫留守。作品：辞免参赞军事兼知建康府奏状。赴建康画一利害。<div id='poem_1271837' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271837' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271837?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免参赞军事兼知建康府奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271837")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271837_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271837'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271837'>臣起于诸生，叨窃名宦，军旅之事，实不谙晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271837_comment'></div>顾方外敌凌侮，主忧臣辱，臣于兹时蒙被使令，义无辞难，死生惟命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271837_comment'></div>但今日之事，势异畴昔，虏情叵测，邦计犹虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271837_comment'></div>至如守备之脆坚，列将之能否，强弱之辨，进退之宜，难以隃度而周知，必须亲履而详访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271837_comment'></div>若乃以虚为实，以是为非，苟且目前，咎将谁执？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271837_comment'></div>岂一身夷灭之足惜，而误国欺君之是虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271837_comment'></div>臣实何人，而当此选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271837_comment'></div>又况帅藩之重，宫钥之严，虽曰摄承，亦难冒据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271837_comment'></div>伏望圣慈收还误宠，更图奇杰，仰备驱驰，特赐除臣在外宫观。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1271837_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1271832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴建康画一利害</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271832")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271832'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271832'>一、臣今来起发，欲先往镇江府措置事宜讫，即至建康交割职事，就令本府以次官时暂权管，却往两淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271832_comment'></div>将来若有边事，亦许臣往来措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271832_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1271832'>一、臣如体访得武臣内有智略忠义习知边事，或能干办繁难之人，欲乞从臣不拘见任、寄居、待阙官，指名踏逐，分付诸军量才使唤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271832_comment'></div>如都督府有合差委干当事务，亦许依此施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271832_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1271832'>一、两淮措置事务，全在州县官吏协心爱惜，不扰而办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271832_comment'></div>如有违戾去处，许臣按劾闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271832_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1271832'>一、臣应有奏报文字，并乞径赴御前投放开拆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1271832_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年4月</a>　罢都督府参赞军事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　官知建康，领行宫留守。江东路沿江州军水灾，上札子恳请朝廷力治荒政，救饥防闲。作品：论萧琦第宅及水灾赈济札子。<div id='poem_1271833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论萧琦第宅及水灾赈济劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（知建康府日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271833")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271833'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271833'>臣六月二十二日准御宝封送下御笔付臣及萧琦第宅图本，臣已望阙百拜祗领讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271833_comment'></div>伏念臣孤远贱臣，遭遇陛下，入从出藩，眷简优隆，糜捐万死，难以报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271833_comment'></div>今又锡以宸翰，宠嘉踰等，云章奎画，永藏私家，臣阖门老稚，不胜感恩恋圣、欢喜踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271833_comment'></div>萧琦之居，即日并工营缮，谨遵睿训，更加高大，及多与空地，令可驰射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271833_comment'></div>琦在此侨寓，臣五七日之间一往见之，饮食医药钱酒之属，常常照顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271833_comment'></div>所有按月请俸，合系总领司支，已行关报讫，缘未有支行真俸指挥，有司不敢擅行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271833_comment'></div>琦远客累重，欲望圣慈特赐处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271833_comment'></div>所有供给钱，建康府已应副讫，仰乞睿照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271833_comment'></div>江东路沿江州军，水灾甚广，臣节次曾具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271833_comment'></div>夏税亦自无可输纳，秋苗决然无望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271833_comment'></div>如淮西庐、和之间，人民亦多被害，窃虑秋冬之交，饥民聚为盗贼，臣虽已差官前去太平州、广德、宣、池州措置，更乞圣慈宣谕宰执，预治荒政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271833_comment'></div>淮上百姓方罢筑城掘壕、般塼踏弩之役，四月以来，急去插秧，冀望收成一饱，忽被水害，人情皇皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271833_comment'></div>仰惟陛下焦劳万机，德动天鉴，灾异之来，决非人力，如尧、汤之时，定有冥数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271833_comment'></div>但于赈济防闲，抚摩惠养，不得不尽，伏望曲轸渊衷，中外幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271833_comment'></div>江上诸州，将兵阙额甚多，臣已令所差官将被水阙食强壮人说喻招刺，支与例物，亦消弭盗贼之一端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271833_comment'></div>谨具劄子奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271833_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1271833_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　官知建康，领行宫留守。致信汤丞相（思退），提出兴修水利，修复圩区，以役代赈。作品：汤丞相。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《汤丞相》（尺牍），名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷三十九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年8月15日</a>　官知建康，领行宫留守。中秋，与诸客集游赏心亭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　官知建康，领行宫留守。有诗达苏著（廷藻）作品：即事简苏廷藻。<div id='poem_114748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_114748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_114748")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_114748_comment'></div><div id='poem_title_1272070_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272070'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272070'>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272070_comment'></div>自癸未至于戊子，吾妇之死于是六日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272070_comment'></div>越己丑，将殡于宝林之佛寺，以俟卜吉而藏焉。<div class='inline' -----title
和县（和州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='27f5cb695ba64419a910dfa4b7956b64_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("27f5cb695ba64419a910dfa4b7956b64");'><span id='27f5cb695ba64419a910dfa4b7956b64_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>，19岁</div><div id='27f5cb695ba64419a910dfa4b7956b64' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　八、九月间，随父回和州省故里，得灵芝一株，因以之为郑侨年上寿，有诗。作品：寿芝颂代总得居士上郑漕。<div id='poem_1272046' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272046' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272046?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寿芝颂代揔得居士上郑漕<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　时年十九作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272046")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272046_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272046'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272046'>上既专任一德，方内底定，眷江之北，昔为战墟，生聚教训，十年于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272046_comment'></div>曰：「畴予宝臣持节，以岂弟德惠为予抚绥之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272046_comment'></div>百辟卿士再拜言：「漕江东臣某，再考绩为天下最，宜可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272046_comment'></div>上曰：「俞哉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272046_comment'></div>于是有诏华原增秩，总部淮南十有六州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272046_comment'></div>诏下之日，淮民欢呼，奔走相告，自州达之县，自县达之田里，自田里达之穷岩幽谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272046_comment'></div>公江东之治，仁声义气，渐被于两淮，故淮民闻公之来，其喜如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272046_comment'></div>越翌日，历阳郡东鄙樵民有得异草于松根者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272046_comment'></div>郡人张某，寔公门下士，属公诞辰甫及，当有颂诗形容盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272046_comment'></div>乃以九月吉旦，洁齐执笔，为文未有绪，俯而假寐，若有告者曰：「姑置之，天将以芝畀女为公寿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272046_comment'></div>某惊悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272046_comment'></div>已而樵民奉芝款门曰：「畴昔获此，弗之识，而神梦谓余：是盖所谓芝者，天以华原公将持节吾土，是生灵物而为瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272046_comment'></div>且此月之十日，则公生之日，是芝则又昭示公难老之徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272046_comment'></div>若里人有张氏者，寔公客，亟归之，俾得献公，不者祸女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272046_comment'></div>神言如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272046_comment'></div>我惧，是以来」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272046_comment'></div>某亦解昨者假寐若告之言，盛服再拜而受之，信芝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272046_comment'></div>一本二干，高广有咫，坚密温润，色如紫玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272046_comment'></div>轮囷蓊郁，骈为七枝，华叶敷芳，则十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272046_comment'></div>蔼然若卿云捧日，灿然若奇葩艳春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272046_comment'></div>噫戏异哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272046_comment'></div>未曾有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272046_comment'></div>神之命公，可谓深切著明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272046_comment'></div>不知天之于人，相去远近，而其物类之感召，如是其敏且速耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272046_comment'></div>且以公将持节西州而为呈瑞，则胡不降甘露、流醴泉、异亩同颖、凤皇翔集耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272046_comment'></div>不以是数者为应而应以芝，天意若曰：芝上瑞也，不春而华，不秋而实，不根而植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272046_comment'></div>剪而置之，虽历数千百年而犹敷腴充实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272046_comment'></div>则芝非特上瑞，又寿草也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272046_comment'></div>天与公瑞，则于除命之后，瑞草发于淮西之境；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272046_comment'></div>天与公寿，则生朝之前，寿草产于古松之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272046_comment'></div>物像昭显，决非偶然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272046_comment'></div>乡惟甘露、醴泉、嘉禾、翔凤之来，谓之祥瑞则可矣，乌在其为寿徵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272046_comment'></div>于以见天之锡公富贵寿考，广大繁昌，有永无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272046_comment'></div>岂两淮之民独受其福，将天下生灵寔受其福；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272046_comment'></div>岂公独有其瑞，将朝廷国家寔有其瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1272046_comment'></div>然则此芝之来，所系大矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1272046_comment'></div>谨拜手稽首而为之颂曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1272046'>濯濯灵芝，施于古松，天锡珍祥，以寿郑公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1272046_comment'></div>文武郑公，其德孔硕，文正之子，柔嘉维则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1272046_comment'></div>天子命公，汝予宝臣，宣力四方，其牖我民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1272046_comment'></div>公拜稽首，奉天子命，自西徂东，惟一其政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1272046_comment'></div>孰寒而饥，公衣食之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1272046_comment'></div>孰疠而疵，公药治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1272046_comment'></div>孰犷不率，则训则治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1272046_comment'></div>孰奸贼民，则耨则夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1272046_comment'></div>条疏节披，罔亦不宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1272046_comment'></div>天子命公，汝有成绩，盍其归矣，箴补衮职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1272046_comment'></div>淮堧奕奕，其疆千里，奠国北门，孰与予理？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1272046_comment'></div>在列咸咨，曰公克任，天子命公，辍女往镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1272046_comment'></div>公来之初，灵芝则生，亦以寿公，宠锡百朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1272046_comment'></div>蔚彼芝矣，厥生孔时，爰发其祥，以公来绥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1272046_comment'></div>蔚彼芝矣，公介眉寿，数百千祀，与国长久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1272046_comment'></div>神则有言，芝以瑞公，入侍帝旁，九旒升龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1272046_comment'></div>神则有言，芝以寿公，楚南春秋，绿发方瞳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1272046_comment'></div>我作颂诗，式诏罔极，诞保休徵，有永无斁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1272046_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='1abdb326f38a45fba61371ed3e747687_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1abdb326f38a45fba61371ed3e747687");'><span id='1abdb326f38a45fba61371ed3e747687_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，30岁</div><div id='1abdb326f38a45fba61371ed3e747687' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年8月</a>　自宣城回和州省视祖茔，致书刘锜，乞罢两淮民社。作品：又刘两府（某以久不省祖茔）<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《又刘两府》，名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷三十九。）</span><div id='poem_1271964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又上刘两府</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271964")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271964'>某窃瞻国之盛衰，必观诸人望之用舍，谢太傅消摇东山，雅意丘壑，当时议者顾谓「安石不起，如苍生何」，言若大而夸，然卒之成肥水之功者安石也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271964_comment'></div>裴中立以谗居外，两河诸侯浸淫问鼎，中立复相，忠者怀而强者畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271964_comment'></div>人望之用果如何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271964_comment'></div>自五月来，朔方传闻汹汹，岂惟自江以北，百姓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1271964", 1271964, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>束担</span>以待，而江、浙之间，亦复骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271964_comment'></div>忽有邮书报相公开帅府以号令诸将，制册扬廷，恩礼赫奕，凡士大夫与夫闾巷之民、田夫牧人，莫不欢喜奔走，更相告语，以谓相公既用，则吾事必济，无得忧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271964_comment'></div>至于赤籍伍符，则又踊跃抃厉，以有赴敌致命，义无却顾之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271964_comment'></div>黠虏震慑，先声所暨，奉头鼠窜，遗魂落胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271964_comment'></div>乌乎休哉，古未有也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271964_comment'></div>恭惟某官不世之功成在旦夕，便当肃清宫禁，祗谒寝园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271964_comment'></div>某无似，庶将载笔后车，草露布以俟献也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271964_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1271964'>某以久不省祖茔，自宣城暂归历阳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1271964", 1271964, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>村落</span>，一二日复西上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271964_comment'></div>民间恃相公近在维扬，皆得自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271964_comment'></div>惟是民兵一事，朝廷忧惧，近日复有约束，分隶诸军，田野之人，愈更皇恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271964_comment'></div>孔子曰：「以不教民战，是谓弃之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271964_comment'></div>《周官》井田之法，春蒐、夏苗、秋狝、冬狩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271964_comment'></div>其坐作进退，固已阅习，而犹曰不教者，盖谓未尝教之以知礼、知义、知信、知勇，如子犯之所云也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271964_comment'></div>今之民虽坐作进退冥然不知，乃欲驱之以当大敌，民之死不敢自爱，万一沮吾军势，悔将何及？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271964_comment'></div>仰惟某官同国休戚，知无不言，况此淮民，又属戏下，敢告相公，具以利害达之冕旒，将两淮民社一切罢免，岂惟十万生灵皆出全护，脱性命于锋镝，而缓急之际，不误国事，尤其大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271964_comment'></div>伏惟相公垂情，无以某小子而废斯言，熟计而亟图之，无任激切恐惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1271964_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='88d31876564549319575d3e714829269_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("88d31876564549319575d3e714829269");'><span id='88d31876564549319575d3e714829269_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>，35岁</div><div id='88d31876564549319575d3e714829269' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年10月1日</a>　省和州故里，十月旦作文，记胡昉（明秀）在和州开凿千秋、姥下、石跋三河之事。作品：三河记。<div id='poem_1272039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三河记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年10月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272039")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272039'>直秘阁胡昉治历阳之明年，令行禁止，道不拾遗，于是始以民之馀力开三河，曰千秋，曰姥下，曰石跋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272039_comment'></div>因民之利，不劝以从，雷动风偃，天造地设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272039_comment'></div>知閤门事龙大渊将上旨视其成，都统制刘源、江东运使韩元吉，淮西运使梁竑皆会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272039_comment'></div>夫兴事造业之难，圣智惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272039_comment'></div>是举也，惟天子之信臣临之，而诸贤参同异之论，称其平以复于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272039_comment'></div>将不独吾千里蒙其利，为保鄣，为茧丝，昉其任是责哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272039_comment'></div>乾道丙戌十月旦，张某书于三瑞堂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1272039_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年10月</a>　省和州故里，于州守胡昉（明秀）席上有词。作品：菩萨蛮（乳羝属国归来早）<div id='poem_111654' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111654' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111654?labeling=true' target='_blank'>菩萨蛮<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十四 </span>和州守胡明秀席上</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111654")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111654_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111654'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111654'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_111654", 111654, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>乳羝</span>属国归来早。知君胆大身犹小。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111654'>一节不须论。功名看致君。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111654_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111654'>镇西楼上酒。父老为公寿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111654'>更祝太夫人。年年封诏新。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111654'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_111654_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
当涂

class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111555'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111555'>问讯湖边春色，重来又是三年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111555'>东风吹我过湖船，杨柳丝丝拂面。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111555_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111555'>世路如今已惯，此心到处悠然。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111555'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_111555", 111555, /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>居当涂。与王质（景文）有诗唱和。作品：和王景文三首。<div id='poem_546059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和王景文<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546059")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546059'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546059'>陆行忌豺虎，水去怯风波。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546059'>世路险犹尔，客中愁更多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546059'>吾生真漫与，天道合如何。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546059'>千古兴亡意，临风一放歌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546059'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546059_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546060?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546060'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546060'>斯文到之子，砥柱阅颓波。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546060'>致主规模别，伤时疾疢多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546060'>大臣谗贾谊，逆旅欠常何。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546060'>无路排阊阖，聊当扣角歌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546060'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546060_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546061?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546061'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546061'>王师行六月，淮海静无波。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546061'>元老前筹密，诸军捷奏多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546061'>西风向萧瑟，北顾要谁何。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546061'>闻说收兵后，讴吟杂雅歌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546061'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546061_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
杭州

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年12月</a>　至临安备礼部试，与从弟孝伯晤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在临安应礼部试。为桧党所抑，秦埙名列第一，孝祥名列第二。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年3月</a>　在临安应廷试，高宗亲擢孝祥为第一，抑秦埙为第三。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在临安。拒曹泳请婚于殿廷，泳深憾之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在临安期集所，上书为岳飞辨诬并请表其忠义。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在临安。始与刘珙交，并师事之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　在临安期集所，初交虞允文。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c939acd0aa1d46659308494dee48ce89_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c939acd0aa1d46659308494dee48ce89");'><span id='c939acd0aa1d46659308494dee48ce89_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1156')">1155-1156年</a>，24-25岁</div><div id='c939acd0aa1d46659308494dee48ce89' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　十一月底或十二月初，赴朝面对，上札子劝帝总揽权纲以尽更化之美。作品：论总揽权纲以尽更化札子。<div id='poem_1271812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论总揽权纲以尽更化劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（秘书正字召对日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271812")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271812'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271812'>臣恭惟陛下天纵神圣，身济兴运，兢兢行道，馀三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271812_comment'></div>以陛下之心，行陛下之政，唐、虞、三代，宜不足进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271812_comment'></div>而怀忠之士，以今揆古，容欲有议者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271812_comment'></div>群臣负陛下使令也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271812_comment'></div>自建炎以来，朝廷之治，盖尝一再更张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271812_comment'></div>方陛下厉精于中兴之初，则执事者立异相高，隆虚名而略实用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271812_comment'></div>逮陛下恭己于修好之后，则专国者怙权植党，废公议以窃主威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271812_comment'></div>夫君，天也，父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271812_comment'></div>事天事父若此，尚何暇望其它哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271812_comment'></div>今陛下收还威柄，人才用舍，蔽自圣志，先时二者之敝，固已革去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271812_comment'></div>然臣之愚，犹欲冒昧自竭者，诚愿陛下清閒之燕，密谕迩臣，使之无苟目前，益务远略而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271812_comment'></div>夫事有可为，当各进所闻，岂必拘形迹之疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271812_comment'></div>政或偏敝，当勿惮改作，不宜习见闻之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271812_comment'></div>玩岁月，则将失投机之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271812_comment'></div>饰文具，则必盭责实之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271812_comment'></div>使群臣精白以承休德，则陛下高拱而昭成功，永辑隆平，无有纪极，惟陛下留神财幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271812_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1271812_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年12月</a>　除秘书省正字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　友人郭从范为丞相赵公之没作《广招》，张孝祥作《广招后序》<div id='poem_1271998' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271998?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广招后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271998")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271998'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271998'>《广招》，吾友郭从范为丞相赵公作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271998_comment'></div>丞相没南荒，不及见绍兴乙亥冬之事，天下哀之，故从范作此文以尉九原之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271998_comment'></div>张子曰：「丞相以忠受知天子，同列媢疾，群纤嗾吠，丞相以迁死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271998_comment'></div>丞相之死不死也，今大憝幽戮，圣政日起，丞相志愿毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271998_comment'></div>挟奸欺君，虽生犹死，谓丞相之魂可无招也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271998_comment'></div>从范年未三十，长不满五尺，胸次浩然，常欲轩轾天下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271998_comment'></div>闻不平事，攘臂齧齿，椎床唾壁，终日咄咄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271998_comment'></div>使从范幸而见用，必不淟涊帖然随流波也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271998_comment'></div>又区区为赵公作此文，从范之心可知也已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271998_comment'></div>可知也已！</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1271998_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年6月</a>　在京任秘书省正字。面对，上札子三篇。作品：乞改正迁谪士大夫罪名札子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（关于活动内容，宛敏灏《张孝祥年谱》（《词学》第二、三辑）将张孝祥上《乞改正迁谪士大夫罪名》札子事系于绍兴二十五年（1155））</span>乞修日历札子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（关于系年作品，宛敏灏《张孝祥年谱》（《词学》第二、三辑）将张孝祥上《乞修日历札子》建议取已修日历详审是正事系于绍兴二十入年（1158））</span>论涵养人才札子。<div id='poem_1271813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞改正迁谪士大夫罪名劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（秘书正字召对日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271813")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271813'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271813'>臣仰惟陛下天造神断，与海内更始，士大夫流窜降黜，一皆抆拭，待之如初，甚盛德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271813_comment'></div>臣窃见前者大臣窃陛下之威福，济私心之喜怒，逮其莫景，很恣尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271813_comment'></div>士大夫稍自振厉，不肯阿附，或小有违忤，则罗致之狱，毛举缕析，旁逮知旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271813_comment'></div>惧其不能废锢，必以赃私罪污之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271813_comment'></div>有司观望风旨，锻鍊烦酷，使之诬伏，爰书讯鞠，贯穿首尾，强立左验，务令案节备具，牢不可破。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271813_comment'></div>今虽累降诏旨，许以辩雪，然有见贤能之士，或曾蒙陛下奖拔，则忌之益深，乃使虚被诬蔑，自新无路，人才终弃，实可悯惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271813_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈断自宸衷，特降睿旨下刑部：诸命官自去年郊祀赦前犯赃私罪，除州县监临之官，因民户论诉，监司按发，若有冤抑，依条审实外，如系近年取怒故相，并缘文致，有司观望，锻鍊成罪之人，特免看详，并与改正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271813_comment'></div>庶几士大夫实沾恩宥，复全名节，得备国家选用，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271813_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1271813_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1271819' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271819' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271819?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞脩日历劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（起居舍人兼修玉牒实录院检讨官日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271819")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271819_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271819'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271819'>臣闻神宗皇帝相王安石用私意作《日录》，一时政事美则归己，陈瓘以死争之，著为《尊尧集》、《日录辩》等书，忠臣义士，感激增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271819_comment'></div>恭惟陛下躬履艰难，济登休治，宝慈与俭，仁民爱物，圣德之盛，固已聿追先烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271819_comment'></div>而故相信任之专，礼遇之隆，又非特如安石受知于神祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271819_comment'></div>臣窃谓政事举措，号令设施，一皆蔽自圣断，故相或能将顺赞襄而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271819_comment'></div>臣惧其作《时政记》，亦如安石专用己意，掠美自归，掩陛下之圣明，私群臣之褒贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271819_comment'></div>日历之官，因取其说著于简策，大非尊戴君父，传信万世之义，臣实恐惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271819_comment'></div>仰惟陛下既遴选史臣，付以论撰，欲望骏发明诏，再取去岁以前臣僚修过日历，详加是正，审订事实，贬黜私说，发明圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271819_comment'></div>庶几作宋一经，袭六为七，垂之无穷，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271819_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1271819_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1271814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论涵养人才劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271814")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271814'>臣闻国势之强弱，不系于土地之广狭，甲兵之利钝，而系夫人才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271814_comment'></div>所谓人才者有二焉：文章足以藻饰治具，风采足以羽仪荐绅，此平时用之而有馀者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271814_comment'></div>静有以察未形之机，动有以应方来之变，如药石真可疗病，如谷粟真可救饥，此则平时既不可不涵养蓄储，而羽檄交驰之际，则又不可顷刻而无此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271814_comment'></div>恭惟陛下以天纵之圣，躬履兴运，而宵旰求治，深思远虑，将以遗子孙万世之安，搜罗人才，惟恐或失，所谓藻饰治具、羽仪荐绅者固自不乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271814_comment'></div>然臣区区之忠，犹效此言者，诚惧夫实用之才尚少也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271814_comment'></div>夫楩、楠、杞、梓，自拱把知其为良，然不假之以岁月，培壅封埴，遽责之以任重，鲜有不挠折者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271814_comment'></div>是人才又贵夫涵养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271814_comment'></div>欲望圣慈深诏二三大臣，俾更广求实才可用之人，善谋能断，文不足而质有馀者，置诸中都，扶持长养，屡试熟察，以须其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271814_comment'></div>在平时则隆国势以折未萌，于缓急则受任奔走、御侮捍患无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271814_comment'></div>诚得一二十辈森布在列，则陛下可以垂拱无为，固宗社于磐石，而二三大臣亦可以优游怡愉于庙堂之上，而无所事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271814_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1271814_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年6月</a>　在京任秘书省正字。其伯父张邵卒，孝祥作祭文。作品：代诸父祭伯父文。<div id='poem_1272068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代诸父祭伯父文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272068")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272068'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272068'>维绍兴二十六年，岁次丙子，十月己巳朔，初六日甲戌，弟具位某等，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于先兄宫使待制张公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272068_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272068_comment'></div>我家故微，我祖则振，何以振之，曰德与仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272068_comment'></div>逮我先君，其艰其勤，益扬厥光，而卒不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272068_comment'></div>我观于乡，莫我之贫，人孰我怨，而咸我亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272068_comment'></div>化贪以廉，易浇以醇，巍巍阴功，与天理并，钟美于公，克宏厥因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272068_comment'></div>先君是师，少则有称，游于党庠，颀然凤麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272068_comment'></div>踔厉风发，超逸绝尘，徒步入关，蜚声成均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272068_comment'></div>擢第以归，谓当亲荣，陟岵告凶，衔哀茹辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272068_comment'></div>终丧筮仕，浙河之濆，携我诸季，奉先夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272068_comment'></div>则孝则慈，仰事俯循，家徒壁立，穆然春温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272068_comment'></div>羯胡乱华，京关缠氛，恸哭仰天，上书扣阍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272068_comment'></div>狡童逋诛，枢臣提军，以公参筹，亟奏厥勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272068_comment'></div>帝庸宠嘉，召见紫宸，公矢其谋，慷慨自陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272068_comment'></div>忠愤激发，肝胆轮囷，主辱臣死，臣敢爱身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272068_comment'></div>愿张皇威，于彼殊邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272068_comment'></div>宗伯之长，异数式敦，黄金九环，车朱两轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272068_comment'></div>我出我疆，虎狼缤纷，驱胁使从，九死是濒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272068_comment'></div>公曰我死，本朝则尊，唾骂逆豫，汝亡无辰，义动丑虏，野心亦驯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272068_comment'></div>顾视介者，既降而髡，公欲斩之，惧而宵奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272068_comment'></div>虏絷维公，犬羊与群，沙漠雪积，烟云尘昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272068_comment'></div>一节起居，面黧肤皲，饥肠齧毡，冻衣结鹑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272068_comment'></div>怀阙倾日，思亲望云，引脰南乡，泪乾声吞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272068_comment'></div>生还何时，十五秋春，天子怜公，番番良臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272068_comment'></div>我图尔功，其赞国钧，柄臣忌公，公歌《小旻》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272068_comment'></div>外祠延阁，淹留海滨，母子白首，䌽衣更新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272068_comment'></div>世赏之渥，燕及弟昆，风木不停，艰疚荐臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272068_comment'></div>三年庐墓，羸然哀茕，终老抱疾，斋厨无荤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272068_comment'></div>奸慝既屏，公道乃申，一麾池阳，起膺帝纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272068_comment'></div>布政未月，恩惠浃沦，条疏节披，剔蠹理棼，引疾遽还，莫谕所云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272068_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272068_comment'></div>小留归装，桐川之阴，忽与诸公，告诀周谆，曰悟大命，倾于浃旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272068_comment'></div>乃作治命，累数千言，书之简编，摽列缕分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272068_comment'></div>必以我丧，归葬四明，遍告朋友，及郡守丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272068_comment'></div>又移我书，如前之陈，我之得书，震惧以惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1272068_comment'></div>此岂戏耶，抑有其徵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1272068_comment'></div>遽往侍公，何疾之婴？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1272068_comment'></div>饮酒赋诗，欢如平生，惟是后前，棺椁衣衾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1272068_comment'></div>我苦谓公，弃此弗贞，公笑不答，促我以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1272068_comment'></div>六月乙未，公之初生，畴昔之夜，既沐而薰，顾谓诸孤，汝眠勿兴，寝以衣冠，寂无闻声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1272068_comment'></div>旦起视公，则公既薨，体柔色敷，蝉蜕之轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1272068_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1272068_comment'></div>使以讣行，于杭于升，我与季闻，糜肝沸心，奔走会丧，吁天不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1272068_comment'></div>念我先兄，大我宗祊，我辈宦学，须公以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1272068_comment'></div>胥保胥训，先子是承，有德未报，去骑箕星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1272068_comment'></div>二叔安鄂，欲来弗能，手足同体，剪焉摧倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1272068_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1272068_comment'></div>我公之生，松贞兰芬，金石其刚，冰鉴之清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1272068_comment'></div>终始大节，纪在汗青，尚须鸿儒，墓隧其铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1272068_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1272068_comment'></div>公之文章，如汉两京，浑浑其全，凿凿其精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1272068_comment'></div>挥毫落笔，龙蛇矫腾，一斗百篇，纸价为增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1272068_comment'></div>敬用纂辑，畀之云仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1272068_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1272068_comment'></div>我取遗训，一一作程，乃兹诸孤，婚嫁教令，我辈任责，其敢弗钦？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1272068_comment'></div>有渝此言，岂无鬼神？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1272068_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1272068_comment'></div>窀穸之期，卜此岁零，小留于郊，其居则宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1272068_comment'></div>诸孤在傍，以妥厥灵，逝者不留，三虞是临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1272068_comment'></div>帝有密章，贲于幽扃，匪作斯文，惟以荐诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1272068_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1272068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年8月</a>　充国子监点检试卷官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　除秘书省校书郎，兼国史实录院校勘。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　在京任秘书省校书郎兼国史实录院校勘。与范成大有书信往来。作品：答范司户。<div id='poem_1271922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答范司户</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271922")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271922'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271922'>捐书甚宠，非所当受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271922_comment'></div>又惟晚学冒进，来教以颂不以规，大非畴昔冀望于同年者，藏去悚仄而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271922_comment'></div>秋气高洁，伏惟坐曹清暇，体中胜常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271922_comment'></div>某出寒乡寂寞之滨，滥超众俊，寔自知其不可，而公朝乃以备史官之阙，朝夕惴惴，非朋旧推扬之过有是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271922_comment'></div>伏纸无任愧惕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1271922_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　在京任秘书省校书郎兼国史实录院校勘。是年，始与韩元吉游，委元吉为其妹法善择偶。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　在京任秘书省校书郎兼国史实录院校勘。初识张元干，与有诗酒之交。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='77317b41a4c04f7098ce2a9d7b75751b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("77317b41a4c04f7098ce2a9d7b75751b");'><span id='77317b41a4c04f7098ce2a9d7b75751b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1159')">1156-1159年</a>，25-28岁</div><div id='77317b41a4c04f7098ce2a9d7b75751b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　在京任秘书省校书郎兼国史实录院校勘。娶仲舅之女时氏为妻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　在京任秘书省校书郎兼国史实录院校勘。作《朱安之墓志铭》<div id='poem_1272067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朱安之墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272067")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272067'>始某不识安之，独闻其贤于某之从父，从父与安之游，相好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272067_comment'></div>安之没，其子绩、缜以志文属从父，从父命某，某不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272067_comment'></div>按安之朱氏，讳敦仁，出汉尚书令晖，自会稽徙鄞五世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272067_comment'></div>君生十年而孤，慎终无违礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272067_comment'></div>朱氏大族，外内千指，君壹训齐，盖居家严，处己约，与人恕，自其少时，则有恢厚长者之称矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272067_comment'></div>举进士不偶，弃归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272067_comment'></div>中岁家益丰，益务施，邻里缓急悉抵君，未尝以在亡辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272067_comment'></div>晚喜西方氏学，自谓有所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272067_comment'></div>属疾，以后事戒诸子，安卧而逝，享年六十有九，寔绍兴甲戌十有二月丁未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272067_comment'></div>曾王父文伟，王父用评，父揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272067_comment'></div>夫人徐氏，四男子：绩也，缜也，叔季早死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272067_comment'></div>二女子，适王造、刘楶，造今为山阳簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272067_comment'></div>孙男女十三人：九龄、九思、九功、九皋、九德、九泽、九成，女嫁董宏，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272067_comment'></div>君葬以既殁后二年，乡曰句章，原曰梅芝，月以辛丑，日以丙午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272067_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1272067'>有淑如君，卒不克施，有承其休，原寔委之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272067_comment'></div>梅芝之封，山川郁盘，君于此藏，既固既安。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1272067_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年1月20日</a>　转宣教郎（寄禄官）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年3月16日</a>　除秘书郎，依前兼国史实录院校勘。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　除著作郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　在京任著作郎。初交王十朋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　在京任著作郎。芝生太庙，上《原芝》，乞定储位。作品：原芝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（关于活动内容，宛敏灏《张孝祥年谱》（《词学》第二、三辑）将张孝祥上《原芝》事系于绍兴二十六年（1156））</span><div id='poem_1272026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272026?labeling=true' target='_blank'>原芝</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272026")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272026_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272026'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272026'>绍兴二十四年，芝产于太庙楹，当仁宗、英宗之室，诏群臣毕观，奉表文德殿贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272026_comment'></div>既二年，芝复生其处，校书郎张某作《原芝》，曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1272026'>非天私我有宋，我祖宗在天，笃丕祐于子孙，明告之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272026_comment'></div>于惟钦哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272026_comment'></div>在昔仁祖，登三咸五，以天下为公，授我英祖，以永我基祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272026_comment'></div>于惟钦哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272026_comment'></div>我圣天子躬济大业，既平既治，上恬下嬉，惟大本未立，社稷宗庙之灵，亦靡克宁飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272026_comment'></div>有烨兹芝，胡为乎来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272026_comment'></div>天维显思，命不易哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272026_comment'></div>和气致祥，敢曰不然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272026_comment'></div>曷不于他，乃庙产旃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272026_comment'></div>曷不于他，惟二宗之室？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272026_comment'></div>曷不于他，再岁再出？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272026_comment'></div>于惟钦哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272026_comment'></div>天意则然，我祖宗之意则然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272026_comment'></div>于惟钦哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272026_comment'></div>我二三辅臣，以告我圣天子，告我圣天子承天之意，承祖宗之意，早定大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272026_comment'></div>惟一无贰，纷以贰起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272026_comment'></div>辛伯有言，惟贰惟一，治忽所原，匪弗图之忧，惟贰之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272026_comment'></div>敢告圣天子，为万世虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272026_comment'></div>蠢尔小子，越职罪死，弗罪以思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272026_comment'></div>惟二三辅臣，以思以谋，告圣天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272026_comment'></div>言有一得，以裨吾国，万死奚恤，渠敢爱死而畏越厥职？</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1272026_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　除礼部员外郎。作品：除礼部郎官谢沈左相。<div id='poem_1271856' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271856' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271856?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除礼部郎官谢沈左相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271856")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271856_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271856'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271856'>考东观之艺文，方陪俊轨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271856_comment'></div>隶尚书之笺奏，遽列清曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271856_comment'></div>荷铨宰之殊知，躐官彝而超授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271856_comment'></div>伏念某幼而不学，长也益愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271856_comment'></div>出寒乡寂寞之滨，居游已陋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271856_comment'></div>袭老生陈腐之说，剽略奚工？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271856_comment'></div>策名虽冒于一科，触祸仅违于九殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271856_comment'></div>诸侯宾客，姑将稍试于所闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271856_comment'></div>上帝图书，即许窃窥于未见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271856_comment'></div>牙签云委，贝阙天横，蠹鱼枯文字之间，海鸟眩鼓钟之飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271856_comment'></div>瓶罂易耻，宜蒙碗脱之讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271856_comment'></div>组绣非能，敢望锦窠之目？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271856_comment'></div>始令承乏，旋使为真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271856_comment'></div>访台阁之大仪，顾非博综；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271856_comment'></div>诵朝廷之故事，尤愧清通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271856_comment'></div>盖一再岁之久虚，乃不崇朝而轻畀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271856_comment'></div>凌兢就职，激切怀恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271856_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇仆射相公道妙体元，诚纯育物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271856_comment'></div>皋、夔、稷、契，丕成极治之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271856_comment'></div>东、马、严、徐，尽入至公之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271856_comment'></div>占小善者率以录，示大贤之无不容，猥收场屋之虚名，亦玷省垣之高选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271856_comment'></div>某敢不靖共尔位，䌷绎旧闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271856_comment'></div>何目为郎，虽赖曲成于造命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271856_comment'></div>不遑将父，终期外补以便亲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1271856_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年7月</a>　在京任礼部员外郎。其父张祁除知楚州。<br /><a href="javascript:
