ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　在京任礼部员外郎。是年，其妹法善嫁韩元龙为继室。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　在京任礼部员外郎。从曾几（吉甫）游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　在京任礼部员外郎。代父上书左相沈该。作品：代总得居士上沈相该。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年3月</a>　在京任礼部员外郎。为周德友所藏后湖帖题跋。作品：跋周德友所藏后湖帖。<span class='inlineComment2'>（关于系年作品，宛敏灏《张孝祥年谱》（《词学》第二、三辑）认为本年同月张孝祥还作有《游无穷斋记》一文。）</span><div id='poem_1272006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋周德友所藏后湖帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272006")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272006'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272006'>德友少时，趣尚奇伟，一斗百篇，诸老先生慕与之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272006_comment'></div>今岁晚矣，讫未有识，一饱之不谋，可叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272006_comment'></div>右《后湖书帖》自甲轴至己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272006_comment'></div>绍兴二十八年三月望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1272006_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年8月6日</a>　在京试起居舍人。作品：辞免除起居舍人奏状。<div id='poem_1271835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除起居舍人奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年8月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271835")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271835'>今月六日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨除臣起居舍人，日下供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271835_comment'></div>臣闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271835_comment'></div>伏念臣顷以诸生，荷陛下亲擢，俾冠多士，触怨蹈祸，复蒙陛下脱臣父子于九死之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271835_comment'></div>兹又骤自省闼进侍殿陛，凡昔再生，与今超用，一出圣意，不缘他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271835_comment'></div>论报之心，虽臣躯命，非臣敢有，岂宜辄为辞避！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271835_comment'></div>寔以臣齿少人微，尘窃科第，甫及五年，备数南宫，已惧颠踬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271835_comment'></div>况秉笔柱下，专记言动，非辩智闳达，莫宜此选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271835_comment'></div>今台阁诸臣，学识资望高出臣右者不可胜举，苟臣冒宠躐据，必致清议弗容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271835_comment'></div>伏望陛下天地父母之恩，委曲哀怜，察臣危悃，非敢矫饰，追寝误恩，改授贤杰，庶安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1271835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年9月</a>　兼权中书舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年10月</a>　在京任起居舍人兼权中书舍人。与杨椿上《论王公衮复雠议》作品：论王公衮复雠议。<span class='inlineComment2'>（关于系年作品，宛敏灏《张孝祥年谱》（《词学》第二、三辑将张孝祥作《论王公衮复仇议》系于绍兴二十九年（1159））</span><div id='poem_1271820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论王公衮复雠议<span class='inlineComment2'>（兼权中书舍人日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271820")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271820'>复雠，义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271820_comment'></div>夫雠可复，则天下之人，将交雠而不止，于是圣人为法以制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271820_comment'></div>当诛也，吾为尔诛之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271820_comment'></div>当刑也，吾为尔刑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271820_comment'></div>以尔之雠，丽吾之法，于是为人子而雠于其父母者不敢复，而惟法之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271820_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271820_comment'></div>法行则复雠之义在焉故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271820_comment'></div>今夫佐、公衮之母既葬而暴其骨，僇尸也，父母之雠莫大于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271820_comment'></div>佐、公衮得贼而辄杀之，义也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271820_comment'></div>而莫之敢杀也，以谓有法焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271820_comment'></div>律曰：发冢开棺者绞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271820_comment'></div>二子之母遗骸散逸于故藏之外，则贼之死无疑矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271820_comment'></div>贼诚死，则二子之雠亦报，此佐、公衮所以不敢杀之于其始获而必归之吏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271820_comment'></div>狱成而吏出之，使贼洋洋出入闾巷，与齐民齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271820_comment'></div>夫父母之雠，不共戴天者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271820_comment'></div>二子之始不敢杀也，盖不敢以私义故乱法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271820_comment'></div>今狱已成矣，法不当死，二子杀之，罪也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271820_comment'></div>法当死而吏废法，则地下之辱沉痛郁结，终莫之伸，为之子者尚安得自比于人也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271820_comment'></div>佐有官守，则公衮之杀是贼，协于义而宜于法者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271820_comment'></div>椿等闻《春秋》之义，义在复雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271820_comment'></div>公衮起儒生，尪怯如不胜衣，当杀贼时，奴隶皆惊走，贼以死捍，公衮得不死，适耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271820_comment'></div>且此贼掘冢至十数，尝败而不死，今又败焉而又不死，则其恶必侈于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271820_comment'></div>公衮之杀之也，岂独直王氏之冤而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271820_comment'></div>椿等谓公衮复雠之义可嘉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271820_comment'></div>公衮杀掘冢法应死之人为无罪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271820_comment'></div>纳官赎弟，佐之请当不许；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271820_comment'></div>故纵失刑，有司之法宜如律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1271820_comment'></div>谨议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1271820_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年12月</a>　在京任起居舍人兼权中书舍人。年底，其父张祁改知蒋州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　在京任起居舍人兼权中书舍人。与知严州朱翌（新仲）有书信来往。作品：严守朱新仲五纸。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《严守朱新仲》，名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷三十五。）</span><div id='poem_1271912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271912?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上严守朱新仲</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271912")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271912_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271912'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271912'>某比者还，便奉真帖并石刻二诗、《龙溪序引》，既再拜钦诵斯文之妙，三复卒业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271912_comment'></div>又再拜曰，某何者，而先生乃欲教诲收拾，甚惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271912_comment'></div>而今而后，知不肖之身犹可自置于大君子之门，其不忍弃捐如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271912_comment'></div>即日春事已晚，不审坐观事物之变，台候何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271912_comment'></div>某为养窃禄，了无可言，何当侍前，少承耆德之绪论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271912_comment'></div>引望斋閤，卷卷何极！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271912_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1271912'>某春晚尝具记谢石刻序引之赐，盖委一亲戚行，其人自临安取间道入闽，未尝至大府，以故其书不达，复以见归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271912_comment'></div>伏念某乡里晚出，而于事先生长者之礼其略如此，则某既无可言者，然犹自列云云者，万有一先生尚察其无它而恕之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271912_comment'></div>即日不审台候何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271912_comment'></div>经纶德业，敛之一州，使年谷屡丰，闾里安阜者，固哲人之细事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271912_comment'></div>某赣愚不学，资浅齿少，而今兹除授，乃先众俊，朝夕惴惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271912_comment'></div>先生不怜而教之，复被褒借之辞，谨再拜辞避，不敢当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271912_comment'></div>日俟召还，以既愿见之愫，敢乞视时崇护，即膺三节之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271912_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1271912'>某皇恐死罪，敢言之，惟先生哀怜幸听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271912_comment'></div>某伯父凡三人，长尚书，次尝得官矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271912_comment'></div>建炎俶扰，尚书奉大母冯夫人渡江，诸弟悉从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271912_comment'></div>次伯父既娶，独顾松楸不忍去以死，惟馀一女于某姊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271912_comment'></div>冯夫人以其无父母，爱异它孙，嫁严陵朱氏，有子曰俊乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271912_comment'></div>冯夫人属纩时谓尚书曰：「吾怜二十九无孙，汝异时能官其外孙，吾不恨矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271912_comment'></div>二十九盖次伯父行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271912_comment'></div>绍兴二十五年，伯父舍其子而官俊乂，用冯夫人治命，以为己外生而任之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271912_comment'></div>命下而俊乂之父死，今终丧矣，而其家日贫困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271912_comment'></div>俊乂大母无恙，内外数十口，寡姊以书抵某言状，某欲尽取以来，则寡姊义无委姑而去，欲周之则不给，朝夕思之，莫知所以为计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271912_comment'></div>伏念先生为之师帅，使境内有一夫失所者，先生任以为己责，况此十口嗷嗷，饥饿濒死，先生不知之则已，苟知之，岂不恻然动心也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271912_comment'></div>故敢冒布腹心，伏惟先生施大惠于不报之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271912_comment'></div>或有所谓醯局者，月得二三十千，使俊乂托其名而食其禄，以养其重亲，以活其兄弟姊妹，以缓其旦莫沟壑之忧，以纾手足之念，则先生所以惠某者孰大于是！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271912_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1271912'>某伏蒙宠颁四公遗帖墨本，语意真切，字画劲正，可以想见当时风俗之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1271912_comment'></div>先生刻之乐石以表章之，其于学士大夫惠矣，而某遂拜赐，尤极欣荷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1271912_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1271912'>某晚学叨恩，以荣为惧，所冀肯赐某以言，使某朝夕服膺，周旋不失其身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1271912_comment'></div>而今兹溢于笺牍者，顾非某畴昔之望，怵惕移日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1271912_comment'></div>伏自惟念，岂不肖蒙陋不足以辱进于君子之列，而当世巨公不屑教诲之也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1271912_comment'></div>不然，愿有以赐之也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1271912_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年1月</a>　在京任起居舍人兼权中书舍人。引恩诏乞封继母时氏为恭人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　在京任起居舍人兼权中书舍人。是年春，王廉清、王明清、左鄯、郭世模、李大正、李泳等馆其家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年3月</a>　在京任起居舍人兼权中书舍人。其父张祁除淮南转运判官，兼淮南西路提点刑狱公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年5月</a>　在京任起居舍人兼权中书舍人。知枢密院事陈诚之降官，制词为孝祥所行，时人称誉。作品：陈诚之降官制。<div id='poem_1271748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271748?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈诚之降官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271748")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271748'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271748'>怀归有畏于简书，恩始从于均佚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271748_comment'></div>试可弗成于绩用，罚难逭于黜幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271748_comment'></div>既辜体貌之私，宜在谴呵之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271748_comment'></div>具官某始由科第，寖陟迩联，意其简默而不言，则亦深沉而可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271748_comment'></div>擢持兵柄，荐阅岁华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271748_comment'></div>退食自公，宜赴功而乐事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271748_comment'></div>括囊无誉，第持禄以保躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271748_comment'></div>逮庶务之稍繁，即抗言而请去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271748_comment'></div>弹章既上，宠数宜镌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271748_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271748_comment'></div>为祈父之爪牙，初期陈力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271748_comment'></div>视秦人之肥瘠，良负虚怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271748_comment'></div>服此宽洪，无忘循省。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1271748'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1271748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年6月</a>　在京任起居舍人兼权中书舍人。左相沈该落职，制词为孝祥所行，时人称誉。作品：沈该落职制。<div id='poem_1271746' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271746' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271746?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沈该落职制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271746")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271746_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271746'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271746'>君人临照百官，盖欲其精白以承休德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271746_comment'></div>宰辅仪刑四海，岂宜以宠利而居成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271746_comment'></div>繄予既老之臣，自丧不贪之宝，其还显秩，用厌师虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271746_comment'></div>具官某顷以藩条，擢闻机政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271746_comment'></div>惟人求旧，谓文武可以宪邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271746_comment'></div>秉国之均，何风采不如治郡！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271746_comment'></div>朕犹虚己，日伫告猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271746_comment'></div>精神强而折冲，未闻宏略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271746_comment'></div>血气衰而戒得，似减廉声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271746_comment'></div>既已乖鼎鼐之调，始欲挂衣冠而去，虽曲全于体貌，乃荐致于抨弹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271746_comment'></div>其镌秘殿之华，俾即安车之佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271746_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271746_comment'></div>君子慎始，防嫌疑于未然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271746_comment'></div>贵臣抵辜，尚迁就而为讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271746_comment'></div>慨往愆之莫救，期晚节以自全。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1271746_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　在京任起居舍人兼权中书舍人。进故事，以汉文帝、曹操、苻坚为例，力言“不可一日忘兵”及练兵、择将的重要性。作品：进故事二则。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年闰6月</a>　闰六月，试中书舍人。作品：谢除中书舍人表。<div id='poem_1271804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271804?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除中书舍人表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年闰6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271804")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271804_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271804'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271804'>螭坳秉笔，方愧空餐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271804_comment'></div>凤掖代言，遽叨亲擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271804_comment'></div>被身章而滋宠，捧诰牍以弥惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271804_comment'></div>恳避莫俞，省循增惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271804_comment'></div>窃以中书本命令之地，舍人典文字之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271804_comment'></div>学博艺精，斯能华国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271804_comment'></div>职清地近，岂可假人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271804_comment'></div>盖有思之敏者，未必畅于事情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271804_comment'></div>词之工者，未必穷于理致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271804_comment'></div>问古今则高、崔互有所得，评书诏则常、杨各擅所长，世每叹其才难，人亦随于器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271804_comment'></div>非夫言通志虑，识达典章，绚黼黻之文，邃渊源之业，则何以裁坦明之制，居清切之司？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271804_comment'></div>如臣者才不逮人，学徒泥古，偶玷名于巍第，俄策足于要津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271804_comment'></div>属内史之久虚，俾孤踪而代匮，方自虞于显黜，敢有望于为真！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271804_comment'></div>忽拜异恩，祇惭非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271804_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下图回至治，综覈群工，方将藻饰于皇猷，故必网罗于众俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271804_comment'></div>虽大公之施，不间疏微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271804_comment'></div>而小己何堪，误膺简拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271804_comment'></div>臣敢不仰承眷渥，益励操修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271804_comment'></div>职在丝纶，宁有弥缝之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271804_comment'></div>事专笔舌，敢忘献纳之忠！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1271804_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年闰6月</a>　在京任中书舍人。闰六月，上札子反对出卫卒往戍荆州，建议以夔州兵益荆州，转潼关之卒以补夔阙。作品：论卫卒戍荆州札子。<div id='poem_1271825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271825?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论卫卒戍荆州劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年闰6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271825")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271825'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271825'>臣仰惟陛下轸念上游，既以荆州付之刘锜，而又倚信听从，无一不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271825_comment'></div>伏观此来诏旨，为锜而下，数踰二十，如严制节、备官属、颁缗钱、增铠仗之类是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271825_comment'></div>顾中外之论，犹谓锜之所急，寔在兵少，欲出卫卒往戍锜所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271825_comment'></div>夫自吴至荆州，山川阻远，调发数千，与其孥俱，则是数万，不惟经行烦扰，亦非所以外示安靖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271825_comment'></div>臣愚窃欲效计，以谓取之于远，不若取之于近，所谓夔路是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271825_comment'></div>今诸路将兵，往往有名无实，臣尝询之，惟蜀为盛，成都万人，潼川六千，夔路四千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271825_comment'></div>夔之去荆，道路无几，若以夔兵二千益荆州，转潼川之卒以补夔阙，而下成都之甲如夔之数戍潼川，或岁时践更，或一定不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271825_comment'></div>如是则内无迁徙之为劳，外无疑间之可开，周旋几席之上，而形胜之强成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271825_comment'></div>议者必曰，夔当蜀后，夔守虚则蜀以危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271825_comment'></div>臣谓不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271825_comment'></div>自荆入蜀，取道峡中，地势险绝，人必鱼贯而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271825_comment'></div>荆在平衍之地，据吴、蜀之冲，使荆果强，则孰敢踰荆而窥蜀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271825_comment'></div>是夔虽有兵，寔置于无用之地，徙之于荆，则上可经蜀，下控沔、鄂，蜀既无虑，而上游亦固，一动两得，有利无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271825_comment'></div>伏惟陛下留神财幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271825_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271825_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1271825'>〔贴黄〕臣窃考祖宗旧制，诸将兵未有不更戍者，所以均劳逸，习道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271825_comment'></div>如蒙圣慈采择，乞下四川制置使及湖北帅臣同共措置，从长施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1271825_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年7月</a>　在京任中书舍人。与洪遵、王晞亮上疏议选人改官之法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　在京任中书舍人。临安宿卫成闵为了搪塞罪责而按劾部将，高宗姑息迁就，孝祥以处置失当，封还词头，上驳议。作品：缴驳成闵按劾部将奏。<div id='poem_1271824' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271824' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271824?labeling=true' target='_blank'>缴驳成闵按劾部将奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（中书舍人日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271824")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271824_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271824'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271824'>准中书省送到录黄一道，为成闵按劾西溪选锋第一将部将李因，全不照管人兵，致令逃窜，乞罢从军，与远小差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271824_comment'></div>奉圣旨依，李因添差江西安抚司准备差使，令臣书行者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271824_comment'></div>右，臣窃惟国家之所以惩劝天下，赏罚而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271824_comment'></div>然赏不当功，则不如无赏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271824_comment'></div>罚不当罪，则不如无罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271824_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271824_comment'></div>功罪已著而赏罚未行，则赏罚之权犹在也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271824_comment'></div>功罪著而赏非功，罚非罪，则为善者不劝，为恶者不惧，赏罚之柄于是失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271824_comment'></div>自闻西溪卒伍逃窜之事，既两旬浃，其所以不惮死而窜者，情之曲折，陛下既已知之，不待臣之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271824_comment'></div>然二十日之间，主帅而下，未闻略有黜责，外廷之臣不敢以为疑者，意朝廷方此图之而未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271824_comment'></div>今兹则大不然，朝廷既已不治其人，而成闵乃敢无所忌惮，公为劾章，归过队将，乞罢见任，仍送吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271824_comment'></div>夫掊刻军士，役使军士，利入于己，怨积于下者，闵与统制、统领官实为之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271824_comment'></div>闵不为之，则统制、统领官安敢为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271824_comment'></div>统制、统领官不为之，则将副、部队将安敢为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271824_comment'></div>朝廷委曲涵容，置闵与统制、统领官等一切不问，乃特用闵之言罢一队将，所谓队将者，何其独不幸也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271824_comment'></div>罚不当罪，臣恐浸失赏罚之柄，自此此辈愈更恣横，轻侮宪章，事虽至微，关系甚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271824_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈将成闵与当来士卒逃窜本军统制、统领、将副等官等第降黜，其本军统制官仍与罢免，庶为馀人之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271824_comment'></div>或陛下圣意不欲如此行遣，即乞将闵今来陈乞罢队将劄子亦不施行，以破小人诡计，以慰士卒之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271824_comment'></div>所有录黄，臣未敢书行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271824_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1271824'>〔小贴子〕臣访闻马军司寻常减刻军兵请受，及非时役使，最为酷虐，士卒怨帅臣入于骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271824_comment'></div>陛下圣聪，幽隐必察，谅必周知，臣不敢复布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271824_comment'></div>若因此时略与黜责，不惟馀人知所惩戒，亦可以收中原士卒之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271824_comment'></div>疏远冒闻，不胜恐惧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1271824_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年7月</a>　在京任中书舍人。与周麟之、洪遵联名举荐刘泽。作品：论荐刘泽奏。<div id='poem_1271823' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271823' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271823?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论荐刘泽奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271823")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271823_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271823'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271823'>臣等伏睹武功大夫、马军司后军统制刘泽，怀州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271823_comment'></div>初为刘锜偏将，锜器之，使特将一军，顺昌之役有隽功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271823_comment'></div>锜罢，泽以所部屯太平，都统王进掊尅苛暴，军人怨之刺骨，独泽抚士卒如子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271823_comment'></div>进有所科敛，泽一不从，进怒逐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271823_comment'></div>泽家无蓄储，即日乏食，旧部曲议赈给泽，泽不可，曰：「幸有官，可以归吏部」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271823_comment'></div>与其子徒步参选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271823_comment'></div>既判成矣，会马军司后军阙官，此军从刘锜久，倚功怙勇，将非其人，则或颉颃而不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271823_comment'></div>帅择将难之，有以泽告者，以为后军统制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271823_comment'></div>一军，顺，且畏且喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271823_comment'></div>泽之在后军，如在太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271823_comment'></div>军中分市官布，泽曰：「吾军贫甚，顾可以布与吾军耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271823_comment'></div>明日以状谢得布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271823_comment'></div>它日，令军中市瓦，泽又曰：「所居间屋尚多，瓦可撤也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271823_comment'></div>撤以与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271823_comment'></div>泽在军，自己俸之外，虽添给之属，不以一钱供其私，起居饮食，与士卒贱者等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271823_comment'></div>廉勤忠直，根于天性，自其侪伍，虽平时有不快于泽者，亦不能不称其贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271823_comment'></div>泽年五十有二，从军三十年，屡有战功，介于进取，不善委曲，专务奉公守职，存抚士卒而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271823_comment'></div>夷考其行，虽古名将何以过？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271823_comment'></div>是臣等采之公议，辄敢论荐，欲望圣慈将泽不次拔擢，以为中外之劝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1271823_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年8月</a>　在京任中书舍人。汪澈弹劾其“奸不在卢杞之下”，罢为提举江州太平兴国宫（外祠官），亲友颇受株连。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7135668fdabc4d05a6b89e296d81382e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7135668fdabc4d05a6b89e296d81382e");'><span id='7135668fdabc4d05a6b89e296d81382e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>，33岁</div><div id='7135668fdabc4d05a6b89e296d81382e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年2月</a>　以张浚荐，召赴行在（临安）。入对，上四札子。作品：论治体札子。论先尽自治以为恢复札子。论谋国欲一札子。论用才之路欲广札子。<div id='poem_1271826' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271826' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271826?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论治体劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（甲申二月九日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271826")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271826_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271826'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271826'>臣窃惟今日天下之事，可谓极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271826_comment'></div>国威未振，士气未立，财用殚匮，甲兵脆弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271826_comment'></div>譬之元气虚竭之人，百疾俱见，非医如俞、扁，有湔胃浣肠之术，莫能起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271826_comment'></div>天授陛下神圣英武，龙潜既久，周知天下之故，作其即位，则举兹世而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271826_comment'></div>独揽权纲，考核名实，忧劳图回，日不皇暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271826_comment'></div>顾惟内外小大之臣，不足以仰望清光之万一，是以再岁于兹，大勋未集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271826_comment'></div>然臣闻之，立志欲坚不欲锐，成功在久不在速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271826_comment'></div>治有大体，不当毛举细故；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271826_comment'></div>令在必行，不当徒为文具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271826_comment'></div>大僚欲其同德比义，共济艰难之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271826_comment'></div>群臣欲其宿道乡方，不为朋党之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271826_comment'></div>如是则内治不患其不修，外难不患其不弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271826_comment'></div>以此富国，以此靖民，以此复文、武之境土，以此摅高、文之宿愤，踌躇四顾，无不可为者已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271826_comment'></div>如其不然，臣恐药不当而病益深，则其忧有不可胜言者，惟陛下留神财察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271826_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1271826_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1271830' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271830' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271830?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论先尽自治以为恢复劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271830")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271830_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271830'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271830'>臣窃惟金虏不道，絷我行人，中外同愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271830_comment'></div>圣意坚决，申饬边备，以全制胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271830_comment'></div>如臣不肖，蒙被使令，感激隆知，誓当效死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271830_comment'></div>顾受任之初，有当为陛下言者，敢布一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271830_comment'></div>伏惟陛下神圣英武得于天纵，永念祖宗创业之难，太上皇付托之重，兢兢业业，不自暇逸，将以刷无穷之耻，复不共戴天之雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271830_comment'></div>天地鉴观，神灵孚祐，苟充是心，何求不获？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271830_comment'></div>然臣区区之愚，独愿陛下益务远略、不求近功而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271830_comment'></div>夫所谓务远略者，愿陛下尽舍拘挛，扫除积弊，去其所以害治者，而行其所当为者，起居饮食，不忘此志而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271830_comment'></div>夫所谓不求近功者，愿陛下多择将臣，激厉士卒，审度盈虚，踌躇四顾，不见小利而动，图功于万全而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271830_comment'></div>昔我太祖皇帝既得天下，诸藩跋扈，初未服从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271830_comment'></div>我太祖皇帝规模已定，不动声气，磨以岁月，皆为我有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271830_comment'></div>臣愿陛下以太祖皇帝所以平僭乱者为今日恢复中原之策，臣不胜幸愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271830_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1271830_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1271829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271829?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论谋国欲一劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271829")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271829_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271829'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271829'>臣居乡时，邻之富者有二子焉，一欲坐而商，一欲行而贾，而父莫之决也，而使之俱为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271829_comment'></div>二子之始谋非不善也，为其徒者，以二子之不协，则各幸其业之无成，相非而相残，相戾而相倾，居无何，其家卒以大困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271829_comment'></div>又有贫者，亦二子焉，以贫故，汲汲焉相与营致所以养其亲者，均衣而节食，内阋墙而外御侮，朝于斯，夕于斯，期丰其家而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271829_comment'></div>是人者，讫致千金之赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271829_comment'></div>夫富之与贫，图功之难易相去远矣，以其谋或一而或二，贫者以富，富者以贫，甚矣谋不一之为患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271829_comment'></div>《书》曰：「惟精惟一」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271829_comment'></div>又曰：「德惟一，动罔不吉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271829_comment'></div>又曰：「予有臣三千，惟一心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271829_comment'></div>夫惟不一，则天下之事虽至小而无成，况夫济艰难之运，起非常之治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271829_comment'></div>臣不胜忧国爱民之诚，惟陛下留神财察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271829_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1271829_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1271831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论用才之路欲广劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271831")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271831_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271831'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271831'>臣闻国之强弱，不在甲兵，不在金谷，独在人才之多少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271831_comment'></div>项羽未尝不强也，未尝不胜也，而高祖卒取天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271831_comment'></div>盖项氏之臣所谓杰出者，往往不能容，反为刘氏用，无惑乎项亡而刘之兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271831_comment'></div>臣恭惟陛下以英武不世出之姿，当艰难之时，独运神断，思济宏业，孜孜汲汲，二年于兹，而成功泯然未有端绪，盖所谓人才者尚少，不足以备使令耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271831_comment'></div>今入官之门虽广，而用才之路实狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271831_comment'></div>古者取于盗贼，取于夷狄，取于仇雠，取于姻戚，苟才矣，初不问其生出之本末也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271831_comment'></div>今兹不然，非进士科，则朝廷已不敢辄有除用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271831_comment'></div>幸而用一人焉，议者必曰：「此非清流也，此某人之戚党也，此某人之子若孙也，此故尝有所负犯也，此跌宕而不羁也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271831_comment'></div>其用武臣亦然，吹毛求疵，深排力沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271831_comment'></div>夫如是而欲力致天下之豪杰，以济非常之事，难矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271831_comment'></div>欲望圣慈深诏大臣，各体此意，舍去拘挛，收拾度外之士，博取而详察，以备缓急之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271831_comment'></div>大才既多，使之治财赋，使之治军旅，使之宣力四方，陛下将无往而不获，无为而不成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271831_comment'></div>臣不胜卷卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271831_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1271831_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年2月</a>　除中书舍人，迁直学士院，俄兼都督府参赞军事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　在京任直学士院兼都督府参赞军事。始与胡铨（邦衡）交。作品：同胡邦衡夜直。<div id='poem_546017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546017?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同胡邦衡夜直</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546017")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546017'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546017'>慕用高名二十年，敢期丹地接周旋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546017'>先生义与云天薄，老去心如铁石坚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546017'>梦了琼崖身益壮，烟销金坞臭空传。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546017'>一尊莫惜空相属，宫漏穿花夜色鲜<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作月满天）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546017'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546017_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　在京任直学士院兼都督府参赞军事。上札子乞调整军事部署、增加财用、裁减官司人吏。作品：画一利害。<div id='poem_1271827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>画一利害</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271827")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271827'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271827'>一、国家驻兵淮甸，根本之地，实在江南，沿江控扼，当有重镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271827_comment'></div>除建康系帅府外，如镇江、九江、武昌，守臣权轻，缓急难以责办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271827_comment'></div>欲望详酌，移浙西帅于镇江，江西帅于九江，鄂州则带沿江安抚使，仍拨蕲、黄、光三州为管内，遴选帅臣，使治城壁，缮修器械，训习本路兵民，积蓄财谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271827_comment'></div>责以岁月，务收实效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271827_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1271827'>一、窃闻议者欲分抛盐引于民间兑便钱物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271827_comment'></div>缘食盐之人有限，若一顿卖过，却须暗损榷货务常年所入之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271827_comment'></div>臣昨曾具白劄子，乞将妇人封号自恭人至孺人等第立价出卖，许人户书填与母若妻及女，如贵族品官之家，亦许与妾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271827_comment'></div>比之官诰，人更乐从，比之度牒，不损户口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271827_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1271827'>一、诸路如提刑、提举职事，以漕臣兼之有馀，空立两司，官吏浮费，每路不下数万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271827_comment'></div>欲乞详酌，尽行废并，逐司钱物，专委帅臣拘收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271827_comment'></div>其见役人吏，并合裁减，兵卒发归元来州军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271827_comment'></div>漕臣每路止置一员，依淮南体例兼诸司职事，仍不添置人吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271827_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1271827'>一、诸司属官初无职事，止能倚势作威，占破吏卒，搔扰州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271827_comment'></div>除诸路应办军事处量行存留外，其馀并当省罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271827_comment'></div>若监司实有职事合委属官，即于置司处就令州县官兼权，更不添请给人从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271827_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1271827'>一、州县百姓既出免役钱，有物力者犹当差科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271827_comment'></div>官户既免差役，役钱复免一半，轻重不均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271827_comment'></div>欲望详酌，将官户役钱据见科之数增起一倍，并同编户，其收到钱别项桩管赡军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271827_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1271827'>一、行在百司乞委台谏公共相度，将不系紧要处权行住罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271827_comment'></div>公吏并放逐便，候边事宁息日依旧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1271827_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

绍兴

-----title
合肥（庐州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c1186ea6dc724d23882b39b9a3ee8f77_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c1186ea6dc724d23882b39b9a3ee8f77");'><span id='c1186ea6dc724d23882b39b9a3ee8f77_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1160')">1159-1160年</a>，28-29岁</div><div id='c1186ea6dc724d23882b39b9a3ee8f77' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　由芜湖至庐州省父（其父张祁时任淮南转运判官兼淮南西路提点刑狱公事）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年11月</a>　随父居庐州。魏安行由户部员外郎出任淮南转运副使，兼淮南东路提点刑狱公中，孝祥代父作启致意。作品：淮东漕魏郎中。<div id='poem_1271853' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271853' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271853?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上淮东漕魏郎中启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271853")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271853_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271853'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271853'>京辇效官，屡瞻逸轨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271853_comment'></div>边亭奉指，乃借馀光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271853_comment'></div>岂曰为僚，于焉事长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271853_comment'></div>伏惟某官气吞馀子，学眇诸儒，未尝枉尺以直寻，真欲居今而行古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271853_comment'></div>凛乎一代之名士，备更险夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271853_comment'></div>信矣中兴之吏师，所至办治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271853_comment'></div>嗟守阙之虎豹，困横江之鳣鲸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271853_comment'></div>人谓斯何，厥有至公之论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271853_comment'></div>天其或者，将为大用之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271853_comment'></div>殆圣政之更新，偕群贤而汇进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271853_comment'></div>双旌引道，亟分刺史之符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271853_comment'></div>一节趣归，即覆郎官之锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271853_comment'></div>简注深厚，宠灵荐臻，升内阁之新班，专外台之剧寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271853_comment'></div>眷斯民俗，已熟教条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271853_comment'></div>旧所领州，尚郁去思之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271853_comment'></div>及兹开府，当成不戒之孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271853_comment'></div>仰窥训词，即俟报政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271853_comment'></div>某栖迟晚节，漫浪此官，方怀投劾之归，空切登车之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271853_comment'></div>念昔已同之臭味，于今复并于官曹，仰邻烛之分辉，庶山藜之不采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271853_comment'></div>隆寒在候，盛德对时，冀妙毓于生经，用丕迎于景贶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1271853_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年11月</a>　随父居庐州。参知政事贺允中为皇太后遗留国信使使金，孝祥有书致意。作品：贺参政。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《贺参政》，名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷三十八。）</span><div id='poem_1271958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上贺参政</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271958")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271958'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271958'>仲冬之月，尝具劄子仰干钧听，负罪屏处，不敢时以姓名自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271958_comment'></div>惟是区区尊依盛德，慕用恩纪，朝夕于心，未始间断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271958_comment'></div>岁律行尽，恭惟旄麾在道，天相忠贤，钧候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271958_comment'></div>参政先生全名高节照映夷夏，扬历三朝，圣天子深所倚赖，肆攽明命，往聘殊邻，将使中原遗老，瞻望马首，益坚思宋之心，天下幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271958_comment'></div>某出入门阑，积有年数，独恨不得充傔从，效奔走，引睇行府，神爽飞驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271958_comment'></div>政此苦寒，敢乞为宗社生灵加卫启处，亟听来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271958_comment'></div>大人昨蒙朝廷委捕黄贼，今遂擒馘而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271958_comment'></div>但日来所闻北耗，政尔纷纷，伏想庙算自定，应之有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271958_comment'></div>某官归期必在三月，载笔为谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271958_comment'></div>或云曾中躬亦在行途中，可以陪燕谭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271958_comment'></div>子云近尝得书，尝至舟次迎拜否？</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1271958_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年6月</a>　随父居庐州。其父张祁加直秘阁，依前为淮南转运判官兼淮西提刑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年7月</a>　随父居庐州。同知枢密院事叶义问进知枢密院事，奏应变、持久二说，提出备战方略，朝野为之振奋。孝祥因以其父名义上书叶义问，陈抗金之策。作品：代总得居士与叶参政。<div id='poem_1271961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代揔得居士与叶参政</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271961")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271961'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271961'>某仰惟相公昨者登贰西府，有识之士固已相庆，知相公非苟富贵者，得时而行，必大有以慰中外之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271961_comment'></div>既而又相庆曰：「虏之情伪深矣，相公亲涉其庭，且究知之，将为上尽言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271961_comment'></div>于是相公来归，天下倾耳以听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271961_comment'></div>乃七月丁酉，相公进长枢庭，而邮置所传相公避逊之章，所以复于上者，盖卓然以今日之事自任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271961_comment'></div>又传闻相公归自北鄙，即于昕朝力陈机会之不可失，黠虏包藏，宜深为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271961_comment'></div>天听既回，国势自尊，帷幄所筹，罔不慰惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271961_comment'></div>社稷幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271961_comment'></div>生灵幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271961_comment'></div>窃谓朝廷狃于和议将二十年，小大之臣以兵为讳，军政不修，边备阙然，长淮千里，东南恃以为藩篱者，一切置之度外，而彼犬羊之聚，鏖凶啸毒，未尝南乡而忘我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271961_comment'></div>自去春榷场废，朝廷始耸然知虏意之所在，将深图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271961_comment'></div>而上下议论或未然，一日复一日，又至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271961_comment'></div>今事迫矣，天其或者将遂悔祸，贻我宋中兴之基于万斯年，用是降大任于相公，当是责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271961_comment'></div>左丞相汤公忠贯日月，精虑微一，食息之顷，未尝不忧念国家，未尝不垂意人物，而往时诸贤，人各有心，或未知同寅协恭，以济鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271961_comment'></div>今天付相公以此事，上意如此，天意如此，相公之与汤公，讵可不深鉴往事，惟和惟一，以共图休功也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271961_comment'></div>伏惟相公深念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271961_comment'></div>饥者易食，渴者易饮，中原之人困于暴虐，困于旱蝗，困于力役，死者比屋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271961_comment'></div>遗民思宋之心，如遭水火而望救援，其势已急，千载一时，间不容发，伏惟相公深念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271961_comment'></div>绍兴初，诸将用兵淮上，亳、泗、徐、沂之人，箪食壶浆以迎我师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271961_comment'></div>师退，虏复取之，即尽屠其人以泄愤怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271961_comment'></div>然民终不悔，它日我师至焉，其迎我如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271961_comment'></div>去冬蒋州王俊但假托本朝名字，淮北之人信以为然，自蔡、颍至于河北，尅期响应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271961_comment'></div>会俊败获，事虽不克，然以此可见吾民之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271961_comment'></div>今我以一旅之众渡淮，则彼之锄耰棘矜皆为吾用，建瓴破竹，莫捷于此，独恐朝廷惮于先发耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271961_comment'></div>伏惟相公深念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271961_comment'></div>王、戚、李三将忠勇自力，义无返顾，然发纵指示，必惟其人，宜得大臣一其节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271961_comment'></div>事当豫定，若必待赤白囊至而后为之应，将无及矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271961_comment'></div>伏惟相公深念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1271961_comment'></div>今日议事之臣玩岁愒日，以相公与左丞相之所建立为不然者，以十人而九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1271961_comment'></div>秋冬之交，虏或未动，则是议者必杂然谓边头本无事，汤公、叶公过为之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1271961_comment'></div>又将自怠以弛吾备，以挫奋义者之心，患将益深，悔且噬脐，伏惟相公深念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1271961_comment'></div>某忧患摧伤之馀，所欠一死，登相公之门，盖自蚤岁，晚节末路，获备使令，受任之地，寔在穷边，平生志愿，庶其少见于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1271961_comment'></div>去岁单车赴古蒋，适丁互市之变，已而蒙恩摄帅除漕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1271961_comment'></div>某生长淮甸，知虏之情必不但已，日夜究心，心思为之惫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1271961_comment'></div>盖尝缕缕白之庙堂，至于十数，丞相汤公深以为当，然而某人微望轻，动辄龃龉，或者反以为罪，坐糜岁月，徒自慨叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1271961_comment'></div>今者相公既专宥密之寄，深思熟虑，日不暇给，将以戡外侮而隆内治，于斯时也，竹头木屑皆所不弃，况如某受知之深者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1271961_comment'></div>父子百口，毕命驱驰，指天誓心，罔有二事，伏惟相公怜而察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1271961_comment'></div>伏纸不胜忠愤激切之情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1271961_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　随父居庐州。夏秋之交，与知信阳军王之道有诗唱和。作品：某顷蒙信阳使君教以边字韵佳句伏读降叹病倦答谢甚缓复不能奇仰俟斫削二首。<div id='poem_545990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>某顷蒙信阳使君教以边字韵佳句伏读降叹病倦答谢甚缓复不能奇仰俟斲削<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545990")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_545990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545990'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545990'>风流追数建安年，谁遣朱轓并塞边。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545990'>举国向来儒服少，是邦端有大夫贤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545990'>须公帷幄收长策，著我江湖刺钓船。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545990'>池阁追凉肯临否，红妆翠盖拥三千。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545990'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_545990_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_545991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545991?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_545991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545991'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545991'>百适归来又一年，投身烽火戍楼边。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545991_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545991'>私忧自笑愚无策，制胜悬知国有贤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545991_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545991'>北去燕然堪勒石，西来樊口看烧船。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545991_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545991'>中州更有王夫子，笔阵犹能独扫千。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545991_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545991'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_545991_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='997784f597d14402835240d48d85261f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("997784f597d14402835240d48d85261f");'><span id='997784f597d14402835240d48d85261f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1161')">1160-1161年</a>，29-30岁</div><div id='997784f597d14402835240d48d85261f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年12月</a>　年底，返庐州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年1月24日</a>　随父居庐州。其父张祁落职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年1月</a>　随父居庐州。因其父落职放罢，孝祥代父上书宰相以自辨。作品：代总得居士上宰相。<div id='poem_1271846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代揔得居士上宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271846")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271846'>咎深百适，敢逃斋斧之诛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271846_comment'></div>恩予再生，愿广覆盆之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271846_comment'></div>仰止云龙之会，俯殚蝼蚁之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271846_comment'></div>伏念某晚学支离，残生寒窭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271846_comment'></div>躬耕自足，所愿力田而逢年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271846_comment'></div>世禄偶沾，本意为亲而捧檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271846_comment'></div>孤孽自怜于薄宦，廉隅窃慕于前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271846_comment'></div>虑捶楚之莫辞，实简书之是畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271846_comment'></div>诸公长者，猥借齿牙，清都太微，获望旒冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271846_comment'></div>退效一官于尘土，投闲二纪于江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271846_comment'></div>日莫而巾柴车，尝躬鄙事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271846_comment'></div>秋风之破茅屋，安所奠居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271846_comment'></div>虽周道如砥，何有于崎危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271846_comment'></div>而秦网凝脂，竟罹于罗织。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271846_comment'></div>会上圣权纲之独揽，贳下臣缧绁之非辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271846_comment'></div>缀毁裂之冠裳，招散离之魂魄，冀安晚节，绝望荣途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271846_comment'></div>何负薪之疾未瘳，而剖竹之符狎至，荐拜西州之繁使，适当北鄙之多虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271846_comment'></div>申命惟行，恳辞莫遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271846_comment'></div>念廊庙柬知之特达，且关梁捍御之阔疏，衅已结于搔爪，备初微于横草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271846_comment'></div>窃厉死封之志，遂忘负乘之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271846_comment'></div>李牧之居北边，费军租而享士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271846_comment'></div>营平之破羌贼，留步卒以屯田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271846_comment'></div>盗空狐鼠之群，吏戢豺狼之暴，周旋两稔，辛苦百为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271846_comment'></div>顾绩效之未闻，亦规模之粗定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271846_comment'></div>自嗟激烈，人笑迂疏，果飞谤之交攻，致劾书之趣上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271846_comment'></div>尚蒙观过，俾免所居，匪造化之曲成，殆生全之莫保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271846_comment'></div>雨流木偶，所念无归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1271846_comment'></div>火及池鱼，又将奚咎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1271846_comment'></div>聚族近盈于千指，为氓不办于一廛，疾病侵凌，亲朋弃绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1271846_comment'></div>固已阖门而恐惧，尚虞投隙以摧伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1271846_comment'></div>沥血摅辞，搏膺请命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1271846_comment'></div>伏望仆射相公广好生之德，察溢恶之言，悯其尝被于使令，颇亦服劳于奔走，稍援沟中之纳，俾留爨下之焦，收父子之馀年，归田园于故里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1271846_comment'></div>况仄席搜罗于豪杰，欲前筹开济于艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1271846_comment'></div>有如不肖之资，既乖已试之效，傥获洗湔于既往，庶将劝厉于方来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1271846_comment'></div>九顿首以自归，冀垂威听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1271846_comment'></div>三折肱而不悔，誓报隆私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1271846_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年2月</a>　随父居庐州。致书徐度（敦立），询抗金“庙论”作品：代总得居士上徐敦立。<div id='poem_1271852' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271852' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271852?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代揔得居士上徐敦立启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271852")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271852_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271852'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271852'>肃持虎节，还自龙荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271852_comment'></div>陟老上之庭，国威坐振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271852_comment'></div>曳尚书之履，天眷弥隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271852_comment'></div>仰繄徒御之劳，当有神明之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271852_comment'></div>共惟国信尚书学尊一代，气盖诸公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271852_comment'></div>大丞相之家，风流是似；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271852_comment'></div>古君子之操，夷险弗渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271852_comment'></div>方甲兵之问，不至庙堂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271852_comment'></div>惟忠信之人，可行蛮貊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271852_comment'></div>一星北去，三月南归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271852_comment'></div>乔木参天，谅切故都之感；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271852_comment'></div>雪花如席，可堪胡地之寒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271852_comment'></div>兹奉对于清闲，即参华于近密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271852_comment'></div>某栖迟薄宦，景仰壮猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271852_comment'></div>瞻十乘之元戎，莫遂前尘之拜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271852_comment'></div>荫千间之广厦，知无凌雨之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271852_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1271852_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
九江（江州）

target='_blank'>庾楼和林黄中韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", id='poem_sentence_0_546041'>九月扁舟下水风，一尊佳处与君同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546041'>眼高四海氛尘外，诗在千山紫翠中。<div ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546049")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546049'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546049'>珍重池阳鲁使君，忘年交契独情亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546049'>江山佳处公开府，风雨来时我问津。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546049'>翠逼笋舆松径合，绿随秧马稻畦新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546049'>东归剩作登临好，病怯诗肠故恼人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546049'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546049_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宣城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b9ac60cdadc64f2a94917942bd4226c0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b9ac60cdadc64f2a94917942bd4226c0");'><span id='b9ac60cdadc64f2a94917942bd4226c0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，30岁</div><div id='b9ac60cdadc64f2a94917942bd4226c0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　居宣城，得徐度来书，复之。作品：徐左司。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《徐左司》，名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷三十八。）</span><div id='poem_1271959' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271959' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271959?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上徐左司</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271959")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271959_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271959'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271959'>某自顷拜书，候使节之归，旋即侍亲来宣城，异县客寄，忧虞万端，杜门不敢与人事接，是故久疏遣问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271959_comment'></div>忽拜真帖之贶，亹亹数百千言，骈珠叠璧，窭人之所未识，又得之于留落放废、众人躏藉之馀，有怀感著，当如何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271959_comment'></div>麦秋欲晴，既晴辄雨，不审去天尺五，台候起居复何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271959_comment'></div>伏惟参釐万微，嘉政美泽，阴被宇内，宜有福祥来相君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271959_comment'></div>某屏迹诸况如前所云，但得水菽足以养亲，藜藿足以蓄妻子，无诸病则已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271959_comment'></div>官屋虽敝，然某遂假以为逐臣之居，恐复有以为罪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271959_comment'></div>环视茫然，不知所计，长者将何以教之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271959_comment'></div>弥纶中台，亦既更岁，华问休畅，善类引望大用，犹稽此何为耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271959_comment'></div>吾侪小人，尤日日以冀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271959_comment'></div>长公浙西之除，直为归觐之阶耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271959_comment'></div>方丈比得书，手足之戚殊不能堪，畿右之行得免，长者必赐调护也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271959_comment'></div>瞻望云霄，邈然未有侍见之日，仰乞为斯文崇养，亟闻除目之播。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271959_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1271959'>某乡来奏记，已而邮筒拜初冬所下教，政以大人去官，因循不办治报，愧惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271959_comment'></div>汉北之还，闻诸道涂，长者尽得其要领，以复于上，伏想庙论必已制胜于万全，然则在我之策，孰为之先耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271959_comment'></div>往者大人效官边鄙，二年其久，虏之情伪，知之为详，屡以所见闻于朝，独以疏远不赐省察耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271959_comment'></div>今兹放逐，尚口乃穷，岂敢复有云也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271959_comment'></div>诸贤辐凑来廷，强国尊主，真成馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271959_comment'></div>如某辈得一廛躬耕，自食其力，父子团栾，毕命丘樊，它何敢知耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271959_comment'></div>伏惟长者尚怜其情而照之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1271959_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年6月</a>　居宣城。刘锜为淮南、江南、浙西制置使，节制诸路军马，孝祥有书致意，愿“载笔后车，草露布以俟献”作品：又刘两府（某窃瞻国之盛衰）<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《又刘两府》，名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷三十九。）</span><div id='poem_1271964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又上刘两府</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271964")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271964'>某窃瞻国之盛衰，必观诸人望之用舍，谢太傅消摇东山，雅意丘壑，当时议者顾谓「安石不起，如苍生何」，言若大而夸，然卒之成肥水之功者安石也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271964_comment'></div>裴中立以谗居外，两河诸侯浸淫问鼎，中立复相，忠者怀而强者畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271964_comment'></div>人望之用果如何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271964_comment'></div>自五月来，朔方传闻汹汹，岂惟自江以北，百姓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1271964", 1271964, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>束担</span>以待，而江、浙之间，亦复骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271964_comment'></div>忽有邮书报相公开帅府以号令诸将，制册扬廷，恩礼赫奕，凡士大夫与夫闾巷之民、田夫牧人，莫不欢喜奔走，更相告语，以谓相公既用，则吾事必济，无得忧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271964_comment'></div>至于赤籍伍符，则又踊跃抃厉，以有赴敌致命，义无却顾之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271964_comment'></div>黠虏震慑，先声所暨，奉头鼠窜，遗魂落胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271964_comment'></div>乌乎休哉，古未有也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271964_comment'></div>恭惟某官不世之功成在旦夕，便当肃清宫禁，祗谒寝园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271964_comment'></div>某无似，庶将载笔后车，草露布以俟献也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271964_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1271964'>某以久不省祖茔，自宣城暂归历阳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1271964", 1271964, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>村落</span>，一二日复西上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271964_comment'></div>民间恃相公近在维扬，皆得自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271964_comment'></div>惟是民兵一事，朝廷忧惧，近日复有约束，分隶诸军，田野之人，愈更皇恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271964_comment'></div>孔子曰：「以不教民战，是谓弃之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271964_comment'></div>《周官》井田之法，春蒐、夏苗、秋狝、冬狩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271964_comment'></div>其坐作进退，固已阅习，而犹曰不教者，盖谓未尝教之以知礼、知义、知信、知勇，如子犯之所云也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271964_comment'></div>今之民虽坐作进退冥然不知，乃欲驱之以当大敌，民之死不敢自爱，万一沮吾军势，悔将何及？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271964_comment'></div>仰惟某官同国休戚，知无不言，况此淮民，又属戏下，敢告相公，具以利害达之冕旒，将两淮民社一切罢免，岂惟十万生灵皆出全护，脱性命于锋镝，而缓急之际，不误国事，尤其大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271964_comment'></div>伏惟相公垂情，无以某小子而废斯言，熟计而亟图之，无任激切恐惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1271964_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3de04cd3a9e443a7970c6323da992cc0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3de04cd3a9e443a7970c6323da992cc0");'><span id='3de04cd3a9e443a7970c6323da992cc0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1162')">1161-1162年</a>，30-31岁</div><div id='3de04cd3a9e443a7970c6323da992cc0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年9月</a>　居宣城。高宗下责己诏，表示决心抗金，孝祥感奋，上《庙堂札子》给宰相陈康伯。<div id='poem_1271962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上庙堂劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271962")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271962'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271962'>仰惟先生于从容无事之时，不动声气，为圣天子建万世之长策，远视古昔，寔所创见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271962_comment'></div>一昨丙子诏书既下，虽穷山幽谷，妇人孺子，亦皆感泣，盖所以慰率土之望，昭在天之灵，杜纷纠之源，一视听之归，再造炎图，端自此日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271962_comment'></div>而今而后，知黠虏之不敢侮我中国，诸将之不敢轻我朝廷，国势日隆，主威日振，而先生之道德勋名，能言之士所不得而称载也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271962_comment'></div>某负罪屏处，不得拜伏光范，为天下贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271962_comment'></div>然窃喜恩地茂勋先立，使某啜菽饮水，槁死岩谷之间，犹有荣耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271962_comment'></div>伏惟财幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1271962_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月</a>　居宣城。金兵南侵，诸将观望不前。孝祥代宣州守任古（信儒）致书王权，希望王权以国事为重，与诸将协义同力，尽去疑间，共同对敌。作品：代任信儒与王太尉。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《代任信儒与王太尉》，名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷二十四。）</span><div id='poem_1271905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代任信孺与王太尉<span class='inlineComment2'>（权）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271905")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271905'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271905'>某闻太尉之名旧矣，虽未识面，然尝一再通问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271905_comment'></div>及来宣州，见张漕父子日日称说太尉忠义纯一，智略沉雄，治军训旅，多多益办，今时诸将可一二数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271905_comment'></div>某是以击节<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1271905", 1271905, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>诵叹</span>，愿交下风，盖因致书，欲太尉以一干人之功名，保三十年之富贵，某所以与太尉心相知者甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271905_comment'></div>自黠虏渝盟，圣上奋发威断，以迄逋诛，天声震叠，山摇海蹙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271905_comment'></div>太尉兼心膂爪牙之任，杖旄秉钺，锐卒十万，式遄其驱，扬舲济江，分据险阻，可谓盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271905_comment'></div>中外之士，正望太尉以捷音闻，虽定林之役追北百里，然斩获不多，人心未快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271905_comment'></div>数日来或谓虏骑已越滁、寿，太尉复还历阳，果尔，则何为耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271905_comment'></div>淮西重地，朝廷所责望者专在太尉，李侯、成侯其实太尉麾下尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271905_comment'></div>事势之急如此，必三帅协义同力，首尾相应，尽去疑间，合为一家，然后为可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271905_comment'></div>今日调护兹事，独在太尉，太尉聪明，办此不难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271905_comment'></div>所愿太尉念主上平日眷遇之隆，不惮少屈，遣书致礼，交欢二帅，相与誓约，专意国事，屏除私心，尅日共举，以剪穷寇，以复境土，则太尉勋在社稷，身名俱荣，竹帛钟鼎不足称载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271905_comment'></div>万一不出乎此，各自为谋，少失机会，悔将何之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271905_comment'></div>忠愤激切，怀不能已，辄以尺书布之幕下，可否之决，立迟一报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271905_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1271905_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月</a>　居宣城。金兵南侵，诸将观望不前。孝祥以在野之身，致书李显忠，希望李显忠不负朝廷厚望，与诸将互相支援，共建大功。作品：与李太尉。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《与李太尉》，名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷二十四。）</span><div id='poem_1271904' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271904' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271904?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李太尉<span class='inlineComment2'>（显忠）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271904")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271904'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271904'>某闻之，当今号称人杰，磊落奇伟，可撼以义，独太尉三数公耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271904_comment'></div>今春过池阳，始识太尉，置酒高会，开心见诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271904_comment'></div>某窃不自揆，尝为太尉陈其所以报国一二事，太尉不以为罪，击节称善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271904_comment'></div>某于是益知太尉之贤，常常为士大夫道之，谓太尉尝以单骑九百，却二十万之众，它日边候有警，奋不顾身，星流彗扫，敌王所忾者，必太尉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271904_comment'></div>自黠虏渝盟，圣天子赫然震怒，悼已事之失策，诞布明诏，恭行天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271904_comment'></div>太尉膺上简拔，当国一面，悉甲济江，今踰月矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271904_comment'></div>虏骑浸淫，至于历阳，太尉之军，虽尝小捷，然虏既越险而南，幕府犹在舒城，不闻太尉出骑要击，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271904_comment'></div>岂既追北而此未知耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271904_comment'></div>抑太尉方略素定，儒生不得而测识耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271904_comment'></div>两日来羽檄自御前至太尉处者，相接于道，而迁徙之民，自北而来，所传益急，事势危迫，可谓间不容发矣，不知太尉将何策以处此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271904_comment'></div>今淮西之三帅列屯，朝廷安危，实系于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271904_comment'></div>太尉与王侯、成侯必须同心协力而后可以成功，若一人少有顾望，吾事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271904_comment'></div>伏望太尉思主上平日所以期待太尉之厚，委曲置念，交欢二帅，使无纤芥，专图国事，尽去私心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271904_comment'></div>若王侯当其前，则太尉宜与戚帅以锐师出其腹背，首尾齐应，各务致死，则虏众虽多，可以立溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271904_comment'></div>万一不然，少有沮抑，太尉将何以报天子，何以见天下之贤士大夫耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271904_comment'></div>望太尉精思之，速图之，无贻后时之悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271904_comment'></div>忠愤激切之怀，不能此尽，谨遣使臣莫师雄躬造帐前面禀，拱立西望，以俟嘉音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271904_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1271904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月</a>　居宣城。为其友王日休《净土文》作序。作品：龙舒净土文序。<div id='poem_1271999' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271999' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271999?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙舒净土文序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271999")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271999_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271999'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271999'>阿弥陀如来以大愿力摄受群品，系念甚简，證果甚速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271999_comment'></div>或者疑之，余尝为之言：阿弥陀佛，即汝性是；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271999_comment'></div>极乐国土，即汝身是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271999_comment'></div>众生背觉合尘，沦于七趣，立我与佛，天地悬隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271999_comment'></div>佛为是故，慈悲方便，开示悟入，现诸无量，如幻三昧，庄严其国，备极华好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271999_comment'></div>复以辩智，而为演说，令诸众生，欢喜爱乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271999_comment'></div>于日用中，能发一念，念彼如来，欲生其国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271999_comment'></div>即此一念，清净坚固，还性所有，与佛无异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271999_comment'></div>当是念时，不起于坐，阿弥陀佛，极乐国士，悉皆现前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271999_comment'></div>如是修习，乃至纯熟，幻身坏时，此性不坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271999_comment'></div>金莲华台，由性种生，往生其中，如归吾庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271999_comment'></div>诸佛菩萨，即我眷属，性无异故，自相亲爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271999_comment'></div>友人龙舒王虚中，端静简洁，博极群书，训传六经诸子数十万言，一旦捐之，曰：「是皆业习，非究竟法，吾其惟西方之归」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271999_comment'></div>自是精进，惟佛惟念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271999_comment'></div>行年六十，布衣蔬茹，重趼千里，以是教人，风雨寒暑弗皇恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271999_comment'></div>閒居日课千拜，夜分乃寝，面目奕奕有光，望之者信其为有道之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271999_comment'></div>绍兴辛巳秋，过家君于宣城，留两月，始见其《净土文》，凡脩习法门，与感验章著者，具有颠末，将求信道者锓木传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271999_comment'></div>或病虚中：「公儒者而好佛之酷若是，又欲率天下举以从公，不亦戾吾圣人之意耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271999_comment'></div>虚中应之曰：「圣人固云然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271999_comment'></div>《书》非圣人删耶，而曰『惟狂克念作圣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271999_comment'></div>夫狂去圣远甚，而一念之克，即到圣处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271999_comment'></div>众生一念念佛，即到佛处，如之何不可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271999_comment'></div>商太宰问圣于孔子，自三皇、五帝皆不以云，而曰西方有圣人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271999_comment'></div>庸讵知西方之圣人非佛谓耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271999_comment'></div>虚中诿予序其书，故并载之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271999_comment'></div>虚中名日休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271999_comment'></div>是岁十月旦，历阳张某序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1271999_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年11月</a>　居宣城。采石大捷，作词纪之，和庞谦孺（字佑父，或云佑甫）作品：水调歌头（雪洗虏尘静）<div id='poem_111535' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111535' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111535?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span>闻采石战胜和庞佑父</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111535")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111535_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111535'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111535'>雪洗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_111535", 111535, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>虏尘</span>静，风约楚云留。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111535'>何人为写悲壮，吹角古城楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111535'>湖海平生豪气，关塞如今风景，剪烛看吴钩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111535'>剩喜然犀处，骇浪与天浮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111535_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111535'>忆当年，周与谢，富春秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_111535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_111535'>小乔初嫁，香囊未解，勋业故优游。<div id='poem_sentence_5_111535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_111535'>赤壁矶头落照，肥水桥边衰草，渺渺唤人愁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_111535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_111535'>我欲乘风去，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_111535", 111535, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>击楫</span>誓中流。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_111535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_111535'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(111535)'>评注</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_546008'>帐殿称觞送喜频，德音借与万方春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546008_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546008'>指挥夷夏无遗策，开阖乾坤有至神。<div id='poem_sentence_4_546008_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546009' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546009?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546009'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546009'>鞑靼奚家款附多，王师直到白沟河。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546009'>小儒不得参戎事，赋赋新诗续雅歌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546009'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546009_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月</a>　居宣城。陪宣州守任古谒昭亭祠，访应庵、如庵二僧，有诗纪之。作品：奉陪宣守任使君谒昭亭神祠二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（关于活动内容，宛敏灏《张孝祥年谱》（《词学》第二、三辑）将张孝祥在宣城谒昭亭事系于绍兴三十年（1160））</span><div id='poem_546003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉陪宣守任史君谒昭亭神祠<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_546003_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546003'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546003'>缓驱千骑出朝京<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：门名）</span>，唤得春回眼界青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546003'>旗脚灵风来庙步，马蹄山雪过昭亭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546003'>极知太守怀忠款，端为君王荐德馨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546003'>惭愧去年冬十月，军书彻夜听鸣铃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546003'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546003_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546004?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546004'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546004'>丰年已卜稻如京，雪尽春从草际青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546004'>竹里红旗行点点，松间白塔见亭亭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546004'>暖回宿麦开寒色，风约疏梅度晚馨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546004'>却忆宣城李太白，也将诗句掣斋铃<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546004'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote'
