href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年闰2月</a>　闰二月，还宣城辞亲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年闰2月</a>　在宣城，过友人王朝英所居梅溪竹院，有题记。作品：题王朝英梅溪竹院。<div id='poem_1272003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题王朝英梅溪竹院</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年闰2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272003")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272003_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272003'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272003'>朝英童子时与余同师，已而同登名天府，不见十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272003_comment'></div>壬午春，余自建康还宣城，道过朝英所居，为留一昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272003_comment'></div>朝英诵近诗数篇，句法清丽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272003_comment'></div>方筑屋竹间，聚书谢客，益丰所学，盖朝英之进而及于古未可量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272003_comment'></div>张子曰：夫士惟学而后知不足，今朝英不以其能自画，车坚驭良，策之以无倦，异时余将复访朝英于竹院，则其所称叹又不止于诗而已也，朝英尚勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272003_comment'></div>闰月既望，张某安国题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1272003_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月</a>　在宣城，作文记上年宣州守任古修城备敌事。作品：宣州修城记。<div id='poem_1272028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣州修城记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272028")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272028'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272028'>宣为城，西南负山，东北踞溪流，幅员三千四百步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272028_comment'></div>建炎中，侍御史、直龙图阁会稽李公尝守以支溃卒，围阅月引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272028_comment'></div>公益治城，具器用，严为之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272028_comment'></div>当是时，江、淮之间，靡焉骚动，惟宣以城坚好，故不被兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272028_comment'></div>宣之人德李公，尸而祝之，盖距今辛巳馀三十年矣，而定陶任公亦以御史、直龙图阁继李之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272028_comment'></div>惟定陶公德成而行尊，实大而声宏，刚方以立朝，岂弟以牧民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272028_comment'></div>民听既孚，吏虔弗媮，教条一施，事讫于理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272028_comment'></div>乃视城垒，东倾西决；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272028_comment'></div>乃阅戎器，剥折蠹败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272028_comment'></div>公耸然惧曰：「吾惟守土，不此之务，吾失职矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272028_comment'></div>即日出令，裒材揆功，易圮以坚，增庳为崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272028_comment'></div>尺积寸会，役有成数，檄召下县，使以徒集，程督有制，犒赐有时，无偏徭，无堕工，一月而栽，再月而毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272028_comment'></div>千雉云矗，百楼山峙，屹嶪岋峨，若化而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272028_comment'></div>池隍险幽，门闼回阻，谁何周严，至者神沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272028_comment'></div>凡城所须，无一不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272028_comment'></div>既又冶金伐石，刓革揉木，杀簳傅羽，濡筋削角，练工之良，大治兵械，戈剑弓矢，櫜兜戟帜，视诸故府，乃易乃饬，枚计其凡四十万有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272028_comment'></div>邦人士女，四方宾客，骇叹其成，天造鬼设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272028_comment'></div>冬十月，虏驱绝淮，剪我合肥，蹂我历阳，流柹投鞭，规济天堑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272028_comment'></div>并江列城，焦然以忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272028_comment'></div>公旦起闻谍，色不为动，徐召宾佐，分畀其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272028_comment'></div>某调某卒，某赋某甲，某守某险，米盐薪刍，铁炭布帛，琐细之物，毛举其目，严以待命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272028_comment'></div>增斥堠，申火禁，察奸宄，诘逋逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272028_comment'></div>吏持笔牍，毕受成画，号令明壹，奔走就事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272028_comment'></div>邑居之豪，率其僮客，什伍相联，以艺自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272028_comment'></div>受粟取佣，丰杀以宜，旬日得战士五千，严兵登陴，部分整暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272028_comment'></div>驿闻诸朝，恩给台仗，朝莫阅习，导以醲赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272028_comment'></div>四邻绎骚，羽书交驰，吏骇人摇，滋不奠居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272028_comment'></div>而吾宣城，晏起早眠，在都在鄙，弗震弗惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272028_comment'></div>边之迁民，系路来归，振廪授地，罔不得所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272028_comment'></div>十有一月，首亮就毙，阖府文武，撰日解严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272028_comment'></div>父兄子弟，惟公之勤，欢喜踊跃，愿肖公象，置祠宇，如所以事李公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272028_comment'></div>公持不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272028_comment'></div>民不公之谋，亟营屋市中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272028_comment'></div>公命撤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272028_comment'></div>邦人曰：「公德著闻，天子且夺公归之朝，盍乞诸天子而留公」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1272028_comment'></div>则数百千人相与扶携走阙下拜疏，愿借公十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1272028_comment'></div>公又遣县吏禁止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1272028_comment'></div>民从间道疾驰，卒上疏，乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1272028_comment'></div>或谓某：「子之居是邦也，宜知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1272028_comment'></div>今吾父兄子弟将列公之事刻之金石，使子孙不忘公，文非子谁宜为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1272028_comment'></div>某谨应之曰：「不敢辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1272028_comment'></div>虽然，此公之细也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1272028_comment'></div>使公自是进而居可为之地，一众心以为城，尊主威，隆国势，以保障天下，此公之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1272028_comment'></div>而见于宣城者，公之细也，曾何足云劳苦？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1272028_comment'></div>父兄幸教某，某不敢辞，愿因父兄之言，书颠末以诏来今」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1272028_comment'></div>明年三月吉日，历阳张某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1272028_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
抚州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='071422c4323d4d77952617a7794e16b3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("071422c4323d4d77952617a7794e16b3");'><span id='071422c4323d4d77952617a7794e16b3_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　官知抚州。与曾季狸交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　官知抚州。临川兵乱，单骑驰赴军中平之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　官知抚州。出榜禁卖假药。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年6月</a>　官知抚州。孝宗即位，有贺表。作品：贺今上皇帝登极表。<div id='poem_1271790' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271790' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271790?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺今上皇帝登极表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271790")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271790_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271790'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271790'>星辉海润，方肇启于青宫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271790_comment'></div>地辟天开，遂丕膺于赤纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271790_comment'></div>有赫圣人之大宝，于昭天下之至公，庙社逾尊，华夷均庆<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271790_comment'></div>臣闻父传于子，振古虽然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271790_comment'></div>天作之君，若今未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271790_comment'></div>载纂开基之绪，惟新受命之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271790_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下博厚高明，齐庄中正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271790_comment'></div>翼翼之心不已，盖本躬行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271790_comment'></div>喁喁之望咸归，殆非人力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271790_comment'></div>仰太上复艰难之业，付吾君于谈笑之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271790_comment'></div>十一世而益光，迈建武中兴之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271790_comment'></div>八百年其增卜，侈成周过历之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271790_comment'></div>臣身在侯藩，精驰观阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271790_comment'></div>朝五日而善家令，胥瞻孝治之优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271790_comment'></div>复两京而还上皇，更徯大勋之集。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1271790_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年6月</a>　官知抚州。孝宗即位，遣妹夫李蟾进贺银一千两。作品：进登宝位银表。<div id='poem_1271801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进登宝位银表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271801")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271801'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271801'>受四海之图，方盛官仪之复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271801_comment'></div>铸九金之鼎，敢忘牧贡之修？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271801_comment'></div>怅违执玉之趋，祗效来琛之献<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271801_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下配天立极，如日升明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271801_comment'></div>所宝惟贤，已旁求于寿俊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271801_comment'></div>理财以义，且尽贳于逋租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271801_comment'></div>而臣职在剖符，礼应奉币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271801_comment'></div>侑称觞之万寿，知芹美之非珍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271801_comment'></div>簉交戟之百重，慕葵倾而徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271801_comment'></div>所有贺登宝位银一千两，谨遣妹夫进士李蟾捧表管押上进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271801_comment'></div>冒犯天威，臣无任<span class='inlineComment2'>（后阙）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271801_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1271801_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年7月</a>　官知抚州。史浩进参知政事，有书致之。作品：上史参政。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《上史参政》，名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷二十四。）</span><div id='poem_1271902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上史参政<span class='inlineComment2'>（浩）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271902")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271902'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271902'>某伏读制诏，参政以命世宗儒，东宫旧学，精神感会，臣主俱贤，显膺册拜，晋参国秉，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271902_comment'></div>伏念某畴昔登门，猥辱知遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271902_comment'></div>生长四明，丘墓所寄，阡陌相连，实同党里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271902_comment'></div>不敢献谀，愿效微忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271902_comment'></div>伏惟中兴以来，宫僚几人，若贤，若不肖，主上朝夕之游处，毫末曲折，弗逃圣鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271902_comment'></div>而简在眷礼，独公一人，事关运数，非偶然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271902_comment'></div>累月以来，擢用休显，中外之士，拭目歆艳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271902_comment'></div>知参政者则谓渟滀抱负，郁而未伸，逢辰遇合，逮今已晚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271902_comment'></div>其不知者直云师傅旧恩，适用故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271902_comment'></div>夫拔之众人之中，置诸百僚之上，自高宗、文王犹托诸梦卜，况如近时风俗益坏，横得一金，或媢疾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271902_comment'></div>窃料进而贺参政除拜于前，退而议参政阙失于后者，不无其人，故今日参政应之甚难，亦可惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271902_comment'></div>图易其难，图释其惧，参政之策将安出？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271902_comment'></div>愿参政深思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271902_comment'></div>今日朝廷之上，进用人才，措画边事，与凡号令因革，某事非，某事是，人不以属它宰相执政，必曰：「此史参政之为耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271902_comment'></div>盖用之骤则责之重，其理固然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271902_comment'></div>况参政方在北门，远方之人，以邸报不传，兴事造业，一出参政意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271902_comment'></div>今入政府，则此名益不可避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271902_comment'></div>以不可避之名，任甚重之责，当至显之位，然则参政将何以善始善终，以无负圣天子，以无负天下也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271902_comment'></div>自古在昔，莫难于君臣之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271902_comment'></div>二帝三代，置而勿论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271902_comment'></div>必上下一体，言行计从，虽父子兄弟之密，不得与乎其间，如高祖之于子房，先主之于孔明，我太祖皇帝之于赵中令，而后可以拨乱反正，创业垂统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271902_comment'></div>窃观陛下继太上皇帝而为之子，谈笑授受，虽二百年丕成之绪，然稽之天数与人事，寔纂承启运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271902_comment'></div>御极之初，惟新景命，光昭祖烈，将以传无穷而施罔极，必一遵建隆之旧，则陛下之得参政，何以异于艺祖之得韩王？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271902_comment'></div>参政于此，弥纶动化，开阖张弛，惟危惟微，可戒可畏，不一而足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271902_comment'></div>某虽愚不肖，诚愿有以言之，而参政择之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271902_comment'></div>参政傥许之言，则请条列以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271902_comment'></div>伏惟参政方辟大公至正之路，刍荛之贱，试将采择其善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1271902_comment'></div>某也狂率犯分，参政弗怒以教。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1271902_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　官知抚州。建鲁公堂，祀唐代宗朝任过抚州刺史的颜真卿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　官知抚州。知吉州王佐解职，道经临川，席间有妓咏诗，孝祥嘉之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年1月</a>　官知抚州。有诗追怀去年正月与任古谒昭亭。作品：去年正月三日雪霁入昭亭访应庵如庵二老今年在临川追怀往昔用寄卐庵韵。<div id='poem_546000' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546000' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546000?labeling=true' target='_blank'>去年正月三日雪霁入昭亭访应庵如庵二老今年在临川追怀昔游用寄卐庵韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546000")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546000'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546000'>蹇驴冲<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一本作踏）</span>雪度松林，齧<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一本作漱）</span>石溪流有令音。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546000'>旋摘白云濡燥吻，更参黄檗印初心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546000'>岚开复岭云千叠，冻合浮图玉数寻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546000'>一梦经年归去好，宦情全薄此情深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546000'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546000_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　官知抚州。二、三月间，其父张祁起知江州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年3月</a>　官知抚州。中书舍人张震（真父）得罪出朝，寄诗慰之。作品：寄张真父舍人二首。<div id='poem_546013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546013?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄张真父舍人<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546013")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546013_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546013'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546013'>玉佩琼琚出近班，仙槎从此到人间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546013'>聊须海内无双士，往镇坤维百二关。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546013'>御府应留霜简看，乡人休羡锦衣还。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546013'>呜呼国步艰危日，补衮悬知欠仲山。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546014' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546014?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546014_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546014'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546014'>投分平生不数人，忆陪文馆笑谈新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546014'>资中宰树看成拱，荆府诗筒迹又陈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546014'>已恨别离空岁月，那知解后亦参辰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546014'>古来命驾须千里，薄宦区区愧此身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546014'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546014_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年3月</a>　在抚州。转朝散大夫，除尚书仪司郎官，未就任，改知平江府，提举学事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年3月</a>　在抚州。与抚州新任陈知府交承，有启致之。作品：抚州陈知府。<div id='poem_1271890' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271890' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271890?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上抚州陈知府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271890'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271890'>硕肤之誉，久属厌于旧闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271890_comment'></div>斗大之州，乃淹翔于敏手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271890_comment'></div>岂独托交承之契，所欣蒙覆护之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271890_comment'></div>伏惟某官器业伟然，声华籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271890_comment'></div>家学之富，盖有本原；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271890_comment'></div>吏事之精，尤高盘错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271890_comment'></div>暂领一麾之寄，即严三节之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271890_comment'></div>乃眷临川，号称古郡，户乏中人之产，府无经月之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271890_comment'></div>贪吏乾没，既不哀杼柚之空；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271890_comment'></div>齐民无聊，皆去为囊橐之盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271890_comment'></div>宜有循良之政，来苏疲瘵之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271890_comment'></div>愚若孝祥，一无可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271890_comment'></div>糠秕在前之愧，夫何言哉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271890_comment'></div>瑾瑜匿瑕之仁，是所望也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1271890_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年3月</a>　从临川启程赴平江任，有诗书西津渔家。作品：去临川书西津渔家。<div -----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5d0eea4eeabc441e827ac004834ccf97_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5d0eea4eeabc441e827ac004834ccf97");'><span id='5d0eea4eeabc441e827ac004834ccf97_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>，32岁</div><div id='5d0eea4eeabc441e827ac004834ccf97' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年6月25日</a>　王寿朋自临川相从，到达平江后，孝祥送其归临川，作文纪之。作品：王寿朋归临川序。<div id='poem_1271994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王寿朋归霅川序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年6月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271994")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271994'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271994'>王寿朋自临川相从，度彭蠡，登庐阜，方舟顺流，尽览东南山川之胜，盖三阅月，至吴门而后别去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271994_comment'></div>寿朋幼游太学，为名进士，以其馀力旁通神农、黄帝之书，探囊起死，退然无骄色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271994_comment'></div>乡来宾客相与游从如寿朋耐久，可二三数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271994_comment'></div>临分置酒齐云，惘然为书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271994_comment'></div>隆兴初元六月二十五日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1271994_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　官知平江。扶植善类，锄抑强暴，判决如流，庭无滞狱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　官知平江。本年两浙大水，上札子乞不催两浙积欠。作品：乞不催两浙积欠札子。<div id='poem_1271828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271828?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不催两浙积欠劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（知平江府日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271828")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271828_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271828'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271828'>臣窃闻今年浙东、西州郡间被水患，陛下至仁恻怛，即降睿旨，分命监司赈给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271828_comment'></div>遂使数州之民，左餐右粥，如岁丰时，无转徙之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271828_comment'></div>隆恩厚泽，浃洽霶霈，何有纪极！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271828_comment'></div>然臣得之道涂，谓湖、秀诸州，犹催积欠，督责甚急，百姓颇复不堪，皆言圣天子轸念我曹，济之以食，而官司不能推广德意，乃追积年逋税，名色既多，何所从出？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271828_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特赐处分，两浙路监司州县，将今年以前民间所欠逐色科名税物，除官户公人及二等以上户外，其馀或与一切蠲免，或与权行倚阁，至来年秋成起催。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271828_comment'></div>如敢违戾，许人户越诉，及委御史台弹劾取旨，重寘典宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271828_comment'></div>仍令转运司遍榜晓示，庶使斯民家至户到，皆知陛下所以哀矜元元之诚意，而州县之吏不敢奉行灭裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271828_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1271828_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　官知平江。两浙大水，有诗感怀。作品：大麦行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　官知平江。为临安府讲易堂书额。<br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年3月</a>　三月上旬，赴阙陛辞，过镇江金山寺，为宝印禅师书苏绅游金山寺诗，有题跋，并为所建玉鉴堂题额。作品：题苏翰林诗后。<div id='poem_1272011' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272011' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272011'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272011'>右翰林侍读学士、赠太师、魏国苏公之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_545907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545907'>白衣老人无逢迎，香火未收东方明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 繁昌

id='poem_545952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留题彭泽故县修真观</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", id='poem_sentence_0_545952'>五月问修途，今日一百里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545952'>莫投彭泽县，愧此邑中士。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545952'>古观官道傍，借榻暂少憩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545952'>折腰向道士，乞我五斗米。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545952'>聊为奴仆饭，明日更早起<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545952'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_545952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_545952'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_545952_0'>⑴ 原校：一本作借榻容少休，高林度清风，似为客子谋　按：末四句小集卷下作较彼靖节翁，衷情相谬戾。不能早投簪，一官苦匏系。见人屡折腰，奔走徒自蹶。聊为奴仆饭，明日更早起。速过栗里去，毋遗高士鄙。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_545952_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
余干
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='13880cf5f70b404ab33ed9e4f320fea6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("13880cf5f70b404ab33ed9e4f320fea6");'><span id='13880cf5f70b404ab33ed9e4f320fea6_link' class='inlineComment2'>（创作缘起中，赵頙。交游者中，赵頙。）</span><div id='poem_546027' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546027' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546027?labeling=true' target='_blank'>馀干赵公頙<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集卷中作颐）</span>贤宗室也魏公题其堂曰养正且为作铭取易颐之义刻碑堂上予过之为赋诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546028'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546028'>眼里纷纷不要同，从教三径满蒿蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546028'>肯来与子谈周易，此去何人识魏公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546028'>家近星辰双阙北，身居烟浪五湖东。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546028'>清台有日占云气，一丈丰碑夜贯虹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546028_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546028'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546028_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
丰城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bac04c034b664bc58f3287d9835747fd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bac04c034b664bc58f3287d9835747fd");'><span id='bac04c034b664bc58f3287d9835747fd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>，34岁</div><div id='bac04c034b664bc58f3287d9835747fd' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>将至丰城，望山赋诗。作品：鸡笼福地在历阳将至丰城望一山宛然感之赋诗。<div id='poem_546029' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546029' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546029?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鸡笼福地在历阳将至丰城望一山宛然感之赋诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546029")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546029_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546029'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546029'>黄茅白苇径才通，忽见晴岚扫翠空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546029'>从吏只令俱蜑户，仙山何许是鸡笼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546029'>逢人渐觉交游少，问路仍行盗贼中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546029'>自是粗才合粗使，瘴乡那得便途穷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546029_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546029'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546029_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----detail
<div class='label1' id='1d56652463624e41918c6a09f0564a27_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1d56652463624e41918c6a09f0564a27");'><span id='1d56652463624e41918c6a09f0564a27_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>，34岁</div><div id='1d56652463624e41918c6a09f0564a27' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过临江，感怀赋诗。作品：入清江界地名九段田沃壤百里黄云际天他处未有也。<div id='poem_546031' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546031' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546031?labeling=true' target='_blank'>入清江界地名九段田沃壤百里黄云际天他处未有也</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546031")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546031_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546031'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546031'>野水㳽漫欲涨川，稻云烘日更连天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546031'>定无适粤千金橐，可买临江九段田。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546031'>黄犊眠边高树荫，白鸡啼处远炊烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546031'>此中若许投簪绂，便老锄耰卜数椽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546031'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546031_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过临江，为清江台题榜。<br /></div>

-----title
萍乡（袁州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0d403b759f874ba68a58ed1a89df8790_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0d403b759f874ba68a58ed1a89df8790");'><span id='0d403b759f874ba68a58ed1a89df8790_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>，34岁</div><div id='0d403b759f874ba68a58ed1a89df8790' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　过萍乡，为驿旁百年老杉题诗。作品：萍乡境上有驿傍有老杉余百本余过而爱之驿无名余名之曰爱直而为之诗又以告邑大夫赵君公廪曰使继自今为令者幸如君之贤也则此杉长存不然将斧斤斯民以自封植于杉何有。<div id='poem_545956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>萍乡境上有驿傍有老杉馀百本余过而爱之驿无名余名之曰爱直而为之诗又以告邑大夫赵君公廪曰使继自今为令者幸如君之贤也则此杉长存不然将斧斤斯民以自封植于杉何有</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545956")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545956'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545956'>此杉已百年，林立官道侧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545956'>鬼神所诃护，斤斧不敢迫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545956'>爱此遗直姿，凛凛有正色。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545956'>未云支大厦，聊以荫行客。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545956'>作诗调令尹，为我驿壁刻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545956'>但使杉长存，悬知令清白。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545956'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_545956_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
灵川
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='879347dfc8a440c79e49b470ce420ef5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("879347dfc8a440c79e49b470ce420ef5");'><span id='879347dfc8a440c79e49b470ce420ef5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>，34岁</div><div id='879347dfc8a440c79e49b470ce420ef5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年7月</a>　经灵川滑石驿，有诗题碧玉泉。作品：入桂林歇滑石驿题碧玉泉。<div id='poem_546160' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546160' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546160?labeling=true' target='_blank'>入桂林歇滑石驿题碧玉泉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546160")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_546160_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546160'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546160'>百折崎岖岭路头，一环清駃石间流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546160'>须君净洗南来眼，此去山川胜北州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546160'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_546160_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f63c2535771b4a418283e73da875c7cf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f63c2535771b4a418283e73da875c7cf");'><span id='f63c2535771b4a418283e73da875c7cf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>，35岁</div><div id='f63c2535771b4a418283e73da875c7cf' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
桂林
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='49bc44dd52ca41d79ae0ed741c54d80e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("49bc44dd52ca41d79ae0ed741c54d80e");'><span id='49bc44dd52ca41d79ae0ed741c54d80e_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年7月</a>　七月中旬到达桂林，备李金起义军寇境。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年8月15日</a>　官知静江。八月中秋，有词抒怀。作品：水调歌头（今夕复何夕）<div id='poem_111523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>不夜</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_111523", 111523, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>扶路</span>看遨头。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111523_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111523'>玉界拥银阙，珠箔卷琼钩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111523_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年11月7日</a>　官知静江。与郭道深、滕子昭、陈叔蹇游真山观、超然亭。作品：题真山观。<div id='poem_1272008' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272008' class='poemTitle onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1272008", 1272008, "Clauses/2/Comments/3")'>联骑</span>访无无道人，登永宁寺阁，遂入西山，煮茗于超然亭。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　官知静江。序赠吴镒。作品：送吴教授序。<div id='poem_1271995' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271995' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271995?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送吴教授序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271995")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271995_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271995'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271995'>临川于江西号士乡，王介甫、曾子固、李太伯以文为一代宗主，而皆其郡人，故居民多业儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271995_comment'></div>碌碌者出于它州足以长雄，故能文者在其乡里不甚齿录，独素行可考而后贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271995_comment'></div>吴氏子镒，余为州将时所举进士，方群试于有司，予因识之，登于朝中乙科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271995_comment'></div>知举者尝欲以冠多士，既不果，则为之延誉，一时名声籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271995_comment'></div>分教郴州学，以余之素也，来广西从余，历三时而后之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271995_comment'></div>余谓镒不以文胜，盖见贵于乡里者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271995_comment'></div>虽然，古之君子固有独行自立，举世非之而不悔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271995_comment'></div>至贵于乡里，犹未足道镒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271995_comment'></div>盖尚友古人，益思未见其止者与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271995_comment'></div>必试于烈火而后知玉，万物俱流而金石乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271995_comment'></div>余欲金玉镒也，镒勉之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1271995_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年12月8日</a>　官知静江。腊日，与刘子思等人同游伏波山还珠洞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年2月</a>　官知静江。二月初，张维行部归桂林，有词赠之。作品：鹧鸪天（去日清霜菊满丛）<div id='poem_181295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_181295' id='poem_sentence_2_1272037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年4月</a>　官知静江。王伯庠论其“专事游宴”，罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年5月1日</a>　在桂林。为张维（字仲钦）棠阴阁作文以记。作品：棠阴阁记。<div id='poem_1272035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>棠阴阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272035")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272035'>君子之为政，去之久而犹见思者，必有恻怛爱民之诚心，感于民也深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272035_comment'></div>故其来也，如慈父母之抚其子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272035_comment'></div>其去也，如父母舍其子而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272035_comment'></div>父母舍其子而去，子之心之思，宁有既耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272035_comment'></div>犹曰：「吾父母将复吾归」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272035_comment'></div>及其久而不复来也，思之之心益不能忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272035_comment'></div>于是过其宫室，见其所服用与其所爱乐，起敬起慕，尸而祝之，社而稷之，更数十百世而不敢怠者，盖昔之人以为父母，则今之人皆其孙子，孙子而事其祖，宜如何也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272035_comment'></div>余昔为中都官，闻闽有贤令曰张君仲钦，闽之人歌舞之，去而思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272035_comment'></div>前年余为建康，仲钦适通判府事，当涂阙守，余檄仲钦摄焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272035_comment'></div>居数月，余罢建康，仲钦亦代去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272035_comment'></div>余居当涂之别邑，往来田间，闻民之思仲钦，饮食必祷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272035_comment'></div>余曰：「张君之政何如，而使尔不忘若是」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272035_comment'></div>民曰：「我亦不能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272035_comment'></div>但去年有水菑，而君寔来，民不知水；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272035_comment'></div>今年水不为害，而吾惧然若将陨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272035_comment'></div>君之时，吾与官若相忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272035_comment'></div>君去我，我日与州县之吏接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272035_comment'></div>我亦不知其故，知思君而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272035_comment'></div>去年余来桂林，仲钦提点广西狱事，下车一月，冒黄茅瘴走二十五州，以扁舟渡海，吏士扣头涕泣交谏，仲钦搴裳登舟，半济，风作，舟师震骇，仲钦怡然不为动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272035_comment'></div>黜陟罢行，一皆考之民，民扶舆欢噭，以为百年未之见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272035_comment'></div>夫以当涂之思，则知闽之思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272035_comment'></div>以闽、当涂占之，仲钦之去岭表而还天朝也，民之思仲钦可胜述哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272035_comment'></div>昔召伯之教，明于南国，而人爱其甘棠，故余登仲钦之阁，名之曰棠阴，以识民异日之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272035_comment'></div>阁之前有榕木，交荫阁上，仲钦之所游息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272035_comment'></div>乾道丙戌五月朔日，历阳张某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1272035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年5月</a>　在桂林。五月底，与张维、朱元顺、郭道深等人游象山水月洞。孝祥名其亭为朝阳之亭，名其岩曰朝阳之岩，名其洞曰朝阳之洞，并作文以纪之。作品：游朝阳岩记。<div id='poem_1272036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272036?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游朝阳岩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272036")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272036'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272036'>丙戌上巳，余与张仲钦、朱元顺来游水月洞，仲钦酷爱山水之胜，至晚不能去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272036_comment'></div>僧了元识公意，即其上为亭，面山俯江，据登览之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272036_comment'></div>五月晦，余复偕两贤与郭道深来，水潦方涨，朝日在牖，下凌倒景，凉风四集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272036_comment'></div>仲钦忻然，举酒属余曰：「兹亭由我而发，盍以名之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272036_comment'></div>余与仲钦顷同官建康，盖尝名其亭曰朝阳，而为之诗，非独以承晨曦之光，惟仲钦之学业足以凤鸣于天朝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272036_comment'></div>今亭适东乡，敢献亭之名亦以朝阳，而岩曰朝阳之岩，洞曰朝阳之洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272036_comment'></div>元顺、道深合辞称善，即书岩石，记其所以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272036_comment'></div>张某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1272036_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年5月</a>　在桂林。五月底，与张维、朱元顺、郭道深等人游象山水月洞。孝祥名其亭为朝阳之亭，名其岩曰朝阳之岩，名其洞曰朝阳之洞，并次建康朝阳亭诗韵，作诗二首。作品：静江朝阳岩赓建康韵二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《静江朝阳岩赓建康韵》，诗名依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）目录。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年6月</a>　在桂林。六月初，游屏风山，得爱岩。作品：初得爱岩。<div id='poem_545931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初得爱岩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545931")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545931'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545931'>高岩划天门，仄径通乳穴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545931'>隈堆青螺髺，嵽嵲白玉阙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545931'>外有虎豹蹲，中恐蛟蜃蛰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545931'>东荣俯雷电，西出挟日月。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545931'>万壑生悲风，六月不知热。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545931'>但觉骇心目，未易纪笔舌。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545931'>平生山水趣，岭海最奇绝。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545931'>洞府二十四，未厌屐齿折。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545931'>晚乃得游此，馀地皆仆妾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_545931'>同来六七士，嗜好颇相蹑。<div id='poem_sentence_9_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_545931'>举酒酹山神，慰汝久湮灭。<div id='poem_sentence_10_545931_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_545931'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_545931_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年6月</a>　六月上旬，自桂林东归，有诗词数首。作品：罢归。罢归呈同官二首。西江月（窗户青红尚湿）<div id='poem_546073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>罢归</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546073")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546073_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546073'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546073'>亲老难为住，恩深许放归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546073'>北行湘水阔，南望瘴烟微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546073'>兵卫收门戟，征尘上客衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546073'>遥知六七月，喜气满庭闱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546073'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546073_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>罢归呈同官<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546074")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546074'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546074'>去年秋七月，我犯瘴烟来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546074'>赋少畬田熟，徭归驿路开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546074'>上恩均雨露，孤迹返蒿莱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546074'>想像山中趣，参差屐齿苔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546074'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546074_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546075?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_546075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546075'>游子归乡国，斯人滞冗曹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
祁阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='311979a5610f44048482b0cebfeed39a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("311979a5610f44048482b0cebfeed39a");'><span id='311979a5610f44048482b0cebfeed39a_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>六月下旬至祁阳，专程瞻仰浯溪中兴碑与元结故居，有诗词数首。作品：题朱元顺浯溪图。暑甚得雨与张文伯同登禅智寺。读中兴碑。水龙吟（平生只说浯溪）<div id='poem_545927' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545927' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545927?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题朱元顺浯溪图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545927")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545927_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545927'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545927'>去年过浯溪，王事有期程。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545927'>夜半度湘水，但见天上星。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545927'>平生中兴碑，梦入紫翠屏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545927'>已办北归时，十日穷攀登。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545927'>今朝复何朝，忽此短轴横。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545927'>历历眼中见，湘山无数青。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545927'>白云著山腰，楼阁秋气明。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545927'>便欲扶短策，下濯沧浪缨。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545927'>主人山水仙，妙处心自评。<div id='poem_sentence_8_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_545927'>元顺骨已冷，千载交盖倾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_545927'>赏音寄幅纸，益见忠孝情。<div id='poem_sentence_10_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_545927'>题诗疥公画，托我不朽名。<div id='poem_sentence_11_545927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_545927'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_545927_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_545934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>暑甚得雨与张文伯同登禅智寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545934")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545934'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545934'>老火陵稚金，聚作三日热。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545934'>舟行湘江上，蒸煮到鱼鳖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545934'>黑云起东北，一震山石裂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545934'>不知雨来处，但见风卷叶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545934'>银河倚天泻，高浪舞飞雪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545934'>只听打篷声，已觉凉意惬。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545934'>岸傍古佛屋，楼殿颇嵽嵲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545934'>不辞冲泥去，一看雨脚阔。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545934'>吾宗紫岩客，穷苦志不慑。<div id='poem_sentence_8_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_545934'>自我来浯溪，奔走已旬浃。<div id='poem_sentence_9_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_545934'>我懒久废学，愧子来挈挈。<div id='poem_sentence_10_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_545934'>相携得伟观，为子炽然说。<div id='poem_sentence_11_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_545934'>愿子领话头，吾今指摽月。<div id='poem_sentence_12_545934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_545934'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_545934_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_545889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545889' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545889?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读中兴碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545889")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545889_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545889'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545889'>绣绷儿啼思塞酥，重床燎香驱群胡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545889'>阿环锦袜无寻处，一夜惊眠摇帐柱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545889'>朔方天子神为谋，三郎归来长庆楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545889'>楼前拜舞作奇祟，中兴之功不赎罪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545889'>日光玉洁十丈碑，蛟龙蟠拿与天齐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545889'>北望神皋双泪落，祇今何人老文学。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545889'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_545889_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_111520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水龙吟<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>过浯溪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_111520'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111520'>平生只说<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_111520", 111520, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>浯溪</span>，斜阳唤我归船系。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111520'>月华未吐，波光不动，新凉如水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111520'>长啸一声，山鸣谷应，栖禽惊起。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111520'>问元颜去后，水流花谢，当年事，凭谁记。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111520_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111520'>须信两翁不死。<div id='poem_sentence_4_111520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_111520'>驾飞车，时游兹地。<div id='poem_sentence_5_111520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_111520'>漫郎宅里，中兴碑下，应留<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_111520", 111520, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>屐齿</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_111520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_111520'>酌我清尊，洗公孤愤，来同一醉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_111520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_111520'>待相将把袂，清都归路，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_111520", 111520, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>骑鹤</span>去，三千岁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_111520_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
衡阳（衡州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='63b299275efe4bb5958e43e05dc23fcc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("63b299275efe4bb5958e43e05dc23fcc");'><span id='63b299275efe4bb5958e43e05dc23fcc_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年7月7日</a>　七月初七，达衡州，有诗二首。作品：七夕。丙戌七夕入衡阳境独游岸傍小寺。<div id='poem_545908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545908?labeling=true' target='_blank'>七夕</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年7月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545908")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545908_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545908'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545908'>去年永州逢七夕，今年衡州逢七夕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545908'>往来不敢怨道路，迎送但知惭吏卒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545908'>年年七夕有定时，我行属天那得知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545908'>东西南北会逢汝，但愿强健无所苦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545908'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_545908_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_545935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_545935'>今夕已七夕，我犹在天涯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545935'>系船苍石根，人影散晚沙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545935'>上岸是修竹，仄径如行蛇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545935'>茅屋四五间，往昔佛所家。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545935'>经禅劫火尽，旧观初萌芽。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545935'>墙叠古瓦盆，僧披破袈裟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_545935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_545935'>更呼老奚官，卷芦作鸣笳。<div id='poem_sentence_12_545935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_545935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年7月15日</a>　游衡山，七月十五日登祝融峰，有诗。作品：上封寺。<div id='poem_545941' id='poem_sentence_1_111637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111637'>身在九光中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111637_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111637'>风露下，环佩响丁东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111637'>玉案烧香萦翠凤，松坛移影动苍龙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_111637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_111637'>归路海霞红。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_111637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年7月</a>　七月底，返衡州小憩，应州官之请，作文记乾道元年修葺州学事。作品：衡州新学记。<div id='poem_1272038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衡州新学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272038")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272038'>先王之时，以学为政，学者政之出，政者学之施，学无异习，政无异术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272038_comment'></div>自朝廷达之郡国，自郡国达之天下，元元本本，靡有二事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272038_comment'></div>故士不于学，则为奇言异行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272038_comment'></div>政不于学，则无道揆法守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272038_comment'></div>君臣上下，视吾之有学，犹农之有田，朝斯夕斯，不耕不耘，则无所得食，而有卒岁之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272038_comment'></div>此人伦所以明，教化所以成，道德一而风俗同，惟是故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272038_comment'></div>后世之学，盖盛于先王之时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272038_comment'></div>居处之安，饮食之丰，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1272038", 1272038, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>训约</span>之严，先王之时未必有此；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272038_comment'></div>然学自为学，政自为政，群居玩岁，自好者不过能通经缉文，以取科第，既得之，则昔之所习者，旋以废忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272038_comment'></div>一视簿书期会之事，则曰：「我方为政，学于何有」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272038_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272038_comment'></div>后世言治者常不敢望先王之时，其学与政之分与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272038_comment'></div>国家之学至矣，十室之邑有师弟子，州县之吏以学名官，凡岂为是观美而已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272038_comment'></div>盖欲还先王之旧，求政于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272038_comment'></div>顾卒未有以当上意者，则士大夫与学者之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272038_comment'></div>衡之学曰石鼓书院云者，其来已久，中迁之城南，士不为便，而还其故，则自前教授施君鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272038_comment'></div>石鼓之学，据潇、湘之会，挟山岳之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272038_comment'></div>其迁也，新室屋未具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272038_comment'></div>提点刑狱王君彦洪、提举常平郑君丙、知州事张君松，皆以乾道乙酉至官下，于是方有兵事，三君任不同而责均，虽日不遑暇，然知夫学所以为政，兵其细也，则谓教授苏君总龟，使遂葺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272038_comment'></div>居无何而学成，兵事亦已，环三君之巡属，整整称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272038_comment'></div>夫兵之已而治之效，未必遽由是学也，而余独表而出之，盖乐夫三君识先王所以为学之意，于羽檄交驰之际，不敢忘学，学成而兵有功，治有绩，则余安得不为之言，以劝夫为政而不知学者耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272038_comment'></div>凡衡之士，知三君之心，则居是学也，不专章句之务，而亦习夫他日所以为政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272038_comment'></div>不但为科第之得，而思致君泽民之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272038_comment'></div>使政之与学复而为一，不惟三君之望如此，抑国家将于是而有获与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272038_comment'></div>明年八月旦，历阳张某记。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1272038'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1272038_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0b18e5efa3b14ed9ad51f8609804d299_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0b18e5efa3b14ed9ad51f8609804d299");'><span id='0b18e5efa3b14ed9ad51f8609804d299_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>，35岁</div><div id='0b18e5efa3b14ed9ad51f8609804d299' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至长沙，拜会刘珙，有启。作品：刘舍人（五管旷官）<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《刘舍人》（启），名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷二十三。）</span><div id='poem_1271891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上刘舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271891")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271891_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271891'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271891'>五管旷官，已逭黜幽之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271891_comment'></div>三湘谋帅，又叨使过之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271891_comment'></div>亶惟衣钵之传，实有钧陶之自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271891_comment'></div>某奉身无术，与世全疏，冥行于利害之涂，窘处乎谗谤之薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271891_comment'></div>载从去国，屡遣作州，率以五六月之间，则为数千里之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271891_comment'></div>精神耗于忧畏，筋力疲于奔驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271891_comment'></div>忽去忽来，固未免揶揄之鬼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271891_comment'></div>乍贤乍佞，独奈何萋斐之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271891_comment'></div>岂无二顷之可耕，况复双亲之既老，决意投簪之适，弗图赐履之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271891_comment'></div>恭命而行，恳辞不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271891_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官学穷圣蕴，道觉民先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271891_comment'></div>羞昆崙，薄蓬莱，迥立风尘之表；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271891_comment'></div>决汝、汉，排淮、泗，横驰翰墨之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271891_comment'></div>比收一笑之功，遂殄陆梁之寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271891_comment'></div>虽在公以为馀事，然宽上之所甚忧，肆予环而召归，当告册而爰立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271891_comment'></div>即以所临之巨屏，付之承学之诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271891_comment'></div>某敢不谨守箴规，益思策励？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271891_comment'></div>老吾老，幼吾幼，方深蕲锡类之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271891_comment'></div>步亦步，趋亦趋，终难望绝尘之轨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1271891_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至长沙，拜会刘珙，有诗。作品：谢刘恭父玉潭月色真石室之赐。浣溪沙（卷旗直入蔡州城）<div id='poem_545909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_545909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545909'>何人遗我双玉瓶，武夷先生翰林卿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272155_comment'></div>乃眷门阑之旧，获承尊俎之馀，陈九献之缛仪，表十连之盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272155_comment'></div>某官声名四海，翰墨两朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272155_comment'></div>骑麒麟而翳凤凰，簉丛霄之嘉会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272155_comment'></div>射鵔鸃而掩翡翠，扈紫禁之清尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272155_comment'></div>主眷式隆，士心景附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272155_comment'></div>八命伯，九命牧，具瞻赐履之雄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272155_comment'></div>万石簴，千石钟，载旌帅阃之伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272155_comment'></div>静扫绿林之寇，严趋清跸之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272155_comment'></div>望碧纱之笼，久注神仙之籍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272155_comment'></div>听白麻之告，径跻丞弼之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272155_comment'></div>况嗣建于旌旄，实亲传于衣钵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272155_comment'></div>且慰列城之望，少为数日之淹，醉我旧官，寿公慈母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272155_comment'></div>声流夜瑟，莫非鼓舞之儿童；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272155_comment'></div>泪点秋竿，却是攀留之父老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272155_comment'></div>某等幸瞻高宴，猥列贱工，敢酌民情，上陈口号：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1272155'>年时授钺许专征，蜂蚁千屯一笑清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272155_comment'></div>已变耕桑弥旷野，却驱旌旆入神京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272155_comment'></div>才从湘水东边去，且到台星极处明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272155_comment'></div>传语邦人莫留恋，使君元是我门生。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1272155_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年7月</a>　官知潭州。为陈琦（择之）书克斋铭及圣师问答。作品：题陈择之克斋铭。<div id='poem_1272013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272013?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题陈择之克斋铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272013")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272013_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272013'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272013'>陈琦择之，名其斋曰克，张敬夫为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272013_comment'></div>某复为书圣师问答与敬夫之铭，置斋中左右序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272013_comment'></div>乾道丁亥七月，张某识。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1272013_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。谢尧仁（梦得）来访，与论诗文。作品：湖湘以竹车激水粳稻如云书此能仁院壁。读谢梦得文。送谢梦得归昭武。<div id='poem_545937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545937' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545937?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖湘以竹车激水粳稻如云书此能仁院壁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545937")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545937'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545937'>象龙唤不应，竹龙起行雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545937'>联绵十车辐，伊轧百舟橹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545937'>转此大法轮，救汝旱岁苦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545937'>横江锁巨石，溅瀑叠城鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545937'>神机日夜运，甘泽高下普。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545937'>老农用不知，瞬息了千亩。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545937'>抱孙带黄犊，但看翠浪舞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545937'>馀波及井臼，舂玉饮酡乳。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545937'>江吴誇七蹋，足茧腰背偻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_545937'>此乐殊未知，吾归当教汝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_545937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_545937'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_545937_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1272004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读谢梦得文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272004")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272004'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272004'>梦得天下之奇士，彼龌龊者固不足以知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272004_comment'></div>其文浩瀚，如卷东海而注之江、河，奇伟激越，纷万车甲马而争驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272004_comment'></div>视其外，则枯木寒灰，槁项黄馘，若真无意于兹世者之所为。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1272004_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546098' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546098' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546098?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送谢梦得归昭武</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546098")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546098_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546098'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546098'>莫吟青玉案，恐弊黑貂裘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546098'>国步艰难日，人间浩荡秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546098'>不须鸟工往，且作贾胡留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546098'>后夜回春阁，凄然一段愁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546098'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546098_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。秋，送别张孝仲，有诗用长子张同之韵。作品：送仲子弟用同之韵。<div id='poem_546097' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546097' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546097?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送仲子弟用同之韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546097")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546097_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546097'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546097'>凄然鸿雁影，晚岁索衣裘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546097_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546097'>惜别湘江夜，归程楚甸秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546097_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546097'>极知违定省，不敢更淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546097_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546097'>明月分携处，无言只是愁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546097_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546097'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546097_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。筑敬简堂，以为论道之所。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年10月</a>　官知潭州。朱熹应邀来长沙。作品：朱编修（敬简堂记遂烦挥翰）<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《朱编修》（尺牍），名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷四十。）</span>题朱元晦所书凯歌卷后。<div id='poem_1271968' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271968' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上朱编修</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271968")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271968_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271968'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271968'>某敬服名义，愿识面之日甚久，非敢为世俗不情语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271968_comment'></div>得刘丈书，又见与钦夫书，知且为衡岳之游，傥遂获奉从容，何喜如之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271968_comment'></div>不胜朝夕之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1271968'>某昨日方从钦夫约，遣人迓行李，奉告，乃承已至近境，欣慰可量！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫必授馆，不然当于我乎馆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271968_comment'></div>使令辈遣前，恐远来者须更休耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271968_comment'></div>应有委，乞示下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1271968'>风雨留人，尊候复何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271968_comment'></div>《登台》诗彊勉不工，《出师表》同上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271968_comment'></div>老兄游山，亦须待稍晴，未可以遽，千金之躯，宜自爱惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271968_comment'></div>洪涛际天，溺马杀人，将安之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1271968'>某平生慕用，岂谓来湘中乃获解后接款，慰幸可胜言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271968_comment'></div>怀亲遽归，苛留不得，至今慊然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271968_comment'></div>人还，一再奉赐书，感服感服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271968_comment'></div>某老者深动东归之兴，比已专介请祠，力致恳诸公，傥遂得之，不旬月去此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271968_comment'></div>枢庭编摩，望虽高，然非所以处元晦也，意者姑借此为掀擢之渐耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271968_comment'></div>此间诸事，钦夫诸友书中必能详言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271968_comment'></div>政远披承，千万珍护，即登严近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1271968'>《敬简堂记》遂烦挥翰，真可以托不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271968_comment'></div>但堂中之人，于敬简工夫殊未进，须士友不我遐弃，时时训厉之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫间相从，未尝不矫首奉思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271968_comment'></div>黄君内艰，可念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271968_comment'></div>仲隆想已趋朝，更不作书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271968_comment'></div>怀英行已踰月，临行疡作于背，甚可念，幸而即愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271968_comment'></div>渠自去岁得渴疾，此不可再也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1271968'>某别去再见新岁，怀乡道义不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271968_comment'></div>自来荆州，老者病甚思归，舟楫往来江上，不复定处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1271968_comment'></div>仆亦心志忽忽，百事尽废，虽如元晦，一书亦不暇遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1271968_comment'></div>乃两奉诲教，相予之意益勤，内省愧惕，不但不答书可以为罪，盖敬简之功不进，它日无以见吾元晦耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1271968_comment'></div>某自到官即请去，凡六七，最后乞致仕，乞寻医，且欲不俟报弃官而归，诸公乃亦相察，今复得祠禄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1271968_comment'></div>近制不必俟代者，已治舟楫，载衣囊，五七日便可离此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1271968_comment'></div>刘丈之去，奇哉伟哉，此行至江上，当迂数程见之，亦约钦夫，又不知肯来否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫却数通书，定叟将有远役，兄弟不能相舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1271968_comment'></div>张仲隆前后五劄议论过人，皆某所不能言者，叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1271968_comment'></div>元晦阙期已及，闻未有幡然之意，如何如何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1271968_comment'></div>某有田在谢家青山下，屋十馀间，下俯江流，今归真不复出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1271968_comment'></div>元晦异时或欲览江、淮山川之胜，乘兴东游，则仆可以奉从容于梁山、博望、慈湖、采石之间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1271968_comment'></div>此外惟为斯文珍重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1271968'>某近因至城西，于土中得一碑趺，细视之，良有刻画，盖明皇所注《道德经》幢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1271968_comment'></div>磨治之馀，仅可识，即以十夫掘取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1271968_comment'></div>其半在土中者甚完，字画非经生所能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1271968_comment'></div>已舁置府中，今装褫一本去，钦夫极爱之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1271968_comment'></div>经磨治处中有大穴，盖以载他碑者，尤古，类汉碑，并遣上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1271968_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题朱元晦所书凯歌卷后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_546286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546286'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546286'>我词不足录，聊以醒渠醉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546286'>更参三十年，当与风子对。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546286'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_546286_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年10月</a>　官知潭州。朱熹应邀来长沙，孝祥与其有酬唱之作。作品：酬朱元晦登定王台之作。<div id='poem_546107' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546107' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。十月底或十一月初，朱熹由潭州去衡山，孝祥为饯行，有词相送。作品：南乡子（江上送归船）<div id='poem_111579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111579' class='poemTitle href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。为政简易，时济之以威。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。送雷*之临武为令，有序。作品：送临武雷令序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（创作缘起中，雷潈。交游者雷潈。）</span><div id='poem_1271997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送临武雷令序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271997")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271997'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271997'>雷氏子潨为临武县令，将行，问所以为县于子张子，敬与之言：夫虎豹之暴也，犹豢而畜之，岂非度其意之所安而逆其情之惧者与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271997_comment'></div>是以王者之治本人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271997_comment'></div>今吾临武之人，人也，其好生而恶死，趋利而辟害，与吾等也，独奈何以夷视之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271997_comment'></div>故吾愿雷子之居是官，不欲夷其民，善推其所愿欲而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271997_comment'></div>摩而抚之，搏而磔之，其宽其猛，各有攸当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271997_comment'></div>雷子之为临武，将以是而有济与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271997_comment'></div>未可知也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1271997_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。有词寄张维（仲钦）、朱元顺、滕子昭。作品：临江仙（试问宜楼楼下竹）<span class='inlineComment2'>（关于系年作品，宛敏灏《张孝祥年谱》（《词学》第二、三辑）系此词于乾道四年（1168））</span><div id='poem_111577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111577?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_111577'>试问宜楼楼下竹，年来应长新篁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111577'>使君五岭又三湘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111577'>旧游知好在，熟处更难忘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111577_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111577'>遥怜阴过酒尊凉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_111577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。有词寄朱元顺。作品：念奴娇（绣衣使者）<div id='poem_111567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>再和</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111567")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111567_comment'></div><div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_111567", 111567, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>应须</span>天上去，一日君恩三接。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111567'>臣心如水，不教炙手成热。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111567_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111567'>还记岭海相从，长松千丈，映我秋竿节。<div id='poem_sentence_4_111567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_111567'>忍冻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_111567", 111567,
