ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。与朱熹有书信来往，告熹“已专介请祠”作品：朱编修（某平生慕用）<div id='poem_1271968' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271968' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上朱编修</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271968")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271968_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271968'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271968'>某敬服名义，愿识面之日甚久，非敢为世俗不情语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271968_comment'></div>得刘丈书，又见与钦夫书，知且为衡岳之游，傥遂获奉从容，何喜如之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271968_comment'></div>不胜朝夕之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1271968'>某昨日方从钦夫约，遣人迓行李，奉告，乃承已至近境，欣慰可量！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫必授馆，不然当于我乎馆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271968_comment'></div>使令辈遣前，恐远来者须更休耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271968_comment'></div>应有委，乞示下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1271968'>风雨留人，尊候复何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271968_comment'></div>《登台》诗彊勉不工，《出师表》同上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271968_comment'></div>老兄游山，亦须待稍晴，未可以遽，千金之躯，宜自爱惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271968_comment'></div>洪涛际天，溺马杀人，将安之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1271968'>某平生慕用，岂谓来湘中乃获解后接款，慰幸可胜言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271968_comment'></div>怀亲遽归，苛留不得，至今慊然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271968_comment'></div>人还，一再奉赐书，感服感服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271968_comment'></div>某老者深动东归之兴，比已专介请祠，力致恳诸公，傥遂得之，不旬月去此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271968_comment'></div>枢庭编摩，望虽高，然非所以处元晦也，意者姑借此为掀擢之渐耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271968_comment'></div>此间诸事，钦夫诸友书中必能详言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271968_comment'></div>政远披承，千万珍护，即登严近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1271968'>《敬简堂记》遂烦挥翰，真可以托不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271968_comment'></div>但堂中之人，于敬简工夫殊未进，须士友不我遐弃，时时训厉之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫间相从，未尝不矫首奉思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271968_comment'></div>黄君内艰，可念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271968_comment'></div>仲隆想已趋朝，更不作书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271968_comment'></div>怀英行已踰月，临行疡作于背，甚可念，幸而即愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271968_comment'></div>渠自去岁得渴疾，此不可再也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1271968'>某别去再见新岁，怀乡道义不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271968_comment'></div>自来荆州，老者病甚思归，舟楫往来江上，不复定处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1271968_comment'></div>仆亦心志忽忽，百事尽废，虽如元晦，一书亦不暇遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1271968_comment'></div>乃两奉诲教，相予之意益勤，内省愧惕，不但不答书可以为罪，盖敬简之功不进，它日无以见吾元晦耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1271968_comment'></div>某自到官即请去，凡六七，最后乞致仕，乞寻医，且欲不俟报弃官而归，诸公乃亦相察，今复得祠禄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1271968_comment'></div>近制不必俟代者，已治舟楫，载衣囊，五七日便可离此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1271968_comment'></div>刘丈之去，奇哉伟哉，此行至江上，当迂数程见之，亦约钦夫，又不知肯来否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫却数通书，定叟将有远役，兄弟不能相舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1271968_comment'></div>张仲隆前后五劄议论过人，皆某所不能言者，叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1271968_comment'></div>元晦阙期已及，闻未有幡然之意，如何如何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1271968_comment'></div>某有田在谢家青山下，屋十馀间，下俯江流，今归真不复出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1271968_comment'></div>元晦异时或欲览江、淮山川之胜，乘兴东游，则仆可以奉从容于梁山、博望、慈湖、采石之间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1271968_comment'></div>此外惟为斯文珍重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1271968'>某近因至城西，于土中得一碑趺，细视之，良有刻画，盖明皇所注《道德经》幢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1271968_comment'></div>磨治之馀，仅可识，即以十夫掘取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1271968_comment'></div>其半在土中者甚完，字画非经生所能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1271968_comment'></div>已舁置府中，今装褫一本去，钦夫极爱之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1271968_comment'></div>经磨治处中有大穴，盖以载他碑者，尤古，类汉碑，并遣上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1271968_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。冬，为欧阳汇（字晋臣）万卷堂作文以记。作品：万卷堂记。<div id='poem_1272041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>万卷堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272041")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272041'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272041'>欧阳文忠公之诸孙曰汇字晋臣者，居庐陵之安成，筑屋其居之东偏，藏书万卷，扁之曰万卷堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272041_comment'></div>乾道丁亥冬，晋臣自庐陵冒大雪过余于长沙，曰：「汇堂成久矣，而未有记也，愿以为请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272041_comment'></div>夫人莫不爱其子孙也，而为之善田宅，崇货财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272041_comment'></div>今汇有三子，不愿以此愚之也，盖辛勤三十年，以有此书，以有此堂，而使三子者学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272041_comment'></div>余以为文忠公之德宜有后也，而今未之闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272041_comment'></div>充晋臣之志，其在兹已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272041_comment'></div>其在兹已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272041_comment'></div>晋臣归，幸为我告之：古之所谓读书者，非以通训诂、广记问也，非以取科第、苟富贵也，亦曰求仁而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272041_comment'></div>仁之为道，天所命也，心所同也，圣人之所觉焉者也，六经之所载焉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272041_comment'></div>得乎此，一卷之书，有馀师矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272041_comment'></div>不然，尽读万卷之书，以为博焉，其可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272041_comment'></div>以为知读书，则未也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1272041_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　官知潭州。为汪文举撰墓志铭。作品：汪文举墓志铭。<div id='poem_1272064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272064?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汪文举墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272064")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272064_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272064'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272064'>余年十八时居建康，从乡先生蔡君清宇为学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272064_comment'></div>清宇之门人以百数，有汪氏子胶者，小于余两岁，修谨敏锐，独异流辈，余亦敬而友之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272064_comment'></div>方是时，胶之家在豫章，独其大父字文举云者携胶以俱，欲胶之有成也，不复治他事，昼夜督课，与胶上下卧起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272064_comment'></div>居无何，胶崭然有声场屋，连取乡荐，号名进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272064_comment'></div>后十年，家君奉使淮南，胶之父处仁官舒之桐城，亦以才办治，家君荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272064_comment'></div>盖胶之学以有立，与处仁之能其官，文举寔使之然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272064_comment'></div>文举今死矣，胶以铭见属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272064_comment'></div>余与胶游二十年，余官临川、吴门，胶尝千里来过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272064_comment'></div>其守建康也，胶受馆于余，为直记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272064_comment'></div>余居于湖，胶率两三月辄一来，来即留一月或四五十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272064_comment'></div>盖与胶投分如此，而文举能教其子孙，又可铭也，铭其何疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272064_comment'></div>文举之先建康人，徙豫章之武宁，遂为武宁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272064_comment'></div>事亲以孝称，亲亡哀毁过礼，虽老矣，言及其亲，未尝不泣也，以是子孙皆孝谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272064_comment'></div>家饶财，自奉甚约，至周人之急，剧于己事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272064_comment'></div>绍兴初，江西旱，米斗数千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272064_comment'></div>文举视其囷仓，尚可得缗钱十数万，尽斥之以与邻里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272064_comment'></div>有王生坐大狱，请尽鬻其产文举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272064_comment'></div>文举蹙然曰：「若是则而家何以生耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272064_comment'></div>视其直并券归之，王生赖以免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272064_comment'></div>文举之父字平甫，幼孤，尝随其母适李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272064_comment'></div>文举视李氏与汪姓等，经纪其家，教其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272064_comment'></div>它日，李之子有醉而溺死者，文举哭之恸，厚葬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272064_comment'></div>胶方试春官，未之知也，梦衣冠而谢者曰：「吾而不谨死于水，荷君大父归骨于土矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272064_comment'></div>间阅内典有得，属纩不乱，乾道丁亥二月戊子也，年七十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272064_comment'></div>葬以十一月乙酉，祔以夫人李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272064_comment'></div>四男子：处仁，秉义郎，监江州甲仗库；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272064_comment'></div>处恭、处隽为进士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272064_comment'></div>处厚早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272064_comment'></div>孙三人：长胶也，珙、圭其季也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272064_comment'></div>孙女五人：归镇江府录事参军张汲、将仕郎王嗣宗、进士黄廷佐，处者二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272064_comment'></div>曾孙瀛、溉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272064_comment'></div>文举名翥，文举之父曰安，祖曰安弼，曾祖曰岫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272064_comment'></div>文举尝命于朝，得初品官，非其好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272064_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1272064'>武宁之东，长湖之原，文举兹藏，后将多贤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1272064_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年12月6日</a>　官知潭州。送宋子华归乡。作品：送野堂老人序。<div id='poem_1271996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271996' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271996?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送野堂老人序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年12月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271996")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271996'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271996'>乾道丁亥六月，余来长沙，于是金华宋君子华为之丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271996_comment'></div>子华老于学校，忠厚慈祥，练习典章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271996_comment'></div>事之来也，子华虽不言，而意之所属，盖得之于眉睫之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271996_comment'></div>某得师焉，以免于戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271996_comment'></div>子华今归矣，某盖娄申之于有位者而未达也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271996_comment'></div>虽然，达不达于子华何足道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271996_comment'></div>夫不在其身，必在其子孙，子华年固未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271996_comment'></div>子华由是显，以为天子之名卿才大夫，则必惟其宜，将其后四世五公也耶，未可知也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271996_comment'></div>十有二月六日，历阳张某安国书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1271996_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年12月15日</a>　官知潭州。为郑子礼新堂书扁为记。作品：寿芝堂记。<div id='poem_1272042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272042?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寿芝堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年12月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272042")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272042'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272042'>秘阁修撰襄邑郑公子礼，自湖南转运副使就拜本路提点刑狱，提刑置司衡州，而衡州，子礼落南寓家所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272042_comment'></div>于是有芝产于内寝，一本九茎，五色备具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272042_comment'></div>子礼筑新堂未有名也，客或考芝之祥，名之曰寿芝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272042_comment'></div>盖五芝生五岳，得以和药，皆致神仙，寿千岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272042_comment'></div>子礼今年七十有二，康宁而好德，其奉使典州，皆有绩惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272042_comment'></div>语曰：仁者寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272042_comment'></div>则芝之生，岂徒然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272042_comment'></div>余与子礼广西、湖南同官，又有连也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272042_comment'></div>既书其扁，又为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272042_comment'></div>乾道丁亥十二月望，历阳张某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1272042_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年1月15日</a>　官知潭州。上元设醮，有词二首。作品：鹧鸪天（咏彻琼章夜向阑）鹧鸪天（子夜封章扣紫清）<div id='poem_111706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹧鸪天<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>上元设醮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111706")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111706'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111706'>咏彻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_111706", 111706, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>琼章</span>夜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_111706", 111706, id='poem_sentence_1_111706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111706'>九光倒影腾青简，一气回春绕绛坛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111706_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111706'>瞻北阙，祝南山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111706'>遥知仙仗簇清班。<div "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>翡翠</span>帘开识<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_111706", 111706, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>圣颜</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_111706_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_111714' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111714' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111714?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹧鸪天<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111714")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111714_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111714'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111714'>子夜封章扣紫清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111714'>五霞光里佩环声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111714'>驿传风火龙鸾舞，步入烟霄孔翠迎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111714_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111714'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_111714", 111714, id='poem_sentence_4_111714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_111714'>三湘五管同民乐，万岁千秋与帝龄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_111714_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年1月15日</a>　官知潭州。元宵与张栻、邵怀英分韵。作品：元宵同张钦夫邵怀英分韵得红旗字。<div id='poem_545985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元宵同张钦夫邵怀英分韵得红旗字<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545985")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545985'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545985'>佳月妒纤云，微和扇东风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545985'>聊持一杯渌，共此千灯红。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　官知潭州。与吴伯承多有酬赠唱和之作。作品：南歌子（人物羲皇上）吴伯承生孙分韵得啼定字。从吴伯承乞茶。和伯承送茶韵。和伯承惠笋。次吴伯承送苦笋消梅韵二首。<div id='poem_111581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_11_545965'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_545965_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　官知潭州。二、三月间，下乡劝农，有诗。张栻等随行。作品：劝农以湘波不动楚山碧花压阑干春昼长为韵得干字。<div id='poem_545961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>劝农以湘波不动楚山碧花压阑干春昼长为韵得干字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545961")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545961'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545961'>积雨已连月，长沙尚春寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545961'>今朝定何朝，唤客来江干。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545961'>问讯湘西寺，雾重江漫漫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545961'>聊须万斛舟，渡此千尺湍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545961'>老松如相迎，翠落头上冠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545961'>却望城中花，宝髻垂珠鬘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545961'>劝农有故事，般乐非所安。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545961'>薄晚会春园，老稚随马鞍。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545961'>彘肩侑尊酒，呼唤来同盘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_545961'>从容及鄙事，尔汝开心肝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_545961'>我是耕田夫，偶然此为官。<div id='poem_sentence_10_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_545961'>饱不知稼穑，愧汝催租瘢。<div id='poem_sentence_11_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_545961'>愿言各努力，长年好相看。<div id='poem_sentence_12_545961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_545961'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_545961_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年6月</a>　官知潭州。与张栻访卜居长沙城东之陈仲思，有诗。作品：陈仲思以太夫人高年奉祠便养卜居城东茅屋数间澹如也移花种竹山林丘壑之胜湘州所无食不足而乐有余谓古之隐君子若仲思者非耶乾道戊子六月某同张钦夫过焉裴回弥日既莫而忘去钦夫欲专壑买邻钦夫有诗某次韵。赠陈监庙。<div id='poem_545962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈仲思以太夫人高年奉祠便养卜居城东茅屋数间澹如也移花种竹山林丘壑之胜湘州所无食不足而乐有馀谓古之隐君子若仲思者非耶乾道戊子六月某同张钦夫过焉裴回弥日既莫而忘去钦夫欲专壑买邻钦夫有诗某次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545962")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545962'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545962'>平生交游中，此士故耐久。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545962'>不折为米腰，颇袖斲轮手。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545962'>卜居并东郭，草草宫一亩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545962'>日课种树书，笺题遍窗牖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545962'>花草当姬妾，松竹是朋友。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545962'>上堂娱偏亲，家饭随野蔌。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545962'>客至即举诗，兴来亦沽酒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545962'>清溪绕屋角，高木老未朽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545962'>翻翻荷见背，戢戢鱼骈首。<div id='poem_sentence_8_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_545962'>幽观天所藏，胜践我独后。<div id='poem_sentence_9_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_545962'>不因南轩君，兹游几时有。<div id='poem_sentence_10_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_545962'>为君便买邻，溪南好冈阜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_545962'>我喜君亦狂，呼儿挈尊卣。<div id='poem_sentence_12_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_545962'>一洒尘埃胸，快若苗去莠。<div id='poem_sentence_13_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_545962'>夜凉佳月出，人影散箕斗。<div id='poem_sentence_14_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_545962'>恨我当先归，君能小留否。<div id='poem_sentence_15_545962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_545962'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_545962_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_545963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545963' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545963?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠陈监庙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545963")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545963'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545963'>陈子居城东，茆屋三四间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545963'>下有五亩园，灌畦泐清湾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545963'>松柏充羽葆，荷芰作髻鬟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545963'>再拜太夫人，寿比衡麓悭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545963'>我早与子游，期子到孔颜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545963'>察子意甚真，不与时辈班。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545963'>扁舟漾荆渚，馀子颇谤讪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545963'>大道甚坦夷，勿叹行路难。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545963'>彼自种荆棘，吾宁剪榛菅。<div id='poem_sentence_8_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_545963'>一醉乘秋风，共此霜月弯。<div id='poem_sentence_9_545963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_545963'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_545963_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　官知潭州。断配术士皇甫世通。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年7月</a>　在潭州。复敷文阁待制，徙知荆南、荆湖北路安抚使。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湘阴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='db40d3cf95d6405a989a14c360bd20bb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("db40d3cf95d6405a989a14c360bd20bb");'><span id='db40d3cf95d6405a989a14c360bd20bb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>，35岁</div><div id='db40d3cf95d6405a989a14c360bd20bb' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，行经湘阴，有词抒怀。作品：蝶恋花（漠漠飞来双属玉）<div id='poem_111692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111692' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111692?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蝶恋花<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>行湘阴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111692")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111692_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111692'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111692'>漠漠飞来双<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_111692", 111692, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>属玉</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111692'>一片秋光，染就潇湘绿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111692'>雪转寒芦花簌簌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111692'>晚风细起波纹縠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111692_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111692'>落日孤云归意促。<div id='poem_sentence_4_111692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_111692'>小倚蓬窗，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_111692", 111692, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>写作</span>思家曲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_111692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_111692'>过尽碧湾三十六。<div id='poem_sentence_6_111692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_111692'>扁舟只在滩头宿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_111692_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>于湘阴送别诗僧万致一。作品：过湘中得诗僧万致一于书无所不读非苟得诗名于僧中者余欲与俱还吴中而万家浯溪将结草庵其上送余至湘阴复归作四十字以别。<div id='poem_546088' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546088' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546088?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过湘中得诗僧万致一于书无所不读非苟得诗名于僧中者余欲与俱还吴中而万家浯溪将结草庵其上送余至湘阴复归作四十字以别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546088")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546088_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546088'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546088'>别去太匆匆，回船梦泽东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546088'>拟寻行脚路，忽遇打头风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546088'>梵网威仪在，天花结习空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546088'>它年三百首，吾为子流通。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546088'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546088_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
岳阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4830c1266f7a4d70b85bfd71836d2cb5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4830c1266f7a4d70b85bfd71836d2cb5");'><span id='4830c1266f7a4d70b85bfd71836d2cb5_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>八月中旬，过洞庭湖，有词抒怀。作品：念奴娇（洞庭青草）念奴娇（星沙初下）<div id='poem_111569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111569'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111569'>洞庭青草，近中秋，更无一点风色。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111569'>玉鉴琼田三万顷，著我扁舟一叶。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111569'>素月分辉，明河共影，表里俱澄澈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111569'>悠然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_111569", 111569, id='poem_sentence_2_111563'>平楚南来，大江东去，处处风波恶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111563'><span class='link' target='_blank'>祭金沙堆庙辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271743")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271743_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271743'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271743'>憺九秋之半兮，绝洞庭予将归，登磊石以遐瞩兮，天水莽而相围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271743_comment'></div>鲸波浩其呼汹兮，蛟鳄择食以自肥，盲风凭怒无时期兮，横中流吾焉依？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271743_comment'></div>舟人谂余以湖君之神灵兮，曰甚仁而又威，若蓍龟之可信兮，盍洁齐而致祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271743_comment'></div>嗟余祷之既久兮，岂夫神今日之我违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271743_comment'></div>晨光杲其东升兮，破积雾之霏微，凝秋霁之万顷兮，樯乌转而北飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271743_comment'></div>棹夫集合以奏功兮，若驷马熟路而騑騑，寄千里于一瞬息兮，才举手而一挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271743_comment'></div>如灵宫以午泊兮，目眩积沙之辉，随涛波以上下兮，岌金城之巍巍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271743_comment'></div>信真仙之攸宅兮，羌见闻之所稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271743_comment'></div>粉墙行树缭以直兮，铺首鸣其朱扉，俨帝服之中居兮，亦班宠于厥妃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271743_comment'></div>来牲酒之杂遝兮，纷满堂之芳菲，怀沙大夫之侑食兮，噫孰知其是非！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271743_comment'></div>鸟喙鱼服，沙鲿鰋鲤，睢盱以列侍兮，骇怪谲之裳衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271743_comment'></div>盖专制楚之七泽兮，实参握乎天威者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271743_comment'></div>由余役之既久兮，阙水菽于庭闱，瞻白云以延望兮，朝隮至乎夕晖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271743_comment'></div>苟利涉以遄达兮，岂妄福之敢希？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271743_comment'></div>感神贶余以独厚兮，铭肺膺而三欷，跪陈辞而侑觞兮，聊彷佛其音徽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1271743_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>八月中旬，过洞庭湖，谒金沙堆庙，祭屈原，感之赋诗。作品：金沙堆庙有曰忠洁侯者屈大夫也感之赋诗。<div id='poem_545926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545926' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金沙堆庙有曰忠洁侯者屈大夫也感之赋诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545926")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545926_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545926'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545926'>伍君为涛头，妒妇名河津。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545926'>那知屈大夫，亦作主水神。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545926'>我识大夫公，自托腑肺亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545926'>独醒梗群昏，聚臭丑一薰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545926'>沥血摧心肝，怀襄如不闻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545926'>已矣无柰何，质之云中君。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545926'>天门开九重，帝曰哀汝勤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545926'>狭世非汝留，赐汝班列真。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545926'>司命驰先驱，太一诹吉辰。<div id='poem_sentence_8_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_545926'>翩然乘回风，脱迹此水滨。<div id='poem_sentence_9_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_545926'>朱宫紫具阙，冠佩俨以珍。<div id='poem_sentence_10_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_545926'>宓妃与娥女，修洁充下陈。<div id='poem_sentence_11_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_545926'>至今几千年，玉颜凛如新。<div id='poem_sentence_12_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_545926'>楚人殊不知，谓公果沉沦。<div id='poem_sentence_13_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_545926'>年年作端午，儿戏公应嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_14_545926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_545926'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_545926_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>八月中旬，过洞庭湖，于金沙堆观月，有文纪之。作品：观月记。<div id='poem_1272040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272040?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观月记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272040")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272040'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272040'>月极明于中秋，观中秋之月，临水胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272040_comment'></div>临水之观，宜独往；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272040_comment'></div>独往之地，去人远者又胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272040_comment'></div>然中秋多无月，城郭宫室，安得皆临水？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272040_comment'></div>盖有之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272040_comment'></div>若夫远去人迹，则必空旷幽绝之地，诚有好奇之士，亦安能独行以夜而之空旷幽绝，蕲顷刻之玩也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272040_comment'></div>今余之游金沙堆，其具是四美者与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272040_comment'></div>盖余以八月之望过洞庭，天无纤云，月白如昼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272040_comment'></div>沙当洞庭青草之中，其高十仞，四环之水，近者犹数百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272040_comment'></div>余系舡其下，尽却童隶而登焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272040_comment'></div>沙之色正黄，与月相夺，水如玉盘，沙如金积，光采激射，体寒目眩，阆风、瑶台、广寒之宫，虽未尝身至其地，当亦如是而止耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272040_comment'></div>盖中秋之月，临水之观，独往而远人，于是为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272040_comment'></div>书以为《金沙堆观月记》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1272040_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2b22156928604a67ad34e3a8693a0c55_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　赴荆州任，途经洞庭，有词。作品：浣溪沙（行尽潇湘到洞庭）<div id='poem_111623' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111623' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_111623'>楚天阔处数峰青。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111623'>旗梢不动晚波平。<div -----title
黄冈（黄州）

id='poem_sentence_0_546093'>平生闻赤壁，今日到黄州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546093_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546093'>古戍参差月，空江浩荡秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_546093_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过黄州，游东坡，有诗抒怀。<div id='poem_546094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546094' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546094")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546094_comment'></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_546094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546094'>老仙骑鹤去，稚子饭牛歌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111526?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>汪德邵无尽藏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111526")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111526_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111526'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111526'>淮楚襟带地，云梦泽南州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111526_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111526'>沧江翠壁佳处，突兀起红楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111526_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111526'>凭仗使君胸次，与问老仙何在，长啸俯清秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111526_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111526'>试遣吹箫看，骑鹤恐来游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111526_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111526'>欲乘风，凌万顷，泛扁舟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_111526_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_111526_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_111526'>此意无尽藏，分付水东流。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_111526_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='17a739aaf1a9445097464404159f5d68_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("17a739aaf1a9445097464404159f5d68");'><span id='17a739aaf1a9445097464404159f5d68_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，38岁</div><div id='17a739aaf1a9445097464404159f5d68' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年4月</a>　四月上旬，至黄州，会知州杨由义，为作《黄州开澳记》<div id='poem_1272045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄州开澳记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272045")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272045'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272045'>守杨宜之至黄三月，问诸父老，曰：「黄之所以未复其故者，以古澳之未浚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272045_comment'></div>黄为州，临江背山，沙岸壁立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272045_comment'></div>客艘上下，无所于泊，幸而毕关征，则弃去如脱兔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272045_comment'></div>四方之物至黄者，不复贸易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272045_comment'></div>黄之民，惟其土之毛，昼合于市，无所售，则闷然以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272045_comment'></div>夫然者，以四方之来者不留故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272045_comment'></div>今诚还澳之旧，使顺流而下、溯江而上者，不于黄有风涛之厄，稍为旦暮计，黄之为黄，庶乎可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272045_comment'></div>宜之惕然，不皇顾其帑廪之有无，即日鸠工，惟父老之言为信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272045_comment'></div>亲率畚锸，于以用民，而民无怨，阅廿日而开澳之工毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272045_comment'></div>始澳有上源，乘夏潦之淫，沙水俱至，水去沙积，日浚治之，亦填淤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272045_comment'></div>宜之谓澳者所以藏舟，绝一源则下澳长无湮塞之患，盖前之议者未及讲也，乃罢开上澳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272045_comment'></div>余来适丁其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272045_comment'></div>且宜之之言方公务德则启其端，余视方公为丈人行，故乐记所以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272045_comment'></div>乾道五年四月八日，张某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1272045_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　至黄州，会友人谈献可，为作《史警序》作品：史警序。望江南（谈子醉）<div id='poem_1272000' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272000' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272000?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史警序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272000")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272000'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272000'>余自荆州得请还湖阴，未至黄州二十里，扁舟溯浪来迎者，故人谈献可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272000_comment'></div>握手问无恙，命酒相劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272000_comment'></div>略赤壁，泊黄冈，望武昌西山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272000_comment'></div>余叹曰：「壮哉周公瑾之为丈夫也，一举而三国之势定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272000_comment'></div>使老瞒屏息帖耳，不敢睥睨吴、蜀者终其身」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272000_comment'></div>献可曰：「是则然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272000_comment'></div>孰知三国之势定而天下之人不复知有汉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272000_comment'></div>公瑾、孔明外托大义，实自为计，确乎以刘氏为心者谁与」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272000_comment'></div>余惕然正色，不敢复议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272000_comment'></div>献可又出所作《史警》十馀篇相示，纯正剀切，得古人论议所未到，余三复击节之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272000_comment'></div>同舟至蕲阳而别，因书以冠诸篇首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272000_comment'></div>献可蕲水人，献可名也，字亦云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272000_comment'></div>乾道己丑四月既望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1272000_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_111636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111636?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忆江南<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>赠谈献可</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111636")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111636'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111636'>谈子醉，独立睨东风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111636'>未试玉堂挥翰手，只今<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_111636", 111636, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>楚泽</span>钓鱼翁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111636'>万事举杯空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111636_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111636'>谋一笑，一笑与君同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111636'>身老南山看射虎，眼高四海送飞鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_4_111636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_111636'>赤岸晚潮通。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_111636_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
蕲春

id='poem_sentence_1_111612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111612'>水光山色翠相浮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111612_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111612'>我欲吹箫明月下，略须停棹晚风头。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111612'>从前五度到蕲州。</div><div 武汉
-----detail
