-----title
江陵（江陵府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1b261428598f4cc989ffb60553cc48f3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1b261428598f4cc989ffb60553cc48f3");'><span id='1b261428598f4cc989ffb60553cc48f3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1169')">1168-1169年</a>，37-38岁</div><div id='1b261428598f4cc989ffb60553cc48f3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年8月</a>　八月初，到达荆州任上，与前任方滋交接。作品：荆南宴交代方阁学。<span class='inlineComment2'>（江陵府，建炎四年（1130）改为荆南府，淳熙中复曰江陵府（1174-1190））</span><div id='poem_1272157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆南宴交代方阁学</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272157")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272157'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272157'>高牙大纛，来威江、汉之滨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272157_comment'></div>闲馆珍台，去蹑星辰之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272157_comment'></div>叠两世无穷之契，侈一时创见之荣，符节亲传，尊罍夙设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272157_comment'></div>伏惟某官学该今古，名满华夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272157_comment'></div>元老克壮其猷，既宣竭四方之力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272157_comment'></div>廷臣无出其右，盍登延三事之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272157_comment'></div>上永怀夜半之询，公雅动秋风之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272157_comment'></div>绿章封事，重违勇退之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272157_comment'></div>黄纸除书，即是催归之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272157_comment'></div>细数授衣之月，预占拜衮之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272157_comment'></div>某官敢谓交承，寔均子姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272157_comment'></div>九门置钥，已惭糠秕之前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272157_comment'></div>五岭建旄，未觉规模之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272157_comment'></div>亶如今日，复接后尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272157_comment'></div>万旅连营，肃中严之鼓吹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272157_comment'></div>十眉环坐，纷合奏之笙歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272157_comment'></div>期尉父老之情，敢奉俳谐之语：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1272157'>盖世英名五十年，功名久合冠台躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272157_comment'></div>只从紫塞传归诏，便上黄扉领化甄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272157_comment'></div>事契两家应更好，节旄三镇适相传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272157_comment'></div>荆江便作松江看，小驻秋风下水舡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1272157_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　官知荆南。修边备，筑寸金堤，置万盈仓。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年8月</a>　官知荆南。为邕州守蒋允济作墓志铭。作品：邕帅蒋公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1272066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邕帅蒋公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272066")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272066'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272066'>乾道元年，余守桂林，初识浔州守蒋君德施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272066_comment'></div>是岁君趋朝，执政三人者共称君之贤，赐对，擢守邕管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272066_comment'></div>其明年，余免归江东，君与邦人送余于兴安，置酒击鲜乳洞之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272066_comment'></div>时方六月，洞中极寒，水如冰雪，余与君褰裳脱履，篝火入之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272066_comment'></div>凌兢石间，题名赋诗，火尽乃出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272066_comment'></div>于是君六十有二矣，精神矍铄未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272066_comment'></div>又明年，余帅长沙，桂州旧僚以书来，则云君至邕管死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272066_comment'></div>夫以君之岂弟慈祥，忠信孝友，而位与年才止于此，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272066_comment'></div>桂州在二广号称士乡，其间固多贤，然余之所与游者，若君与石君惠叔，其尤贤者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272066_comment'></div>君之没，惠叔盖亦前数月死，故余甚悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272066_comment'></div>明年八月，余帅荆州，君之子砺自桂徒行数千里，持惠叔之弟安持状君行事求铭于予，予方谢府事未间，砺至刺血为书以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272066_comment'></div>夫以余悲君之心而砺之诚孝如此，则乌可以不铭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272066_comment'></div>君讳允济，为桂之兴安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272066_comment'></div>父熙，以君赠奉直大夫，其葬也，得致堂先生胡公为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272066_comment'></div>致堂道学高一世，语不妄发，奉直之铭可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272066_comment'></div>奉直力贫教二子，君与其兄允升，俱中绍兴二年进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1272066_comment'></div>历柳州柳城尉、容州普宁令，改秩知邵州新化县，贺州富川县，新州教授，通判宾州，知浔州、邕州，于是朝廷方知君，而上亦且试君于邕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1272066_comment'></div>将用君矣，而君遂死，积官朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1272066_comment'></div>君在州县凡四十年，一以恩信结民，务安便之，其出入期会，皆与民先为要约，无一切迫促之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1272066_comment'></div>岭南取民无艺，贫不堪，则黠且强者往往群为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1272066_comment'></div>君所至常平其赋，又设方略，盗畏之，多去易业，间发捕必得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1272066_comment'></div>新化号难治，奸民猾吏与寓客之有力者，根株囊橐，令不得一摇手，即以危法中之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1272066_comment'></div>君至属尔，俗为之变，积岁不输之租，车牛系道，库廪皆溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1272066_comment'></div>会丁太夫人忧，租未至县者，知君去，复以归，相率数百人遮部使者，愿夺君丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1272066_comment'></div>在富川，适行经界，鄙远不素习，旁郡惊扰，有死者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1272066_comment'></div>君亲为指画，条疏节披，吏受其成而民听之，从容讫事，部使者取其法下诸郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1272066_comment'></div>尝摄昭州，始官出钱二百予民，输布一匹，既复折布为钱，十倍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1272066_comment'></div>君疏以闻，竟减其半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1272066_comment'></div>隆兴诏书第良二千石，君在浔州，为广西第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1272066_comment'></div>尝按平南巡检祝尚贤，夺一官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1272066_comment'></div>及君丧过浔，尚贤哭舟中哀甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1272066_comment'></div>或问之，曰：「曩我实犯法，非公之私，公贤者，我安得不哭」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1272066_comment'></div>邕州控蛮獠，岁买国马，百货所聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1272066_comment'></div>君至，尽蠲异时武臣敝事，马大入，诸蛮怗服，至不敢相雠杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1272066_comment'></div>死之日，哭者罢市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1272066_comment'></div>君娶于秦氏，生四子：砥、硕早卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1272066_comment'></div>次砺，以君任将仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1272066_comment'></div>次确。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1272066_comment'></div>又娶王氏，有女春娘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1272066_comment'></div>君之孙男女凡六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1272066_comment'></div>君葬以乾道四年八月丙申，在兴安县之赵村巨木塘，二夫人祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1272066_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1272066'>居也孝友，仕也循良，外甚和愉，中乃峻刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1272066_comment'></div>惜乎生于南方，仕于南方，天子方将用之于既老，而君则啬于数而云亡也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1272066_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　官知荆南。秋冬时节，有词贺弟张孝直（平国）生日。作品：鹊桥仙（湘江东畔）<div id='poem_111682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹊桥仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>平国弟生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111682")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111682'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111682'>湘江东畔，去年今日，堂上簪缨罗绮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111682'>弟兄同拜寿尊前，共一笑、欢欢喜喜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111682_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111682'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_111682", 111682, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>渚宫</span>风月，边城鼓角，更好亲庭一醉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111682'>醉时重唱去年词，愿来岁、强如今岁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_111682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　官知荆南。冬日，与马纯（子约）登荆州城楼，作词咏怀。作品：浣溪沙（霜日明霄水蘸空）<div id='poem_111615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/111615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浣溪沙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二十四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111615")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111615_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111615'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111615'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_111615", 111615, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>霜日</span>明霄水蘸空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111615'>鸣鞘声里绣旗红。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111615'>澹烟衰草有无中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111615_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111615'>万里中原烽火北，一尊<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_111615", 111615, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>浊酒</span>戍楼东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_111615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_111615'>酒阑挥泪向<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_111615", 111615, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>悲风</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_111615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_111615'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(111615)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　官知荆南。汤衡从游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　官知荆南。正、二月间，游荆州天庆观，得唐明皇所注道德经残碑。作品：跋道德经碑。<div id='poem_1272002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋道德经碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272002")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272002'>荆州开元观直牙城西五百步，有南极注生铁像，祥符八年更为天庆观，绍兴五年，迁观楚镇门之东，旧观废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272002_comment'></div>乾道五年春，某与客过焉，像在坏垣中，覆以竹屋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272002_comment'></div>屋后积草，草中小碑高三尺，即《初建天庆观记》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272002_comment'></div>去草，见碑趺隐隐有字，洗刮久之，可读，盖唐明皇所注《道德经》，是时诏天下道观皆立经幢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272002_comment'></div>因火中折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272002_comment'></div>天庆之役，官吏督促，妄道士不暇它求石，即取折幢穴其腹植碑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272002_comment'></div>经文行草，注楷法，行间茂密，唐经生固多善书，然此或非经生所能办也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272002_comment'></div>既还碑天庆，发地出趺，合八方，得三千馀字，剥缺断续，益奇古，百夫辇致文公堂下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272002_comment'></div>历阳张某识。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1272002_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　官知荆南。将道德经残碑拓本送朱熹，并有书致之。作品：朱编修（某近因至城西）<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品《朱编修》（尺牍），名称依徐鹏校点《于湖居士文集》（上海古籍版）卷四十。）</span><div id='poem_1271968' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271968' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上朱编修</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271968")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271968_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271968'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271968'>某敬服名义，愿识面之日甚久，非敢为世俗不情语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271968_comment'></div>得刘丈书，又见与钦夫书，知且为衡岳之游，傥遂获奉从容，何喜如之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271968_comment'></div>不胜朝夕之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1271968'>某昨日方从钦夫约，遣人迓行李，奉告，乃承已至近境，欣慰可量！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫必授馆，不然当于我乎馆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271968_comment'></div>使令辈遣前，恐远来者须更休耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271968_comment'></div>应有委，乞示下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1271968'>风雨留人，尊候复何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271968_comment'></div>《登台》诗彊勉不工，《出师表》同上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271968_comment'></div>老兄游山，亦须待稍晴，未可以遽，千金之躯，宜自爱惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271968_comment'></div>洪涛际天，溺马杀人，将安之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1271968'>某平生慕用，岂谓来湘中乃获解后接款，慰幸可胜言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271968_comment'></div>怀亲遽归，苛留不得，至今慊然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271968_comment'></div>人还，一再奉赐书，感服感服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271968_comment'></div>某老者深动东归之兴，比已专介请祠，力致恳诸公，傥遂得之，不旬月去此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271968_comment'></div>枢庭编摩，望虽高，然非所以处元晦也，意者姑借此为掀擢之渐耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271968_comment'></div>此间诸事，钦夫诸友书中必能详言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271968_comment'></div>政远披承，千万珍护，即登严近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1271968'>《敬简堂记》遂烦挥翰，真可以托不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271968_comment'></div>但堂中之人，于敬简工夫殊未进，须士友不我遐弃，时时训厉之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫间相从，未尝不矫首奉思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271968_comment'></div>黄君内艰，可念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271968_comment'></div>仲隆想已趋朝，更不作书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271968_comment'></div>怀英行已踰月，临行疡作于背，甚可念，幸而即愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271968_comment'></div>渠自去岁得渴疾，此不可再也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1271968'>某别去再见新岁，怀乡道义不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271968_comment'></div>自来荆州，老者病甚思归，舟楫往来江上，不复定处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1271968_comment'></div>仆亦心志忽忽，百事尽废，虽如元晦，一书亦不暇遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1271968_comment'></div>乃两奉诲教，相予之意益勤，内省愧惕，不但不答书可以为罪，盖敬简之功不进，它日无以见吾元晦耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1271968_comment'></div>某自到官即请去，凡六七，最后乞致仕，乞寻医，且欲不俟报弃官而归，诸公乃亦相察，今复得祠禄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1271968_comment'></div>近制不必俟代者，已治舟楫，载衣囊，五七日便可离此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1271968_comment'></div>刘丈之去，奇哉伟哉，此行至江上，当迂数程见之，亦约钦夫，又不知肯来否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫却数通书，定叟将有远役，兄弟不能相舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1271968_comment'></div>张仲隆前后五劄议论过人，皆某所不能言者，叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1271968_comment'></div>元晦阙期已及，闻未有幡然之意，如何如何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1271968_comment'></div>某有田在谢家青山下，屋十馀间，下俯江流，今归真不复出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1271968_comment'></div>元晦异时或欲览江、淮山川之胜，乘兴东游，则仆可以奉从容于梁山、博望、慈湖、采石之间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1271968_comment'></div>此外惟为斯文珍重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1271968'>某近因至城西，于土中得一碑趺，细视之，良有刻画，盖明皇所注《道德经》幢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1271968_comment'></div>磨治之馀，仅可识，即以十夫掘取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1271968_comment'></div>其半在土中者甚完，字画非经生所能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1271968_comment'></div>已舁置府中，今装褫一本去，钦夫极爱之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1271968_comment'></div>经磨治处中有大穴，盖以载他碑者，尤古，类汉碑，并遣上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1271968_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　官知荆南。有诗赠卢司法（江陵法曹）作品：赠卢司法。<span class='inlineComment2'>（交游者卢司法名不详。）</span><div id='poem_545987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_545987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/545987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠卢司法</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_545987")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_545987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_545987'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545987'>逃秦卢博士，读书不读律。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545987'>江陵法曹掾，移病满百日。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545987'>燕坐供佛香，青灯照绳床。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545987'>肺热今无恙<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一本作今好否）</span>，门前春草长<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《于湖居士文集》卷五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545987'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_545987_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　官知荆南。送荆州进士入都，有诗。作品：诗送荆州进士入都。<div id='poem_546100' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546100?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诗送荆州进士入都</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546100")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546100'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546100'>人才收楚产，宾荐谨周官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546100'>就日三吴近，披风七泽宽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546100'>解包珍贡入，瑑玉宝光寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546100'>簇仗春旗里，看君策治安。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546100'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546100_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　官知荆南。为杨冠卿（梦锡）《客亭类稿》题跋。作品：题杨梦锡客亭类稿后。<div id='poem_1272009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272009' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272009?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题杨梦锡客亭类稿后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272009")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272009_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272009'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272009'>为文有活法，拘泥者窒之，则能今而不能古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272009_comment'></div>梦锡之文，从昔不胶于俗，纵横运转如盘中丸，未始以一律拘，要其终亦不出于盘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272009_comment'></div>盖其束发事远游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272009_comment'></div>周览天下山川之胜，以作其气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272009_comment'></div>所与交者，又皆当世知名士，文章安得不美耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272009_comment'></div>余官荆南，梦锡自交、广以《客亭类稿》来，精深雄健，视昔时又过数驿，读之终篇，使人首益俯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272009_comment'></div>历阳张某安国书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1272009_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　官知荆南。与张栻等长沙诸友有书信诗文来往。作品：有怀长沙知识呈钦夫兄弟五首。<div id='poem_546259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546259?labeling=true' target='_blank'>有怀长沙知识呈钦夫兄弟<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546259")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_546259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546259'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546259'>顺宁去覆郎官锦，府谷仍监太府钱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546259'>唯有吾宗老兄弟，闭门依旧绝韦编。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546259'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_546259_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546260?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_546260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546260'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546260'>春风花柳又芳妍，更接髯郎水竹园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546260'>小阁横桥俱胜绝，只应欠我共开尊<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集本卷下作筵）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546260'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_546260_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546261' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546261' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546261?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_546261_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546261'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546261'>召公分陕是东邻，天远堂中好主人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546261'>更喜新来黄太史，剩拚佳句了新春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546261'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_546261_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546262' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546262' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546262?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_546262_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546262'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546262'>髯郎高卧元无恙，何日湘滨具一舟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546262'>肯约春风同过我，为公酾酒炙肥牛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546262'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_546262_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_546263' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546263' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546263?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_546263_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546263'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546263'>洛阳家世邢郎子，间止逍遥自在身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546263'>病肺秋来定苏眚，可能乘兴到沙津。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546263'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_546263_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　官知荆南。荐洛阳郭雍于朝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月</a>　官知荆南。三月旦，万盈仓建成，作文以纪。作品：荆南重建万盈仓记。<div id='poem_1272044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆南重建万盈仓记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272044")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272044_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272044'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272044'>按《荆州图经》，府仓在牙城西街北，今之仓者，乃在牙城之南街西，其迁废岁月，不可得而考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272044_comment'></div>初，荆州平时，米、麦、麻、豆岁输于府者合十四万有奇，今财七之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272044_comment'></div>以其少也，故廪庾出纳，在官者不复甚经意，因陋就简，以至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272044_comment'></div>十年来，荆州屯兵，诸道之饟者受给无所，于是因仓之馀地，续续为屋，横邪曲直，随地之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272044_comment'></div>如积薪，如布算，或高或庳，上雨旁风，至栋桷委地，而犹藏谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272044_comment'></div>军士月给皆黑腐，以饲鸡豚，且不食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272044_comment'></div>余至官三月，既筑溃堤，间与僚吏周视官寺，盖无有不敝坏者，而仓为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272044_comment'></div>会朝廷赐以峡州所买之木，即檄统制官董江、节度判官赵谦、摄掌书记汪琳，撤旧屋而新之，合为屋一百五十盈，揭之曰万盈仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272044_comment'></div>外峻墙垣，内谨扃钥，台门高广，听事深明，面势位置称其为大有司也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272044_comment'></div>自湖之南北，江之东西，举无与吾仓为俪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272044_comment'></div>是役也，奔走程督，又有摄潜江巡检郭撝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272044_comment'></div>凡用木九千枚，缗钱六千，米千斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272044_comment'></div>既成而余以亲疾丐祠去，前所谓官寺之当葺者，仅能毕甲仗库，若学宫、军帑，则已鸠工而未成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272044_comment'></div>乾道五年三月旦，历阳张某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1272044_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　官知荆南。金堤筑成，设醮以祭。作品：荆州修堤设醮。<div id='poem_1272094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272094' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272094?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆州修堤设醮青词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272094")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272094'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272094'>古之南郡，今者西门，控吴、蜀之咽喉，兼襄、汉之唇齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272094_comment'></div>兵戈蹂践，阅四十年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272094_comment'></div>版籍凋残，无三万户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272094_comment'></div>属故岁有防堤之失，当隆冬兴土木之工，徭役既多，流亡是惕，历三元之初日，按八景之真文，恭辟灵场，肃延霄驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272094_comment'></div>仰赞两宫之寿，俯祈一道之安，锡以丰年，保其常产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272094_comment'></div>贳馀灾于比屋，移厥咎于微臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272094_comment'></div>帝之所临，臣不敢悔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1272094_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月</a>　官知荆南。作文以纪金堤筑成。作品：金堤记。<div id='poem_1272043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1272043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1272043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金堤记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1272043")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1272043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1272043'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1272043'>蜀之水既出峡，奔放横溃，荆州为城，当水之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1272043_comment'></div>有堤起于万寿山之麓，环城西南，谓之金堤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1272043_comment'></div>岁调夫增筑，夏潦方淫，府选才吏，分护堤上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1272043_comment'></div>乾道四年，自二月雨，至于五月，水溢数丈，既坏吾堤，又齧吾城，昼夜澒洞，如叠万鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1272043_comment'></div>前尹尚书方公，极救灾之道，决下流以导水势，亲督吏士别筑堤，城中民安不摇，越两月而后水平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1272043_comment'></div>秋八月，某自长沙来，以冬十月鸠材庀工作新堤，凡役五千人，四十日而毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1272043_comment'></div>已决之堤，汇为深渊，不可复筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1272043_comment'></div>别起七泽门之址，度两阿之间，转而西之，接于旧堤，穹崇坚好，悉倍于旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1272043_comment'></div>既成，某进府之耋老，问堤之所以坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1272043_comment'></div>曰：「异时岁修堤，则太守亲临之，庳者益之，穴者塞之，岁有增而无损也，堤是以能久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1272043_comment'></div>今不然矣，二月，下县之夫集，则有职于是者率私其人以充它役，或取其佣而纵之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1272043_comment'></div>畚锸所及，并宿草与土而去之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1272043_comment'></div>视堤既平，则告毕工，于是堤日以削而卒致于溃也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1272043_comment'></div>予感其言，因书之以告来者，使知戒焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1272043_comment'></div>筑堤馀材，裒之作小亭于堤之半，取少陵「江湖深更白，松竹远微青」，扁之青白亭，而刻文于壁间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1272043_comment'></div>五年三月，张某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1272043_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月</a>　在江陵。三月，获准辞官，进显谟阁直学士致仕。寻复得祠禄，提举江州太平兴国宫。有书信致朱熹。作品：朱编修（某别去再见新岁）<span class='inlineComment2'>（宛敏灏《张孝祥年谱》（《词学》第二、三辑）云张孝祥“请祠侍亲。三月，进显谟阁直学士致仕”，未言及张孝祥“寻复得祠禄，提举江州太平兴国宫”（韩酉山《张孝祥年谱》）。另，宛谱系于此处的张孝祥作品有《踏莎行》（旋葺荒园）、《有怀》、《请说归休好》二首、《喜归作》）</span><div id='poem_1271968' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1271968' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1271968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上朱编修</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_1271968")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1271968_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1271968'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1271968'>某敬服名义，愿识面之日甚久，非敢为世俗不情语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1271968_comment'></div>得刘丈书，又见与钦夫书，知且为衡岳之游，傥遂获奉从容，何喜如之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1271968_comment'></div>不胜朝夕之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1271968'>某昨日方从钦夫约，遣人迓行李，奉告，乃承已至近境，欣慰可量！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫必授馆，不然当于我乎馆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1271968_comment'></div>使令辈遣前，恐远来者须更休耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1271968_comment'></div>应有委，乞示下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1271968'>风雨留人，尊候复何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1271968_comment'></div>《登台》诗彊勉不工，《出师表》同上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1271968_comment'></div>老兄游山，亦须待稍晴，未可以遽，千金之躯，宜自爱惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1271968_comment'></div>洪涛际天，溺马杀人，将安之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1271968'>某平生慕用，岂谓来湘中乃获解后接款，慰幸可胜言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1271968_comment'></div>怀亲遽归，苛留不得，至今慊然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1271968_comment'></div>人还，一再奉赐书，感服感服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1271968_comment'></div>某老者深动东归之兴，比已专介请祠，力致恳诸公，傥遂得之，不旬月去此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1271968_comment'></div>枢庭编摩，望虽高，然非所以处元晦也，意者姑借此为掀擢之渐耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1271968_comment'></div>此间诸事，钦夫诸友书中必能详言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1271968_comment'></div>政远披承，千万珍护，即登严近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1271968'>《敬简堂记》遂烦挥翰，真可以托不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1271968_comment'></div>但堂中之人，于敬简工夫殊未进，须士友不我遐弃，时时训厉之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫间相从，未尝不矫首奉思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1271968_comment'></div>黄君内艰，可念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1271968_comment'></div>仲隆想已趋朝，更不作书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1271968_comment'></div>怀英行已踰月，临行疡作于背，甚可念，幸而即愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1271968_comment'></div>渠自去岁得渴疾，此不可再也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1271968'>某别去再见新岁，怀乡道义不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1271968_comment'></div>自来荆州，老者病甚思归，舟楫往来江上，不复定处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1271968_comment'></div>仆亦心志忽忽，百事尽废，虽如元晦，一书亦不暇遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1271968_comment'></div>乃两奉诲教，相予之意益勤，内省愧惕，不但不答书可以为罪，盖敬简之功不进，它日无以见吾元晦耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1271968_comment'></div>某自到官即请去，凡六七，最后乞致仕，乞寻医，且欲不俟报弃官而归，诸公乃亦相察，今复得祠禄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1271968_comment'></div>近制不必俟代者，已治舟楫，载衣囊，五七日便可离此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1271968_comment'></div>刘丈之去，奇哉伟哉，此行至江上，当迂数程见之，亦约钦夫，又不知肯来否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1271968_comment'></div>钦夫却数通书，定叟将有远役，兄弟不能相舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1271968_comment'></div>张仲隆前后五劄议论过人，皆某所不能言者，叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1271968_comment'></div>元晦阙期已及，闻未有幡然之意，如何如何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1271968_comment'></div>某有田在谢家青山下，屋十馀间，下俯江流，今归真不复出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1271968_comment'></div>元晦异时或欲览江、淮山川之胜，乘兴东游，则仆可以奉从容于梁山、博望、慈湖、采石之间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1271968_comment'></div>此外惟为斯文珍重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1271968_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1271968'>某近因至城西，于土中得一碑趺，细视之，良有刻画，盖明皇所注《道德经》幢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1271968_comment'></div>磨治之馀，仅可识，即以十夫掘取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1271968_comment'></div>其半在土中者甚完，字画非经生所能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1271968_comment'></div>已舁置府中，今装褫一本去，钦夫极爱之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1271968_comment'></div>经磨治处中有大穴，盖以载他碑者，尤古，类汉碑，并遣上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1271968_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月</a>　在江陵。三月，获准辞官，进显谟阁直学士致仕。寻复得祠禄，提举江州太平兴国宫。有诗呈刘珙。作品：呈枢密刘恭父。<div id='poem_546033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_546033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/546033?labeling=true' target='_blank'>呈枢密刘恭父</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_546033")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_546033_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_546033'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_546033'>鼎席方虚望已隆，上游那得更烦公。<div id='poem_sentence_0_546033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_546033'>敢言两镇成交契，自是孤根累化工。<div id='poem_sentence_1_546033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_546033'>旧弼新开元帅府，闲官且领太平宫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_546033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_546033'>归家净洗如椽笔，准拟燕然勒骏功。<div id='poem_sentence_3_546033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_546033'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_546033_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月</a>　在江陵。三月，获准辞官，进显谟阁直学士致仕。寻复得祠禄，提举江州太平兴国宫。有诗寄南康钱守。作品：栖真寄南康钱守。<span id='poem_content_545949'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_545949'>忆昔姑苏台，实与君子别。<div id='poem_sentence_0_545949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_545949'>一别已六年，音书间何阔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_545949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_545949'>我行半天下，尘土污须发。<div id='poem_sentence_2_545949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_545949'>君亦抱艰棘，衣袂洒清血。<div id='poem_sentence_3_545949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_545949'>今日复何日，相望一山隔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_545949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_545949'>我领通玄府，乃在庐山北。<div id='poem_sentence_5_545949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_545949'>君宦山之南，兵卫森画戟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_545949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_545949'>无由接杯酒，但可共明月。<div id='poem_sentence_7_545949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_545949'>作诗付邮筒，聊复寄消息。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月</a>　将自江陵启程返乡。张栻未能亲自为孝祥送行，有《赠学士安国公归芜湖序》送达。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月</a>　三月下旬，自江陵启程东归，有词别同官。作品：遮鸪天（又向荆州住半年）<div id='poem_111715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_111715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25540, "南宋", "张孝祥", "poem_title_111715")'>张孝祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_111715_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_111715'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_111715'>又向荆州住半年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_111715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_111715'>西风催放五湖船。<div id='poem_sentence_1_111715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_111715'>来时露菊团金颗，去日池荷叠绿钱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_111715_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_111715'>斟别酒，扣离弦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_111715'>今宵拚醉花迷坐，后夜相思月满川。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_111715_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

石首
